et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and if pain is felt, just as we said for the liver abscess.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work, there is fear that the patient may die now, or a fistula may form which cannot be healed.
de la mice	From the mouse.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse as we have said in the sections on treatments, and it does not improve, then there are three types of cautery which are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of which there is one way that you should make three cauteries, or four, in a line according to the length of the mouse, following the shape of the liver cautery we mentioned before;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	And do not rush your hand with the cautery, let the patient lie on their back attentively.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	And another method of cautery is to heat the cautery with two cords, just as we have demonstrated in the case of shoulder dislocation.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	Lift the heart which is towards the armpit, where the patient's wound faces left, and let the elevation by which you lift the heart be according to its height, along the length of the body, and let the cautery be placed across the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After placing the two flaming cords so that they pierce through to the other side of the heart, then pull them tight, and thus there will be four of them.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see fit, cauterize with a three-ner cautery.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has gotten rid of the inflammation over a long time, and this is better than the other treatments mentioned above.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not useful for treating dropsy, except in the manner known as 'ascites'.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have mentioned in our divisions, and your treatment does not bring benefit, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the swelling, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back along the spine, and one towards the breast;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterizations be close to the base of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cautery open to drain pus over a long period of time, and do not cease treatment of the patient after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	And healing will come sooner, combining these two intentions with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly shall be the clevis we have previously shown.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And that for the back is an olive-shaped tool, according to what has been set out above.
de l’enfleure des piez	The swelling of the feet.
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical, and are full of yellow water, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go in too deeply, lest you puncture the yellow water, and let the cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Afterwards, make two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the little finger.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And let the long cauterizations be below the knee in front and the other behind, halfway down the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	And leave the cauterizations untouched for a long time without treatment, until it comes out.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After curing other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	By the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the distension of the belly comes from cold and moisture, such that the retaining and digesting virtues which are in the stomach and intestine are weakened, and cannot be cured by natural means;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	And you see the patient in great suffering and of strong constitution, then make a large cauterization on the stomach according to what has been discussed previously for the stomach cautery, with the circular cauterization.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And four subtle cauterizations around the navel with each cauterization being slightly smaller than the other, and two on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, perform a cautery on the wrist, one cautery on each arm, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are located at the fundament, whether there is one or more, and they are ancient, consisting of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and have been treated as we said in previous sections, but to no avail, then perform cauterization:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	On the spine of the back, where it is entirely outside the medulla oblongata and gradually tapers to a point in a triangular shape, perform one cauterization beneath the bulge two inches.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think their stomach is cooled and the meat is not cooking, and one can see swelling of the face, then perform a large cauterization on the stomach as mentioned before, another one on the liver, and yet another on the spleen with all three cauterizations being fastened together.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	And leave the open cautery for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, let the wound heal.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of fleshiness which is named 'thelul'
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you treat the anus, heat up the cautery which resembles a plane, and then place it fully ignited on top of the treated anus;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	And leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the opening of the wound, from which the blood flows out;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this once or twice, and if there is much of the anus, cauterize each part as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	After the treatments with ointments, let them heal until they are cured;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you cauterize with a large cautery on alum, it will provide greater relief.
de plaie mal curee	Of a poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When a patient cannot endure any cutting or opening, as we will explain in this place, then such an illness arises that can only be cured by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When someone has a fistula and it is filled with pus and corrupt moisture, you should treat them with great care and ensure that you know the entire extent of the abscess.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery which looks like a razor, insert it into the fistula according to the size of the tube that has entered there, and restart the cautery until those corrupt parts are burnt, one by one, or twice, or three times, depending on the amount needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And take care not to burn the nerves which are close by, or large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes into the body of the bladder and the intestine, avoid those areas and only perform the cautery on fleshy tissue, while taking care that it does not penetrate.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	Afterwards clean the wound until it is dry, and if the area has been dry for a long time and matter has been removed, then know that the wound is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the matter is not removed, know that the bone has been pierced, and it has corrupted the marrow.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And thus as one of these we say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold arises in the reins, and there is severe flatulence, and it does not resemble a woman's condition, then you must perform a cautery on the reins, one side and the other, with the clavicle cautery we mentioned earlier;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauteries in a row, which will provide greater relief.
de la vessie	On the bladder.
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then cauterize outside on the bladder, where the arm hairs begin, on the right and left side, with each cautery as long as a thumb's width.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and do this cautery outside the back, or two if you need to.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let these be the clavicle cauteries according to the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	Of the marsh.
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends come late;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they arrive, one feels great pain.
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary that one do three cauteries around the navel, as we have said for the bladder cautery, and two outside the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let these be the clavicle cauteries, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hip.
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip joint, and due to this it moves out of place, and the sign is that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	And you will find the place of the nerve origin, then you must cauterize the patient on the hip joint with a circular cautery, and make an incision in front of the joint around the bone as it turns, so that the bone is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and let the cautery be such as those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	If this type of cautery is not present, make three olive-sized cauteries, and let the cauteries be as perfect as all hearts;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat him until he is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain in the hip.
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the hip joint, caused by cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated as we have said in the previous section but is not healed, and the illness is long-standing:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then it is necessary for you to purge the patient of excessive foul-smelling humours with pills or other suitable good medicines.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After that, cauterize him.
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	And the method of cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	That is to say, by means of all burning medicines together, and by fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Cautery by fire is so according to many methods, of which some are such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	That you cauterize on the hip's box with three triangular cauteries in this form, making them deep and large, leaving space between each one equal to a thumb's width, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Sometimes one makes a cautery in the middle above the head of the hip, so there are four of them arranged like this:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish, use the circular cautery we previously mentioned for the hip's dislocation;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But do it in such a way that the circles encompass the whole hip, and all the flesh of the heart be burnt.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	This is the method used for sciatica when the pain is confined to the hip and does not extend down to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes down to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations where the patient says the pain is felt, and one cautery above the ankle, slightly more on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	let the cauterizations be made with a spatula, and burn off any excess fat around the heart;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends down to the toes or nearby, cauterize where they feel the pain with three points or four at the 'point' cautery.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, make more [cautery marks].
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if it seems that the pain is below the knee and towards the thigh, make a cauterization with either a spatula or circular tool, and be careful in all your cautery marks to not leave them so long as to burn nerves and large arteries, and cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who had a fire cautery performed on their ankle, and they let it be until the leg was completely swollen, as well as the foot, and all of the feet were pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal operation in which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, apply a fire cautery to one part and then the other, following this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men said about the cauterization of the hip: thus is its nature, make such an iron tool and let it be at the top as thick as a navel of a date fruit, or a little less, and [let] it be serrated with each tooth being as wide apart from one another by the distance equal to that of a bean.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the serrations be cut in two parts, and also like knifes, and there is one well-made iron handle.
et c’est li forme:	and this is its shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And it should be heated until it is glowing red and emitting sparks, then place it over the affected hip bone, and rotate it along its healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	et le cauterizes une fois, puis retires le cautère et laisses [la plaie] trois jours.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	ensuite fais un emplâtre de beurre, et laisse la plaie ouverte pendant longtemps ;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	après le traitement, jusqu'à ce qu'il soit guéri.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis dit que nous utilisons peu de ce cautère à cause de son aspect, et si peu l'utilisent.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	et pourtant c'est un bon cautère, quiconque peut le supporter, mais laisse là où la peau se durcit.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	Les cautères médicaux ardents sont faits avec un instrument à deux branches où descend le fil de la porte, soit en cuivre ou en fer, sur une paroi longue, et à une hauteur de deux coudées, avec entre chacun l'espace d'un pouce.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and are exposed from below and above, and they join together like this:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Then place the box of the hip on the patient lying on their healthy side, and quickly press your hand firmly onto the box of the hip;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After that, pour the two circles of warm wax, heated over one firepot, in between them and leave it there for an hour; let the patient endure the heat and burning sensation.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For they will feel stinging as if from fire.
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the stinging sensation has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip gently, leaving it like this for three days, and apply butter until what is blackened by the burning has gone.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	Et leave it three days until it decays straight away.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be the final aid after the treatment of ointments until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make him an instrument that holds tightly according to what you did on the hip equally.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is the way of the hot instrument, and I have written it in the treatise on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, equal parts of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	Where there is a small opening so that the point of a lancet can enter.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	And place over it another vessel well sealed, and put on alkali and heat it with gentle fire until there are two fingers of liquid above the powders when you have gripped it in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	And let it sit until water drips down to the lead and tin or can plumbebate, then take all that water, and pour it over heat and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then there will be much water, which is administered in many works of medicine and cauterizations of other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs another work like fire, and has other medicines that are used for cauterization such as the hip with wax, honey, and hot soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment in which a man was cured of hip pain and sciatica; he suffered greatly, and says that no other treatment was used, and that he was healed immediately after this cure was performed, and he bathed as follows: as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And it says to do so that you take fresh and dry green litharge, and grind it very well with one pound of grease, and apply it onto the hip, thigh, and leg where the pain is, then bind it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And let it sit for three hours, depending on how long it takes until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then have him enter the bath until his body is a little heated, and make him get into bed, and the pain will go away entirely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicinal cauterization unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat dung, it helps greatly;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery must be done in such a way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take woolen cloth and grease it with old oil, and place it on the hollow between the big toe and the one next to it, which is called the "fossa".
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After that, take dry goat dung and heat it until it becomes charcoal, then place it on wool and leave it until it is extinguished.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	Repeat this process again, and continue doing so without ceasing until you feel that it has reached the hip, and the pain has ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this manner of cautery is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	From the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether due to falling, being struck, excessive strain, or similar cold substances spreading through it, no type of cautery is suitable except for that which comes from an influx of cold material.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary that after the patient has been cleansed of fetid pills or other similar remedies, which are placed on their back where the pain persists, three lines should be marked with ink, and in each line V cauteries or more should be applied depending on the strength and tolerance of the patient;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and these cauteries should be made according to the method called 'point' cautery;
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see fit, apply III or IIII clavicle cauteries in the middle, according to this pattern;
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This illness often affects young children, the initial signs are narrow chests when they rise and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you find in the last vertebra of the spine, as we do in ours, a resemblance that arises on other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this one and cure it, cauterize with the clean cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery touches every part of the vertebra evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see it, cauterize around the vertebra with the cautery making two or three lines, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treat the place until it is healed according to what we have said, and take care not to apply cautery on a hump that is over a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	Of the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain is caused by moisture that spreads to each part of the body, and when pain occurs in the foot, which doctors call "podagra" specifically, and when it is due to coldness and medicine cannot treat it, it should be treated with cautery in the following manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make several cauterizations around the ankle joint, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a need to apply it to the front of the foot, perform a cautery at every point where one would make a "dot" cautery.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains extend up to the knees and other joints, which happens frequently, apply three or four cauterizations on each knee or every other part, always using the olive-shaped cautery.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need to do more, then make more incisions, but keep your hand away except for when the tip of the heart's spear is burning.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, apply the cautery as we described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pain is in the hands, make incisions around the wrist two lines long.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains no pain in the fingers, make incisions on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pain reaches the arms or shoulders, cauterize each affected part, and provide good care to the patient and administer medications.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you provide good care and cleanse the humours, he will be healed by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	From a fracture of the sacrum
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture occurs in the groin, and the testicles descend into the scrotum, if it is a recent occurrence, on the day you treat it, ensure he does not eat.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	And let him use things that loosen the belly, so that the feces may descend from his abdomen.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After this, have him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his breath until the nostrils are repaired, then pull them towards your fingers, and cauterize below the rupture onto the wrist bone, and make an incision in the form of half a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat up the following instrument for this procedure:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as they are white and cast no shadows.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Afterward, reset the balls to their place.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	And have your assistant hold his hand in place so that it does not return backward.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and work well the thighs of the patient, and place a cushion beneath him, with a strap on the thighs, and another [strap] above his hips to hold down his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery over the mark with all your strength, and hold it straight and press until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat again until you come to the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and be careful that the lip does not jump when you apply the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so the patient does not die from this, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the child's cautery marks be subtle according to their size, and for adults they should also be large according to their measure.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, treat the site of the butter cautery until the scalding is gone;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After the treatment with other ointments until it is healed, let the patient lie on their back for forty days until the wound is fully sealed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is important that their nourishment be sufficient for a long time, so that the wound does not break open when they attempt to go into rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when they wish to get up, have a well-made bandage ready for them, and wear it for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and have good rest, let him work little and guard against too much drinking or eating, and from shouting too loudly;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this treatment, he is entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will now say after this the treatment for cutting, in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of the rupture of the belly.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When worms come into other stomachs and are known to be there, and you see that they no longer grow, if you wish, apply a hot iron cautery according to its quantity, and burn one-third of the heart.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients have said that one must cauterize with a three-angled iron according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the place of insertion and make a line across the width above the rupture, then another one outside, and hold your hand in the middle throughout the whole procedure of cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether from falling or injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it must be cauterized with a cautery called "point", and the cauteries should be applied according to the length of the limb, its size, weakness, strength, location of torsion, and the severity of the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is healed from the first cautery, it is good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If that name should be repeated for another cautery on it, as this custom is such that it must change to the member which is closest, therefore you ought to perform cauterizations until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	surgery
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The month is aided sometimes by cauterization for great help, especially the disease that comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you are about to perform the cauterization, be cautious if the illness is in its early stages and if it has been treated according to what we have said regarding treatment type. If the disease does not subside or remain dormant, and you doubt that corruption could spread throughout the patient's body then apply 5 cauteries on their head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	One at the nape of the neck and another towards the forehead near the end of their hair:
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	And two on each temple, with one behind on the occipital bone.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	And leave your hand there until the cauterization reaches the bone, and until the scabs come off so that the vapors from the thick humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	And cauterize it on the wound according to what is required.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the injury is dispersed everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it clearly deteriorates, then you must cauterize it with these cauterizations we have mentioned on the head, and one cautery on the neck spine, two cauteries on the back spine, one large one on the upper back, another nearby, and two on the shoulders.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the elbows, and two on the heel tendons, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and in the hollows of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	And beware of the nerves located above your heel so as not to burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And sometimes you apply the cautery to the bone of the wrist, and another on the stomach bone, and one more above the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	Know that the more you use cautery, the more help you provide, and it benefits them.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	Understand that the patient does not feel pain from the cautery as a healthy person would because their body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be large and small depending on the limbs and joints, according to what you find in the handling of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply flour paste to the wound with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When inflammation arises in a limb and is treated with medicine, oils, and poultices but does not heal, then apply cautery to the limb according to its size.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization mark be a little inward from the tip of the heart;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes one must make a cauterization mark on the hand, foot or back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thereby removes the inflammation.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and in any case, do not intervene if you are not knowledgeable about the limbs and the paths of the nerves that move the body.
de albaras	Of erysipelas
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is cured, and medical treatments are of no use, then cauterize it with a perfect cauterization mark, according to the size of the tip of the heart, until the white spots are removed, and its colour changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then treat with flour of vetch and lentils mixed with rose oil and plantain leaves, and the blood of pigeons and larks, one part each;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And mix everything together, bind it with cloth, and apply to the wound until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of cancer with cautery.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer appears at its beginning, and you wish to stop it, cauterize it with a circular-shaped cautery, all around the circumference of the cancerous growth.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	Moreover, wise doctors say that one should apply a cautery to the middle of the cancerous wound;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	But I do not think this is good, for I fear it may become ulcerated and corrupted, which I have already seen happen a few times.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And rather it should be cauterized around the edges with the so-called 'circular' cautery, as we have previously mentioned in the section on types of cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness called "adubelati," and it delays death either due to the excessiveness of what it does or because of the patient's water when they are decrepit (meaning very old) and have little blood, or because of the weather;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you want to hasten their death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize it with many small cauteries, pricking around the area;
aprés le laisse ensi.	Afterwards, leave it be.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierce through the entire cautery, heat up the cautery with what it is made of:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	Place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cautery has pierced the heart, and let it be such that the patient feels the cautery externally so that the course of corruption is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Afterwards, treat until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The fire cure with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than the wasting away of limbs, for it eats away at the limbs just as fires consume dry branches.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this illness in a place that can bear fire cautery, then heat the cauteries, both small and large nails, according to what is appropriate for the area or the severity of the illness;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After the cauterization of all parts, make sure to remove all the corruption, leaving nothing behind; ensure that everything corrupted is extracted.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Leave it for three days, then apply to the cauterized areas a soft ointment with oil until all scalding from the fire and corruption is removed.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	Afterwards, treat it with an ointment that produces flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days no inflammation appears, it's good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	If not, restart the cauterization on whatever remains corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this inflammation has sometimes been treated with medicine instead of fire cauterization;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	However, fire cauterization is of greater help; I have already mentioned the treatment with medicine in the section on inflammation:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	boils that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times there occurs in the foot a disease that is called "claws" according to our understanding, and it is a faulty bulging thing that wounds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization for this disease has two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Cautery of fire is that you heat one cautery like a feathered pin, and it should be made of good iron with the measure to fit the nail from all sides, and have fine edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After you place the heated cautery on top of the nail, turn your hand around the nail until it reaches the bottom of the nail.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	Leave it like this for three days until it starts to discharge pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the poultice on overnight; the nail will fall out and be uprooted from its root.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wounded place with an ointment made of fat until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by force in the body, and occur often in hands or feet, then you should treat them with hot water cautery.
et est en teil maniere:	et it is in such a manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a cane of brass or iron, or a feather from an owl's wing, and place it on the nail and wart, that is to say for warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	Place the cane on it so that it touches all around, then put a drop of hot water on it, and hold your hand firmly, pressing your hand while turning it so that the edge of the cane reaches the root of the nail, and allows the hot water to penetrate deeply down to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	Let the patient endure the stinging of the hot water for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then leave it like this, and it will be uprooted with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another until you eradicate all those which are within the body, then treat them with ointments that produce flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The doctor for shaking or trembling disorders.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some shiver from cold due to nerves, or quartan fever, or other causes, you should apply four cauterizations on the spine of their back, one between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cauterization on the foot, and one over the stomach with an olive-sized cautery.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	Allow them to tremble, it will hasten recovery from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	Pustules that stink or smell foul.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes one notices breaks in the body with baths or stinking pustules which come from large corrupted substances.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	When they first appear, it is necessary to cauterize each head of the pimple.
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cautery with myrtle wood, whose tip is seized by fire, or with the root of long aristoloche, or with a lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they cauterize at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and it prevents them from growing any further, but the excess from which they come is broken down, and they are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is severed.
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	There are often great outpourings of blood from the artery that is cut open at the wound that comes to the surface, or during the incision of an abscess, or when cauterizing a limb, and in similar situations.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is quite difficult to staunch (stop the flow of blood).
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet, when this happens to someone, quickly place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and press firmly until the blood is staunched beneath your finger, with no more drops flowing out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then put the olive oil cautery to the fire, multiple small and large ones until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then take one, either large or small depending on the wound and the place where the artery is exposed, and place the cautery onto that vein while holding your finger on it, keep the cautery there until the blood stops flowing.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it sparks when you lift your finger above the wound, and the cauterization is complete, then quickly take another of the cauteries from the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing one after another until the blood is staunched.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	Beware not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and that other mischief does not befall the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And know that when blood escapes from the artery, it cannot be well staunched especially if the artery is large, unless it is by one of the four methods we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	by cautery, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by strong binding with thread, or by applying medicine which has the power to staunch blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and bind it tightly and hold it still.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	That which will bring about stanching by binding tightly with bandages or applying hot objects, or other similar things, is of no avail unless it be done promptly.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if it should happen to anyone and they have no mirror or medicine present, one must place their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it well until it is staunched over the wound and over the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move the finger, but keep it moist with cold water often so that it is very cold until the blood is frozen and thickened and staunched;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and prepare in advance all that is needed for cautery and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book on surgical procedures.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases that require fire cautery or burning medicines, and we described the operations, their causes and instruments as well as the shapes of cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	And I have set forth this chapter on the head down to the feet, and I will proceed in this same way in this chapter so that what one seeks may be more easily found.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so, as I begin this work, dear child, it is important for you to understand that in this chapter there is greater danger and fear than in the previous one about cauterization, thus requiring even greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	Where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For there are many ways in which people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	So there are those who become so fearful with their illness that they die quickly due to the confusion caused by their condition and its great severity.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And we must fear these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	Among them there is one who will give you his advice and tell you:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	But the illness is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not give in to those who come to you with this manner but put more trust in your honor than in your greed and do not act rashly but wisely regarding what you are sure of and can gain rightfully.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	Use prognostics and diagnostics for treating your patients so that their health can be restored.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you to gain a good reputation, glory, and long-lasting fame.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Tres chier fil, Our Lord give you good understanding and righteousness, and may he wish to inspire you with the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or je vous ai ordonné ce chapitre en le divisant par chapitres, selon qu'il est présenté avant celui sur les cautères, que je vous ai déjà décrit du haut de la tête jusqu'aux pieds, afin que vous trouviez plus facilement ce dont vous avez besoin.
dou chief plein d’aigue	tête pleine d'eau.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often comes to children during birth when the midwife grips the child's head too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes it happens for reasons that are unknown, as yet.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease occur in adults, but it brought death to all the children that I have witnessed.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And for this reason, it seems best to leave the work of treating such cases to others.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw that child whose shoulder was full of water, and his head swelled each day until he could no longer bear it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture had gathered beneath the bone above the shoulder-blade, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the procedure is such if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscesses are small, that you make a wide incision in the head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and let it be as long as two thumbs, so that the moisture drains;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see here the shape of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper, and the abscesses are larger, then make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see signs of the skull being open at the sutures on every side, and water spurts out when you press it with your hand inside, and this has not responded to treatment:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	So you must make three incisions within the head like this:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After the incisions are clean with gauze and powder, apply wine and oil, and leave for five days.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then unwrap it, and treat the wound with dressings and ointments, allowing the head to remain extended evenly, while providing the patient dry meat from a pig without moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	Another method of incision is to look where the swelling of the abscess appears, and its collection of pus.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	For sometimes it will be in front (of you).
aucune fois derrier;	For some times behind.
aucune fois en destre;	Never once to the right.
et aucune fois en senestre.	And never once to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut therefore at the place where the abscess appears, and treat the fluid accumulation, and open it according to your ability.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	And take care not to cut an artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	If there is bleeding of blood, the patient may die due to loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of rheumatism
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone has a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or throat, and it is an old illness that does not benefit from medical treatment, then the last resort is cauterization along with cutting the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	Therefore, when you must cut the veins, it is necessary for the patient to lean back their head.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After you rub the place with a coarse cloth until the arteries appear, then choke the patient with all your might using this cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein beats, and the bones of both are behind the ears, and they are covered with skin.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the bones of the neck, then strike both with a sharp spatula twice as thick, so that the cut reaches the bone, and it is made on the wide part of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see it, push the spatula under the artery and cover above it, cutting as deep as necessary across the wound.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	When the vein is cut open, blood spurts out continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to the touch, you must measure three finger-widths, then mark the neck and cut down to the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	And the amount of blood to be let out is six ounces, and perhaps a little more or less, depending on how much the patient can bear and the fullness of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it remains on top of the bone without a splint, remove it so that hot abscesses do not form there; then open the wound and bind it, treating with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	Of migraine.
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes with a cold and due to the moisture of tears and heat in temples and an old persistent headache and similar things, and it is medicated through various medical treatments but nothing helps, we remove the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the way of arrow extraction is as follows: have the patient grasp their own hair from their temples and feel for the artery that beats in the temple, for it shows clearly by its pulsation, except in some men who are too cold-blooded.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is recessed, let the patient grasp their own neck with some fabric and then rub the area with a rough cloth, moistening the spot with hot water until the artery becomes plainly visible.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatule of which this is the form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then pull it upward with pincers, and remove any membranes that are underneath on each side;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, turn it to the tip of the hook, then cut it from that part according to the quantity of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut off, the blood cannot flow out everywhere all at once.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	and draw out blood for six quarters, down to three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong doubled silk thread, so that blood cannot come out before the wound heals and flows continuously.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut the superfluity that is between the two ligaments at the same time, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a knife-like cautery down to the bone until the head is cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And it is a dangerous procedure if the patient has no fever and they are of hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterization helps to dry up moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	because it is of greater help for moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Where it is necessary for the extraction of arteries, one should fill the place with old cotton and put well-made bandages on top;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when one releases them, let it be cured with dry medicines that promote flesh growth and with bandages until it is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if you sense blood flowing from the artery while operating, quickly cut it off with a cauterizer, or use a mixture of vitriol and alum to stop the bleeding;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	If you don't have the aforementioned available, place your hand directly on it until the blood is frozen, and pour cold water over it until the bleeding stops, keeping it tight as required;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	What is easier and lighter in extracting the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cutting cautery into two parts, but make sure the cuts are wide to retain heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too thin, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	There should be a thumb's width between the two knives, and once you have joined both sides together, place the heated iron on top until it reaches the bone, then cut the vein into two.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and they must be separated between the two shoulder joints for it is not completely welded with this cauterization.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	Tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the eyes are flowing down from veins that are above the top of the head, and no medical treatment is beneficial, and you see the patient's face turn red, and they feel a sensation of trembling across their forehead;
