et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and if their skin is taut and moist so that the hair on the eyelids has fallen out, and the eyelids are burned and scalded by the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	The ancients called it "contusion treatment," and what you must do for the patient with this ailment is to shave the hairs from their forehead, then make three incisions on the forehead evenly spaced along its length;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	et soit l'une des fendures ainsi comme deux doit tout emmi le front en avalant aval jusqu'à neif, et les autres deux aux côtes par-dessus les poitrines, et te garde de l'incision des artères qui sont aux côtés par-dessus les poitrines;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	et éloigne ta main de la continuité des deux mâchoires, et que chaque plaie ait une profondeur de trois doigts en travers joints;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	et aies préparée une pièce d'éponge avec beaucoup de chiffons secs pour essuyer le sang, puis introduit l'écope pointue en deux parties dont voici la forme:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	de l'incision qui est sous le tempe jusqu'à la deuxième incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and scrape out all the heart that is between the two clefts to the entire surface that is above the bone, then make another similar incision from the middle one until you reach the other second [cleft], and then extract this spatoulina.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	Insert into the first slit the instrument which is called a 'cultellarium', and it is very sharp on one side, but soft and not sharp on the other side, and this is its shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	Place the sharp edge towards the flesh near the core and the soft edge towards the bone, and insert it until it reaches the middle slit.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes so that the incision is continuous until you reach what appears of the heart, and then make another similar one in the middle cleft up to the other exterior [one];
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	and then extract the blood equally, and express the place for taken blood;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	then put in each cleft a tent of old cotton, and place on it dressings moistened with wine, oil, and egg white, and ensure that no hot abscesses come to the surface;
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	On the third day, untie the bandage, and apply a large compress of warm water, then treat it with basilicum ointment mixed with rosehip oil, and other remedies used to treat wounds until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	Of eye rheum.
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone has chronic inflammation of the eyes with recurring episodes, and you notice their eyes becoming sunken and small, weakening their vision, and the eyelids burning;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	And their hair falls out, and there is pain throughout the head, and the patient sneezes frequently;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	Then you should know that these symptoms and this inflammation arise from multiple causes, and the only true remedy is as follows:
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And you should instruct the patient to lie on their back, then make a big incision in the middle of the forehead, and another from ear to ear.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	Start by making an incision from the left temple to the right temple, cutting down to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples which move to eat
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, wipe away all blood with a sponge, then dislodge between the two lips of the incision and place old cotton and linen bandages;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	then bind moistened cloths soaked in wine and oil on top, and beware of warm abscesses;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	when it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow, then treat it with drying agents that promote healing.
En teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	take two parts of wheat flour, and four parts of colophony, and make an ointment.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	And apply medicine to these wounds to generate flesh throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of the stuffing of ears
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Whatever falls into the ears is one of four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	Or grain, or beast, or mineral stone like iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	Or seed, such as beans, peas, lentils;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	Or flowing things like water and oil and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When a stone or any other object that does not fit the ear falls into it, and cannot grow in the ear, place the ear under sunlight.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, apply a few drops of violet oil or oil of cicely, then administer its extraction.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	And have them sneeze with cumin, and block their nose when the sneeze comes, and put pieces of cloth or wool around the ear.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and lift the ear above.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Many times one sneezes due to this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if there is no sneezing, they administer an extraction with subtle pincers, which are shaped like this:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If one sneezes from the pincers, it is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if not, they administer an extraction with a small subtle curved blade;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if one does not sneeze from that, they make a reed cane and insert the end of the cane into the ear hole forcefully, then plug what is around the cane with soft wax so that no air can enter alongside the cane.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	Then treat the fire severely, for often it comes back as we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	And if it does not come back in this way, take glue and cover the instrument with it as birds are caught, then put a piece of cotton around [the instrument].
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	Then press the glue onto the stone or whatever it is, and treat the fire.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it cannot be treated with all the methods we have mentioned, then hurry to open the ear rather than an abscess so that heat and spasms may come.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	The manner of the incision is such that you first bind the patient's head with a headband and draw some blood according to his strength, then make him sit between your hands and turn his ear upwards, and make a small cut in the root of the ear at the fat or tissue underneath.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and let the fissure be like a crescent moon, until you reach the stone, then remove it according to your ability, and suck swiftly towards your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat [the wound] until it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if there are grains present and they swell, administer their removal;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot come out, use the spatula very gently in this way:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	And bring about an incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not attempt this if you think the grains are moist due to ear moisture, until you have made many small incisions;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract [the grains] with fine forceps and by sucking, as we have said, so that the extraction is alleviated.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the case of water that falls into the ear, the patient should first sneeze and fill the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let them lie on that same ear where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it should jump out because of this, it is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, then take many stones according to the length of your thumb, thin and light, and warm them slightly over the fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	And place the patient's ear over an opening, with their feet apart on either side, and strike another stone upon the stone in the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	Do not stop striking stone against stone until the water comes out completely, and thus it will all come out.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	And if you see this, take a reed and insert one end into the ear, and blow on the other end with fire until the hottest part of the reed is burnt.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then repeat this process with other reeds until all the water flows out, as we have said about stones.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of a small creature, such as a flea or similar, treat it as described in the section on divisions.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	But if it is of a large body that one can feel, then prepare an extraction with pincers.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	And this is the lightest thing to remove that could be in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms lodged in the ears, when you treat it as described in the section on divisions and deal with the distilling process, and the treatment is not effective, then one must examine the ear in sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If no worms appear, then remove them with fine pincers; and if none are seen, take a thread of the same kind.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And it is narrow beneath and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And press the most subtle part of your head into the ear according to the amount of suffering felt by the patient, then suck strongly along the entire chain.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	do this often until all the worms come out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not obey and come out, then plug the chain with cotton as I have said for stones.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not crawl out as we have said, then administer the distillations that ancient doctors have proven in the treatment of worms, and you will find them in the treatise on distillations.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and then distill your oils and medicines into the ear with all these tools, of which this is the shape as you see it.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And whether it is made of silver or copper, place it narrow below into small holes, and above cover to distill.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	to compress within the distillation with an instrument made of copper for this purpose, and if you wish to take a razor and wrap around its point like cotton.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour in your oil or juice, and whatever medicine you wish from your vessels into the tube, and let the tube be in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then insert the razor with all its cotton inside, and press your hand steadily until the oil is distilled or reaches the end of the ear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and let the patient smell it inside [the ear], and be its distillation either warm from the fire or fresh as you distill into the ear.
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	And ensure it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be as effective.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of the stuffing of ears
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born without an opening in their ears.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	And the same thing happens to men due to blockage of a wound or wax inside the ear, and this blockage sometimes becomes so severe that it cannot be seen.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	And at times the obstruction appears outside of the opening, which is clearly visible.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	The one that becomes severe and cannot be seen is quickly treated in multiple ways, and for this, it is necessary to expose the patient's ear to the sun.
et regarde dedens:	And look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	If you see the operation revealed, work with all this spatulum which is its shape:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And let it be sharp and cutting in front and behind, all evenly so that it does not wound the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	If the operation is on the ear lobe or body, hold it with subtle pincers and gently cut away until all flesh is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the suppurations are complete in the ear, take a delicate, lightweight razor and warm it slightly over fire, then place it on the body of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you sense an operation causing the patient to feel itching when heard, pierce lightly and be careful not to damage the ear's nerves.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	Then place in the ear a tent according to the width of the hole, and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do this on any day when the wound is healed, or take a tent-shaped dressing and dampen it in pink water, then powder it with ground vitriol.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And if you see the ear swollen, it is necessary that you remove the dressing and apply another, dampened in a paste made from rose oil and wax, until the swelling has gone.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if there is loss of blood, immerse a sponge and cloth in cold water, place it on the ear, and employ other remedies that stop the flow of blood as described in the chapter on distillations.
de la char des papieres	of the paper flesh
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This remedy for rheumatism which comes in paper rolls for the eyes when they are moist and dry, it is necessary that you spread them with tongs and pincers, and remove the rind from its roots using a spatula.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	Then place ground vitriol on it.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if you strip off the skin, cauterize it with a subtle lenticular cautery, and afterward the cauterizer moves following the incision.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and often return, whenever something remains from their roots;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized by fire, those roots are burned away and do not return.
de la gresle	of the hail
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Often come in the eye papilla things that appear gritty in its form and hardness, and for this reason, this illness is called "glaucoma," which is an assembly of thick moisture on both sides of the papilla.
li ovraiges est telz:	The work is such:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Take care if glaucoma moves from one side to the other, which is a minor thing to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Making it thus wide, then lightly scrape each part, then take it with pincers, and cut it.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	If you cannot cut it without piercing the skin slightly, it does not greatly harm the patient.
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	And if the wound is large, join it with a suture, and treat it until it is healed.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	And if it is small, do not use force, for the ointments will restore it quickly and generate flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the hailstone descends into the ear towards the upper part, turn it over and extend the hailstone with pincers, cut it and press from one side to the other.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the paper is separated by incision, it matters not;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the cataract is couched, apply warm water to the eye, and treat the place from which matter proceeds until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	from the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a grease which gathers on the paper-like membranes above, and this happens more often in children than adults, greatly affecting their eyes, causing catarrh in the mornings, and they cannot bear to look at the sunlight because tears well up in their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	and for this they lay on their faces thereafter, and sleep with their paper-like membranes beneath their eyebrows moistened by the vapour and appearance having covered them in exinach which appears in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press down on the place with your fingers and feel the exit point between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the manner of treatment is such that the patient places his head on your lap.
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	then take a linen cloth, and prepare a tent in the form of a circle according to the quantity that extends beyond each part, then place it on top.
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	press with your hands on either side, so that the excess is gathered within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then make in the middle of the moisture with the sharp spatula a slit no wider than the wound made when opening a vein;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and cut the skin perfectly until you reach the excess;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and in various arrangements, moisture appears from the slit, like the form of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Extract it therefore with one piece of padded cloth between your two hands on the outside, and turn your hand to the right and left until it is spread out.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	And take care not to adjust it in the groove, lest you come into contact with the entire spatula up to the eye, and cause an injury.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the bone does not emerge at the beginning of the groove, slightly increase the size of the groove gently until it appears.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then extract it as we have described, then wet the cloths in warm water and place them on the site, and bind firmly.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	For such people who grind herbs and place them on to corrupt the moisture that has remained.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is healed.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to a hot abscess, treat it with soothing emollient plasters until it is healed.
des poilz des papieres	hairs of paper.
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hair grows in places other than where it is naturally intended to grow and becomes ingrown, this can be detrimental to the eyes, leading to various ailments such as habitual tearing, softening of the eyelids, and discharge, ultimately resulting in eye damage.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment is carried out according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	by means of fire cautery, or by medicinal means according to what is presented before in the chapter on cauterization, and it is done either by incision and suturing or by canes, as I will explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	Place the patient's head on your lap, then turn their left eye towards your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	if it faces inward, that is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, insert a needle with thread into it;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and let it be near the edge of the eyelid where the hairs grow or above these hairs, and pull the thread through to the other side, then turn it with the back of a razor;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	Then make an incision beneath the paper-like membrane under the hairs, cutting all of it away until the large bone (humerus) and its projection is exposed.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Remove the thread and place beneath the membrane a small tent made of cotton and linen, then suture over it an anchor-shaped figure as in myrtle leaves; however, be sure that its size fits your intended elevation of the divided membrane.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if necessary, cut away large portions of the membrane according to how softened it is.
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then make an incision across the entire humerus along both lines you have marked, starting from its large projection to its smaller end.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and be one of the incisions close to natural hairs in the thickness of a root, then insert the uncinus into one of the two corners of the heart, and then remove the skin completely;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then bring together the two lips with a seam using a needle and any fine woolen thread, wipe away the blood, and remove any excess thread on both eyebrows or any sticky substances if you wish to perform this.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if not, have no concern for it, then leave the seam and threads until three or four days have passed.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then treat the wound without a seam using drying and binding substances, for paper lifts upon the healing of the wound and its reunion, but a seam is dangerous (as the ancients said), and these are works without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	and if it is done in another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and you should bleed the skin to produce a shape that is like the leaf of myrtle, as we have described, with three ounces of salt removed according to this form:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then cut this which overcomes the small forces equally according to the form which is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you are unable to hold the forceps, and the thing is not even, then take a needle with one thread, and place it in the middle of the figure;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and place another thread near the larger lobe, and the second thread near the smaller one, and join between your two fingers the threads evenly;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift all the skin that you have bled, as we have described, then join the two lips of the wound by suturing, and treat it until it is healed;
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess forms at your incision site, soothe it with a cautery and similar soothing ointments.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and sometimes the hairs of the scrotum become twisted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	then you must use what we have said about incision.
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the suturing on both sides is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of canine bites follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	You must turn the scrotum inside out according to what I have said, and then make two incisions per side, as well as two fine threads of suture as long as the width of your little finger.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and hold both shoulders of two parts where you are holding the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then join one and the other delicately onto what is above the paper of the eye, and stretch the two chains of the two parts formed;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave it like this for a few days, and the skin that is stretched will die and blacken and rot until it falls off by itself.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it takes too long, apply force to it, then treat it until it is healed.
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and when the wound is healed, if the paper is lifted, the hairs will no longer prick.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	and this is the form of the two chains that you will make according to this figure, and with these measurements in length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The works are such that you take a fine needle, and insert into it a soft and delicate silk thread;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then join the heads (of the bones) together and knot both sides delicately, and let the length of the thread be one palm in length.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then arrange another fine silk thread inside the wound, tie the ends of the threads together tightly.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then place the patient's head on your lap.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And be by the sunlight so that the work is illuminated, for it is delicate and fine work. Then insert the needle into the wound all the way to the root of an adjacent hair, piercing through until you draw it out above a natural hair.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	then extract the hair up to the shaft, and push into the shaft that hair, whether there is 1 or 2 or 3 or more.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	then extract your hand until the hairs come out fully into the shaft in the paper with its natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the shaft is intact and the hair does not come out with it, you will treat the shaft from below along all of its length that you have instructed, until the shaft comes out through the hole above and you see it by the eye's vision;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	then treat the shaft and its length, close the eye and leave it closed for 2 or 3 days until the hair dries in its place and flesh grows over it;
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	and if the hairs are small, accompany them with a long hair from their natural growth pattern, and raise it along with the one you leave [alone], until they elongate and then remove it.
de la porriture de l’oil	From the corruption of the eye
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease, which is called "aleacrati" or the scurf arises in the eye, it occurs in two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	one naturally, and the other unnaturally.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And this occurs suddenly due to a wound, or from a cutting instrument or cauterization, and through similar procedures.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way of treating it is that you split that weld [wound?], and separate its lips, and place inside linen bandages, and bind it until it heals.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and it is not suitable that you use in its treatment things that dry out and constrict [the eye?].
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the disease will return worse than before.
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but use softening substances like fenugreek.
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and the decoction of water or other liquids with flax seeds is cooked, and ointments made from melted diazion are mixed into any oils, and a poultice is prepared; treat this condition as described above.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the secret of your treatment is that you must be cautious not to let it heal in a form different from its original shape.
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And these treatments we have mentioned are only meant to address this illness so that it does not return in its original form.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	from flesh which comes to the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease, which is dislocated and truly called "axacrati", is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	Accidents arise from wounds, fractures, cauterization, and similar procedures.
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	And the way to work on it is as follows: take a needle with doubled thread and insert it into the flesh, piercing from the left armpit to the right, so that the thread comes out through two points of the flesh.
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then stretch the flesh above the entire needle and strike it with a broad spatula.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the appearance of the flesh returns according to what is required, it is good.
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If not, take a razor and place it in the wound, turn back the flesh, and make two incisions on either side inside the flesh.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the two sides of the incision be placed at the two corners you have marked, and make these angles so that when they are assembled together the shape resembles that of the Greek letter "I";
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove that flesh according to its quantity from underneath the skin on either side of what follows the paper, then join these two parts together, and sew them with a woollen thread;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with the softening medications as we have said earlier, and dress it with bandages until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the wound comes from a split or a stitch or a burning, then you must make an incision in full underneath the skin of the flesh and according to what is described above.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then sever between the two lips of the wound, as I said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and one must perform the operation according to the form of the illness, as it is very diverse in its forms, and wise doctors devise every means within their power to restore the shape to its natural form;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and the patients themselves, according to what is required of them in terms of operation and instruments in various positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	Suddenly from paper...
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this adhesion occurs in the hands of men in such a way that the paper over it is stuck with the white part of the eye, and cannot move or perform its natural functions, then you must put the tip of a razor underneath the paper and lift it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and extend them to the pincers, so that you cut off what is hard with the subtle spatula, which should not be too sharp nor too cutting, so that the patient does not suffer from the spatula being too sharp and injuring the eye.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and let your incision, where you peel away the assembly, be light, so that the paper returns to its natural form.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and is cleansed all that assembly, and they sometimes make an eye-wash with salt water, and add fresh water, and collorium.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the paper and the eye a linen tent, and put on the eye wool moistened with egg white.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after three days, use collorium and soothing things until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	Of the nail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that a nail (or claw) is of two types:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	One is nervous and resembles hard skin, and another that is not nervous but resembles white frozen moisture, which when touched with iron and treated with pincers, one cannot do so;
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	And both of these appearances start towards the upper eyelid, and grow piece by piece until they cover all of the eye's vision, light, and movement.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of incision is that the patient should place their head in your lap, then open their eyes;
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	And lift the paper to your hand, then coil the nail with small pincers, extending it above;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and insert a horse hair, or cow hair, or oxen hair, and strong thread.
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	Double the tip of the needle slightly and insert it between the nails, piercing through with the entire needle, then tie the nail with a thread and stretch it upwards, scraping away all the hair on the side of the nail that covers the grape-like growth and the sinew up to the head; cut off what remains at the root of the armpit using a subtle spatula and small forceps, leaving the natural flesh in the armpit so that the body's fluids do not flow out through the incision as is customary.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	And sometimes stretch only the nail with the spatula, and with the thread, as we have said.
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then you must flay the entire spatamil, soft from which it is so formed:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And take care that the spatamil does not touch the fleshy membrane and tear it, nor should the marrow be pierced;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	After the incision, pour a pinch of ground silphium into the eye, and apply collar made of litharge, leaving it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with what is necessary until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not nervous and you cannot insert the needle, nor can the hooks enter it, this similar case of a nail has often been treated by physicians;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow as I have described in the division, and if you see it cut, operate on the eye of the patient, and take a light spatula with a sharp edge according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	and lift the eyelid carefully, and if you see that it doesn't reduce [the inflammation] and the reason presses you, then distil into the eye a collar made of litharge and red copper sulfate, which is finely ground, and plug up the eye until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then restart the other work according to this same operation, until it is all removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing opposes you in the eye, such as a hot abscess, then milk it, and treat first the hot abscess until it is healed, then resume the work as before, until it is healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh in the eyelid causes great harm to the eye, then suspend it with an onion, and cut away part of it but not all, so that a body of tears doesn't come out.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then drip into the eye red colloidal mercury which is made of litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows on the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Some men's eyes are born with a red scar, which covers the pupil and spreads over the whites of their eyes to the outside corners, resembling a red rose.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the procedure is that the patient places their head in your lap, you then open up their eyes and roll back all of this flesh with suitable hooks and hold it firmly.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then cut the first layer of flesh and keep on cutting with a razor until you reach the end, being careful not to damage the eye during the procedure.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And the incisions should be made with a spatula, as we have mentioned before in the chapter about nail incision and small forceps to remove them, as this chapter shows.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	and when the incision is complete and all flesh removed, apply ground linseed oil or if you wish to distill red mercury and similar corrosive medicines, place on the eye outside a cotton pad with egg white so that it is covered from an abscess of heat.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	and if nothing remains there, and warm blood rises above it, and you suspect a hot abscess, leave the eye alone and treat the abscess with soothing things for a hot abscess.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	then return to your work until it is healed, and so do likewise whenever flesh has been removed from the eye in this manner.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, you must ease the treatment of each weak eye according to natural ways.
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	And for accidental wounds, in ironwork;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	Nor should you thrust your hand into any of these works until you see that this limb is capable of bearing the treatment.
des voines des eulz	the veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Below the veins are red lines that cover the eye, obscuring its sight and weakening it daily.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	Therefore, it is necessary for you to first examine the eye, in what state it is, whether it is healthy or diseased, and that there are no other ailments beyond this.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	Then treat it as follows:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Instruct the patient to place their head in your lap, then cleanse those veins as thoroughly as you know how, and ensure that these cleansings are doubly subtle according to this method:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	Et let there be two ounces by degrees in the body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	Then cleanse those veins thoroughly with the fingers, and wipe away the blood one hour later, until you see the veins of the eye become strong again.
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And be careful not to injure the eye with the sharp edges of the spatules, and perform this procedure at noon in front of the sun, and be very diligent in your work so as not to cut anything but those veins.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, then distill into the eye green and red collyrium to corrupt what remains of the film.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you cannot gather all these things at that hour, then make a plaster over the eye with soothing substances for the pain of the eyes, and leave it there for some days until the pain is eased and the hot abscess assured, then begin again according to this method until it is healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And this is the form of treatment:
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the eye's fistula
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The doctor calls them "arissati" when they are fistulae:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you treat it with cauterization and medicine for a burning ulcer as I previously mentioned, and it is not healed, if there is pus in it that you must open over the abscess, leave where it should die, and drain all the moisture until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed, and you see the corruption and blackness, then remove all the instrument by which it was formed.
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	It is called "aspre chief," and it should be made of iron going to the head, and pointed like a file as it currently appears:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	Place it on the place of the corrupted bone, then turn it between your two fingers, and press your hand a little until you know that corruption is removed.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	And do this once or twice, then apply astringent medications to the site.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the wound has healed over and grown flesh, and the body of the vein is also healed, remaining so for forty days without reopening or becoming abscessed, and no ill accidents occur, know that it is cured.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, there remains the procedure of reopening the fistula to the sinus using this method:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	And it is that you reopen the bone a second time with an iron instrument and caustic medications, and when it is reopened take a trephine of this design, and let the tip of the bit be three-sided, tapering to a point as shown here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place it above the bone near the armpit, and move your hand away from their eye by one thumb's length, then turn the drill completely until it pierces through the bone and they feel it because the wind passes through if they hold their hand over their nose.
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	And then apply the place of dry medicines, as I have taught you, and when the scar forms and hardens the places, it goes to the nose.
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	This is a lighter thing for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	From the exit of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eye has opened fully without any obstruction or reduction of breath, you must bind the patient.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	Then clean it, then apply cups or hot iron without wounding to suck, then place on the eye a poultice made of aloes and incense and sarcocolle, then strain the eye, and apply plaster over bandages and cloths.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	and the manner of bandages is such that you take soft enough bandages, and fold each into four, then place one upon another according to the quantity that the eyes need.
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then strain it through a hard and tight bandage, and repeat the cups to suck without bruising;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the cups and keep the eye tightly closed day and night, and if the ties loosen, you must strain it greatly.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	afterwards, remove the ties after day and night, and if you see that the eye is restored, it is good.
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it starts again, apply the plaster, cloth dressings, bandages, and cups until it is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	From the rupture of a hard membrane
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When ruptures occur in the cloudy cornea, it opens up, and something hard comes out like resin grains, which is dreadful to see.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	Then if you see it cut, the work is such that you insert a needle into the root of one part below until reaching above and then insert another needle with a doubled thread from the orbital fissure.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	And pierce it, leaving the first needle according to its position.
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	Then cut the place of the doubled thread and bind part of the cornea around it tightly, then remove the needle and apply moist lint soaked in raw egg onto the eye.
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	And leave it until the son of onion grows with the egg, then treat the eye with comforting things until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And sometimes the wound is restricted by an egg on each side with a circle of cloth until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eye shows great signs of injury, pierce it with a subtle spatula that comes out through the eye and drains the white moisture and lowers the eyelid, entering immediately.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then remove it until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	of the eye's bowels
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This illness, called "alconatti", is caused by foul matter assembled in the eye, appearing like descending water but it is not water.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the manner of appearance for the operation is that you make the patient sit on an equipped and straight chair, then take their head between your hands from two sides, and move it until you see the bow coming above your eyes.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then be fixed, and do not lower or cover the light, and let the patient see things as they usually would.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not descend below, know that this is due to water retention, and if the descent of the bow is not equipped as we have said earlier.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	have the patient sit between your hands, then take a fine spatula and make an incision on the corneal tissue through a pore by following the continuity of the conjunctiva with the corneal tissue and the cornea, until the bow comes out.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and when it has been removed, drip warm water mixed with honey into the eye, or water boiled with fenugreek and honey; then treat it with another remedy until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	Watery eyes
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have seen the appearance of fluids during the procedure, and what is required to puncture it;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	so act according to good health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	You should make the patient sit between your crossed hands, away from direct sunlight for the eye to be bound very tightly.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then place the paper of the eye on your left hand if the eyes are left-sided, or on your right hand if they are right-sided.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take in your right hand, if the eye is left, the instrument called "almagda", or with your left hand, if the eye is right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the instrument near the cornea at the thickness of a hair in that whiteness of the eye towards the lower part of the tear duct, then push the instrument called "almagda" skillfully, and turn your hand until it pierces into the whiteness of the eye, and feel that almagda reaches the empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	And it is necessary that the length of almagda matches perfectly the space from the pupil to the end of the black part.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	This is the cornea of the eye.
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	If you see the bone in that paper due to the clarity of the horny membrane, then you can place the instrument up to where the water is, and express it underneath a way after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the swelling goes down now, the patient will see before them and the instrument in their eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After rest the small one, and if the water rises again through a second way, place force with the instrument, and when it is fixed in there and does not rise, then extract the alum gently by turning your hand back and forth.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	And then pour in a little sealskin, and lift out the eye from it.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then place over the eye with dry lint or wet wool in rose oil and egg white, and bind it with a healthy eye.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those of our time, put on it crushed cumin with plenty of egg white.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the almagda cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, for there are some men who have very hard eyes, then you must take the instrument called 'alberit', of which this is the shape:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	Pierce only the conjunctiva, do not go too deep, but make a subtle hole, then put in the alum, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	And upon completion of the work, prepare for the patient an upcoming pleasant bed, so that they may sleep on their back in a dark place.
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	Let them abstain from all movement, and eat light food, moving neither their head to the right nor left. Bind them according to their condition until the third day.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	Then release them in the same dark room and test their vision. Show them various objects to perceive and then rebind until the seventh day.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	You should not perform this during or immediately after the treatment but rather in anticipation of water rising quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	If an abscess develops, that you release the eye before the seventh day and address it with treatment for abscesses.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	And when it is eased, release the bandage and place on their face a small kerchief to cover for one day, then remain in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	Then remove from the house little by little, and accustom them to these conditions.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	And remember that no disciple should interfere in this matter.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And a man came to us from Iraq, who told us that in his country they make pierced alembics for distilling water, but I have never seen any such thing in our land, nor have I ever read about it in the books of the ancients.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And perhaps this is a new invention.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of the forms of almug, because whoever does not know them will see them.
et soient d’arain proprement:	and be made of pure copper.
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And the head is of the same subtle material, and the end is in three angled corners.
de la char sor le neis	from the flesh above the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Sometimes there arise joined cars diverse, from which some appear like scorpions with many feet;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	And if there be such, where it has chariot enhanced with red fox fur, and also soft chariot of good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In this soft chariot that is not enhanced, you must make the patient sit between your hands towards the sun.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	And open their nostrils, apply ointment to those chariots, and draw them forward.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	Prick with what you can hold steady at the spatule's sharp point from one side, so that you know this flesh is all removed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if anything remains which cannot be cut, open it entirely with the delicate instruments lightly, so that nothing remains there.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if it overwhelms you, with abscess cauterization, do the operation as required;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if they are malignant abscesses, hurry and cauterize so the blood is stanched and all flesh is removed; then apply warm wax or wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the wound operates and moisture comes as far as the palate, know that it is healing;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if moisture does not penetrate as it should, know that there is cartilage in the bone above, which prevents instruments from cutting.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	then you must insert into it a length of linen thread somewhat thicker than the others and tie a knot at each end leaving between them an inch or less of space.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	have the patient grasp with his hand that end of the thread which is attached to the shoulder and draw it in gently until he can smell it coming out into the mouth through the nose;
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	and this is often done to children at school, and it is an easy thing for whoever wishes to do it.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	then hold the end which comes out through the nose with one hand and that which is drawn from the mouth with the other, and draw the two ends together being careful to keep your fingers on either side of the thread.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this so that you know that the night has corrupted that flesh, then draw out the son, wipe away the blood, and dampen the thread with Egyptian ointment, and replace it back into the nose as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, so that the ointments erode all that remains of flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	And then place in the nose a leaden tube for some days until it is healed, and if there is need of drying medicines, use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	And this is the form of the instrument to purge the head, through which oils and medicines are distilled into the nose;
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And it should be made of silver or brass, resembling an open lamp, just like a tube and its handle.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you see fit, make a tight cage, and have the instruments ready to cleanse the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	hold the handle firmly against the head to keep it still when heating oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	from the flesh above the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Often a tumor is born in the head which grows large and becomes visible to the eye.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And for this, you must cut it at the beginning, removing all of it, then apply a cauterizing agent or burning medicine to the area.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	and if it is left to grow large, take note if it is hard, dark in colour and has poor sensation.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	Do not touch it with iron for this is a festering abscess as when one pierces through it once there comes great pain to the patient.
