et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	And if the abscess is soft to the touch, not of fixed colour, and you see that it can be entirely cut out, then empty the patient's bowels and cut it without fear, treating the wound with drying and constricting things.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the nose is cut and sewn
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when the operation of continuing into one of these cartilaginous works yields little benefit, except for some men.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	Therefore, when it happens to anyone, one should look to see if the wound is fresh and full of blood.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then bring together the two lips in a seam, afterwards treating it until it is healed.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	And if the lips are torn apart on both sides, one should scrape away all parts of their hearts until they bleed, then bring together the two lips in a seam, binding them tightly, and dusting it with powder made from dragon's blood and ground frankincense.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	and place a piece of strong plaster or another sealing plaster on top, and leave it until it hardens by itself, then treat it with ointment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The way of the suture is that you gather the solution:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	or with needles, as we have said in the suturing of the abdomen;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or by thread, just as I made you aware.
des apostemes des levres	Of abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	Men's hands develop inside the lips as hard abscesses, resembling warts, both smaller and larger;
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	then it is necessary that you turn the lips back, split each one open and take pincers to extract its contents in each part;
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	Then apply the place after the incision with powdered vitriol, until the blood is stanched;
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then leave it to heal easily, and treat the area with dry substances until it is healed.
de la char des gencives	On the flesh of the gums.
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Often there arises on the gums flesh that grows in an unhealthy manner, which the ancients call 'albulus';
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	You must hold it with forceps, cut it at its root, and let the bowels or blood run out;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	Then put on the area powdered vitriol or other restraining and drying powders;
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	And if that flesh grows back after the incision, which often happens, then cut it a second time and cauterize it;
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	If it does not return after the cautery;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the shapes of the instruments to cut.
des sordens	Of sores.
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Sometimes in the gum area of the mouth, hideous and rough bark-like objects form around teeth.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	And sometimes the tooth turns black or yellow-green, indicating decay has spread to the gum and causing foul odor.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	You must have the patient sit between your hands, their head in your lap, and you remove teeth or bark-like growths until nothing is left.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	And do the same for blackness, greenness, yellowness, and other stains until they are cleaned.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	et if one removes what is at the root cause, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	if not, start again on the second day and third, until you have healed everything.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and know that teeth require various types of instruments to extract them depending on the work that needs to be done because the rasp used for extracting teeth protruding from the gums has a different shape than the one used between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these shapes, and others, should be prepared for you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	When treating tooth pain, it is important to delay the extraction as long as possible because this should not be done lightly.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	For it is a very important matter until such time as one has no excuse to exclude it.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Then when the patient is forced to extract (the tooth), you must be certain of which tooth is causing pain.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain deceives the patient, and they believe it is in a healthy tooth, so they have a good tooth drawn.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	And yet the pain does not leave them for this reason, as the bad tooth remains, for we have seen it happen with these sufferers.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	And when you are certain which tooth is causing the pain, it is necessary to scrape around the tooth on all sides with a spatula, taking care not to damage the gums.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then grasp it with your fingers or with delicate pincers at the first blow and blow, until it is well loosened, then close the pincers tightly.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	And let the shoulder of the patient be on your lap between your knees, and hold it firmly so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the tooth correctly without breaking it, and if it cannot be removed, use one of these instruments and gently insert them on each side, moving it as you did initially.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the tooth is pierced and worn down, you must fill it with small pieces of cloth where the hole is.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	And extract it carefully with tongs so that it does not break when you remove it.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	And one must work very carefully around the gum with great bleeding to extract the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	Be careful not to break the tooth, leaving a part of it behind, as this will cause the patient even greater pain due to the remaining root.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And beware that you do not act like the ignorant surgeon, who in their haste and boldness sometimes breaks the jawbone, and does not attend to what we have described.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but sometimes cause great illness through their roots that remain, or the cart that they break, just as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	and when the tooth is drawn, wash the place with wine or oil and salt;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and if blood flows from it, which often happens, apply crushed vitriol to the place;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if that is of no avail, then cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The shapes of the instruments, with which one first loosens teeth, should have long points and large handles, so that they do not bend when you draw the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	and these are their forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should have thick shafts so that they do not bend when pulling, and be well-made iron with teeth to grip the tooth.
de la racine des dens	From the root of the teeth.
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains intact during extraction, you must place moist cotton with butter on it over the area for one or two days until the tissue softens, then insert the forceps known as "algefri", which resemble a stork's beak.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and they should be shaped like a file on the inside as well, which is their form:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not wish to come out with all these tongs, then you must uncover the flesh all around the root, and place the instrument which is called 'althali', that is to say, a scalpel, of which this is the form:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And let it be strong and thick so as not to break, and if the root jumps out in this manner, it is good;
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	but if not, use all available instruments, for which the shapes that follow are provided:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if one requires assistance with this instrument, which has two blades, of which the form is as follows:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other iron instruments that are positioned at the root of the teeth, and of this instrument which resembles large tongs, of which the form is as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And let these instruments be strong so they do not break, and know that there are many dental instruments;
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other instruments, which are not mentioned here;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	and wise master doctors find their own instruments themselves, according to what their practices and the disease require; for there are such diseases that ancient scholars did not teach any instrument for them due to their diversity; if a bone of the shoulder or other bones is broken, one should search for the suitable tools I mentioned to you earlier, and assist with gestures, this is how it is formed:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And they should be thick and sturdy to hold the bone firmly, so that it does not slip away but can be held and removed;
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	then restore the medicine to its place accordingly, and if there is any rotting in the bone, and it is small, then use all these instruments:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the teeth appear not according to their natural form, and they are ugly, especially in young women, you must know if the tooth is newly born after another one, and it's not in its right place, and cannot be treated or filed.
adonques lou raie;	Then remove it.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	And if it is hollow with the tooth, take this instrument which has this form, and resembles a small beak, and let it be sharp iron at its tip.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And strike it several times with a hammer during the day for its hardness, and so that you do not move other teeth, and if it is apparent that it can be filed, then file it with this kind of rasp whose shape resembles this.
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	And it is also like the file used to make needles.
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	And use the file to smooth the tooth back and forth gently so that it does not move until it is finished.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	Then the full cure for everyone who shaves; and if the tooth is too sharp and injures the tongue, you must file down its roughness until it is even so that it does not injure the tongue or corrupt speech.
quant li dent lochent	When teeth loosen
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the front teeth become loose due to impact or falling, and the patient cannot chew without them dropping out, and you have treated them with constricting medicines but it doesn't work, then...
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	In that case, you must restrain them with a gold wire, because silver wire turns green and decays, but gold never changes.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	And make sure the wire is neither too thin nor too thick, according to the space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you wish to align the teeth, take the thread and pass it double between two healthy teeth, then place the head between the damaged teeth, whether there is one or more, until you come out on the other side of a healthy tooth;
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	then restart the covering until you reach the part where you began, and carefully extract your hand skillfully and gently, so that it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and make sure your tie is at the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then cut the head of the tooth with some pincers, and put it back together, and replace it between the healthy tooth, so that it does not injure the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	and then leave it tight as much as it can stay put, and if it loosens or the thread twists, tighten it with another piece of thread.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	if it stays in place and serves like this for a long time, and that is the form of teeth and the arrangement of two healthy teeth and two moved teeth, as you can see.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth falls out, we put it back in its place, fresh to fresh, as we have said before.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and do not let anyone who is not skilled and patient interfere, and sometimes we make the form of a tooth out of cow bone, and put it in place where there is a missing tooth, and tighten it as we have said, and it stays and serves like this for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	to cut loose the tongue's bond
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Sometimes this ligament comes from under the tongue naturally, as one is born this way.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by accident from a healed wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the work is such that you open the patient's mouth, and hold their head in your hand, then lift their tongue.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then cut the nerve of the tongue, so that the tongue is separated from its attachment, and if there is hardness or knot, and it is a recent wound, then cut out the thorn and sever widely this ligament.
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and take care that the incision is not too deep, for the artery which lies beneath.
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	and when you have done this, raise the place with rosewater and oil, or cold water, then put beneath the tongue a linen cloth.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	And let the patient have baths each night so that the wounds cannot heal.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if bleeding occurs, apply crushed vitriol onto the wound.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	And if the blood flows excessively, then cauterize it with a small cautery, which is beneficial in such cases.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	Then treat it with another remedy until it heals.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	And if you see it turn a different colour, be it black or hard, and the patient does not feel it, do not touch it at all, for it is cancer.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	And if it is turning white and there is moisture present, then drain the pus, and cut it open with a thin spatula, releasing it from both sides.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	and if blood overtakes you during your procedure, apply crushed vitriol immediately until it is extinguished, then return to your procedure until everything is completed.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then clean the place with ash and silk, and treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
des apostemes de la gorge	abscesses of the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	Sometimes lumps appear in the throat which are called "godaths", and we properly call them tonsils, and when you treat them as we have mentioned earlier, if they do not heal, be careful:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	if it is an abscess with little pain and a pale colour, do not treat it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it is red and the root is swollen, do not treat it with iron due to blood flow concerns;
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	But leave it until it is dead, then you will cut it off, or it would break by itself.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it is of white color and the root is delicate, prepare the instrument for cutting, but first ensure that the abscess has cooled down and is calm.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then have the patient sit facing the sun, with their shoulder in your lap, and open their mouth while you take hold of their jaws between your hands, then press down on the tongue using all the instrument, this is how it should be positioned.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	And let it be made of silver or fine copper, just like a knife.
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	When you press down on the tongue with this instrument and see the abscess, take the needle and insert it into the almond, then pull it out forcefully from above as much as you can.
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	and draw all thread out of it with a hook, then shape the tool from this material so that it looks like tongs.
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	but nevertheless the head is curved, with one end fitting into the other, and it is very sharp, and is made of iron or steel.
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you don't have this instrument ready, then cover it with the tongs, of which this is the shape:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And be sharpened on one side, but blunt on the other.
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and once you have shaped one of the mandrels, shape the other in the same way, and after making the incision gargle the patient with warm water mixed with alum, and if there is an outflow of blood, then gargle the patient with water or with boiled pomegranate peels or myrtle leaves, and similar things until the bleeding stops.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat until it is healed;
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	And sometimes other abscesses appear in the throat besides the two tonsils, so treat them just as you would the two tonsils alike.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	I treated a woman for an abscess that had formed inside her throat, specifically a small abscess;
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	And it had almost completely blocked her throat, so that the woman could not breathe through the obstructed passage, nor could she eat or drink, and she would have died if she remained like that for even one or two days.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	The abscess was so swollen that it had burst, with two streams of pus escaping through the nostrils.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	So I immediately made an incision, and inserted a hook into one inch of the throat, then pulled out a large portion of bowels;
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	Then I reinserted it through another hole of the nose, and the worker opened his mouth and pressed on his tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	After inserting the onion into these abscesses, and cutting off a part of it, only a little bit of blood came out.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	And thus the woman's throat was unblocked, and she began to drink water, then wine, and did not stop having this abscess cut for a long time.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	And the abscess reformed again, filling up the space I had emptied until it became very large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	Then I tricked her and cauterized inside her throat.
ensi demora sens croistre;	Thus it remains without growing.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	And I depart from these parts, and be that God made of me afterward.
de l’uve	Of the eye.
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When a beam descends to the earth, and it is swollen and long, it is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	And if it is thick and round below, it is called an "egg".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it is hollowed out as we have said in the division, and the ulcer does not heal, and you see that the flesh around the abscess is calm and delicate, then you must cut it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	And that which is round and gathered together, not long;
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	and if it is bloody or false colored or black, you must avoid incising it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For there is great danger to the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	Therefore, when you see it, according to the manner I mentioned, considering its whiteness and length, make the patient sit facing the sun, and press their tongue against the instrument we previously discussed.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then insert the needle into the eye, draw it out from underneath, and cut at the intersection of the two instruments that I mentioned for incising both testicles.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And you must not cut any further than the superfluous matter that is beyond the natural limit.
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	for if you cut any more, it will harm their voice and speech.
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And after the incision, use what we have said regarding the incision of the two almonds, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the patient fears cutting, you must employ an engine for cauterization to ease their fear.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	And the manner of the cautery is quicksilver.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And have the patient put their head in your lap, and then press their tongue with the instrument we mentioned in the chapter on cauterization, and mix it with hot water that is neither too thick nor too thin;
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	use the tip of this instrument, which has this shape:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And on the head, make a hair-like incision where one would apply the medicine, like the teeth of a spoon, and place the instrument over all the medicine applied to the eye;
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	And have the patient lie on their side so that the saliva and mucus run out of their mouth, carrying the medicine with them, to prevent it from going down their throat and harming them;
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	Then hold your hand over all the medicine and press it onto the eye, for a quantity of half an hour, until you see it blacken and the stinging from the medicine subsides;
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	And if you see this, take some cotton and wrap it around an instrument, then dampen the cotton with the medicine and insert the instrument through the cotton into the eye until the cotton rests on the eyeball.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	Do this frequently until the cauterization is complete, then let it dry out, and it will fall off after four or five days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	If you need to repeat the medicinal cauterization then do so and afterwards wipe around the eye with cotton soaked in butter, cleaning away any excess medicine.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And it is immersed in cold water, and it is healed with gargles until it is cured.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is safer than incisions or cauterization;
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	if it is treated with fumigation in this way, take gentian and hyssop and oregano and rue and chamomile and similar herbs, and combine all or some of them in one pot, adding easy-to-find items, then boil it;
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	and the pot is well-glued with strong clay, and inside the pot have an instrument carved in this way:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And it is made of silver or copper, and one end is inserted into the patient's mouth so that the vapour rises to the affected eye until it is mortified.
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	After you restart it often, until the wound dries up, and take care not to do this at the beginning of the appearance of the abscess being hot, because many things happen there.
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	and do not attempt to do this for the decline of a hot abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not present, take a cane and put a piece of egg white into the patient's mouth so that their mouth does not get too hot.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	because the egg white will not let the steam harm the mouth, and this is a good treatment for overall health.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times it happens to the throat due to a fish bone or spine, or some other object.
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	So you must treat what you can see, and press the tongue with the sun towards the instrument so that you can see the movement of things.
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	And for that which does not appear to you and is stuck in the throat, it is necessary to make the patient vomit before the meat is cooked in the stomach.
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	Perhaps by this the thing will be expelled through vomiting.
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	Or if the patient swallows a piece of sponge, or a piece of sailcloth, or a lettuce root, or a crumb of dry bread.
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	And tie to the sponge a thread, then swallow it.
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	And when it reaches its place, it will be expelled, and then you will pull on the thread.
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if it does not come about from what we have said, then take a lead instrument of this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	and let the instruments be curved towards the head so that they may more easily enter the throat, and have the head raised upwards.
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	and ensure that you do not touch the epiglottis, lest choking occur, nor push against the bone within.
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	and it is better that the patient inserts the instrument, because he knows where things are located.
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	then insert it downward or pull it out forcefully with all the instrument evenly until it is fully removed.
de la sansue de la gorge	from the phlegm of the throat
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	In some cases, surgery may be the treatment of choice as I have mentioned before in our classification system;
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	and when this does not work, then look into the patient's throat in the sunlight, and press their tongue with the instrument I mentioned to you.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	And if you see the leech, draw it out with a very small hook, or use delicate forceps that are suitable for this purpose.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if this does not work, take a hair from the tail of a horse, insert it into the patient's throat, then attach a hot iron to the end of the hair, and repeat this frequently.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And if the patient has water retention all day long.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	then take a full glass of cold water, open their mouth, pour it in as if they were swallowing, and move their hand frequently;
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	and as soon as the tongue feels the water, it will stop.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	If it does not stop as we have said, then smoke the patient with asafetida, using the instrument I mentioned for the fumigation of the eye.
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	Do this many times, for it will stop without fail.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	And the manner of the fumigation is such that you take a pot with visible coals, and cover it with a perforated cover in the middle, and through this hole place the head of the instrument.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	Then I throw my fumigation, and the patient places the head of the cane in their mouth, closing it so that no smoke escapes, but rather goes up to the tonsils.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	And now the tonsils will fall out, and if they do not, restart the fumigation several times;
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	And let the patient feel thirsty, eating salty things and such, but not drinking water;
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	And then it will be necessary for them to go outside due to this treatment.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the shape of the instrument used to extract leeches is like bent tongs when one can see them, with curved arms for insertion into the throat.
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	and it resembles the beak of a bird with its roughness like that of a file, such that what it grasps, it cannot release.
et vez ci la forme:	and you will see here the form;
li chapistres des apostemes	The chapters of abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	There are many variations of abscesses as the following accounts from one source and another in this book describe, differing according to whether they are punctured or cut.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	and it is in two ways first according to its appearance itself, and second because of the moisture it holds.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second kind is according to their location in the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	For abscesses of the head are different from those of the fundament, and abscesses in fleshy places are different from those that come to joints, and each has its own treatment.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And if there are abscesses, one must not pierce them as long as the bowels remain dead according to their condition.
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	And if there are such cases that require piercing when they are ripe, and the bowels do not die according to their condition, like abscesses near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	For when abscesses develop near joints, and one leaves it until it rots all around, perhaps the ligaments and nerves of the joint are corrupted, which is why this causes contraction in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	When the abscess is near the main limb, and if you delay the piercing until it dies, it will harm the principal member.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	When the abscess is near the fundament, pierce it without waiting for it to die.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	And one must not pierce a ripe abscess without completing the digestion process unless it is near the fundament and cannot rot in place, and become elongated inside with the development of a fistula.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	And it cannot heal within a long time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	And you should know the stage of the abscess' perforation which is ripe according to its development, and this is when the pain eases, and the fever breaks, and there is lessening of the pain and redness, and from the softening and pointing of the head of the abscess, and other signs;
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	and you must make the perforation sit where the base of the abscess is, and where it appears softer;
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	and let the perforation be along the length of the body, and if the abscess is in the hands or feet, or in joints and near nerves and arteries, and in all places equally where there is no bending.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In those that bend, according to that member.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when the abscess is in fleshy tissue, it is better that you allow the perforation to remain until it is confirmed as healed by complete digestion, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	For if you pierce it before this, then the body would be elongated by the venom from it, and it is full of much filth.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	and perhaps harden the lips and its depths.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And for any abscess that is pierced according to the breadth of the body, according to what the member requires.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	And you must treat small abscesses and minor injuries;
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	and in large abscesses, big wounds, and many cracks according to the resemblance of the size of the abscess;
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	and if at such abscesses where it is necessary to sever the heart, and cut;
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	when it becomes young like wool, and is soft, then you must do as with boils;
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	And there are some that are split into three angles, and there are others from which one also scrapes like the leaf of myrtle, just as in abscesses caused by gangrene.
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	And there are some where one makes a round incision, and other incisions and similar cuttings.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	Those without a head, such as soft superficial abscesses, should be pierced fully through;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	And when the abscess is large, and it has formed a great amount of pus, and you pierce it, do not extract all the pus at once that hour, but only some.
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	Then pack the abscess with wool until the next day, then extract any remaining matter immediately.
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	Do this several times from place to place until the bowels are completely emptied.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	Especially if the patient is of weak constitution, or a pregnant woman, or small children, or elderly decrepit men.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For the spirits sometimes twitch with the exit of the bowels, which by chance may kill the patient, and you won't realize it.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	So use this chapter with great caution and, when you have pierced your abscess, dry the wound, then examine whether the wound from the abscess is small.
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	And if it is an open gash wound, pack with linen bandages or old cotton rags.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	And if it is a large abscess with many openings, you must insert a bandage into each one so that they touch each other.
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	and if you have cut into the abscess and a portion of the skin, you must fill it with old cotton or lint from linen cloth without moisture, and bind it until the third day;
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then remove the bandage, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if there is bleeding during your procedure, bring cold and light water, dampen the cloths, and place them on the bleeding area multiple times.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	And if the discharge of blood persists, apply medication and ointment, and the powders I have mentioned in various places in this book, and if it is during winter, and the wound or abscess is very raw, you must place tents and moist bandages with wine and warm oil on them;
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	and if it is during summer, and the wound is fleshy, you must apply moist bandages with water and oil, or cold wine and oil, until the third day, as we have said;
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then unbind the abscess, wipe it clean, and treat it as necessary until it is healed.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	This must be known universally in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	I have told you how one should proceed before treating an abscess, and here is the chapter.
des soros	abscesses
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	Where the skull of the head is soft come small abscesses, and they are like cloth, similar to the inside of a hen's egg, and there are many such things (abscesses).
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	There are fat ones and hard ones where there is also moisture like pus;
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	And there are hard ones with stones in them, which are not dangerous if the arteries do not behave contrary to expectations.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the work of cutting is such that you must test every instrument which is called an "entromissoire", from which its form comes afterwards, what thing it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	For if there is moisture present, they do so above the long bone.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when the moisture is drained, one should carefully remove the skin that contained this moisture without leaving anything behind, for it will return if you leave any.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	Then dip cotton into Egyptian ointment if present;
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	If not, dip it in water and salt, apply it to the wound, and leave it there until the next day.
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	And this will cure what remained from the night before.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And you may replace the cotton, as before, on the second day, and the third, until you know for sure that nothing remains from the night.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with an appropriate ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if the abscess retains its fat, cut it open in this manner, from end to end.
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	And you throw your relatives aside, flay them from all sides, and pay close attention to drawing out the bone where it lies.
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	And if the artery makes you hesitate, do as I have told you after that.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And also of the abscess if it is full, and of cutting and treating as I have told you.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And the incision on the full abscess and moisture is lighter, as they have little blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if some of these abscesses or heads lack moisture, like the one I cut from an old woman's head;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	and I found the abscess like a hard stone, rough and white, and it could not be broken.
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	and if one were to have cut it open, they would have also made a wound as deep as that of a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	In other abscesses occurring on the head, whether those that come to children's heads or at the roots of ears, the opening should always be in the lowest place, so as to let out the pus;
et les cure si com il covient.	and treat them as they ought to be treated.
des scrophules	scrofula
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	Often these abscesses occur on the neck, and beneath the armpits, and in the groin, and sometimes elsewhere on the body, and they are numerous, and connected to each other.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	And each scrofula is properly within its side, just as the knot and abscess of the head, as we have said;
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	and there are many similarities to these scrofulas.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	There are some that contain moisture, and there are malignant ones that do not want to obey the rules of health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	in that which you see is of good disposition to touch, and is similar in colour to the body, and moves from each side and is not empty towards the nerves of the neck nor the artery or the passage, and it is not deep;
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	You must cut it from above and peel the skin away in each part, stretching the two lips of the heart with pincers if you need to, just like we said for head abscesses;
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	Keep jabbing it back and forth, making sure you don't cut the nerve or vein, nor use sharp spatulas that might slip from your hand, lest you cut too deeply without seeing what's ahead, cutting something you should not.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you cut a vein or artery and it will not stop bleeding, apply powdered glass or herbs that staunch blood to the wound, binding up the injury tightly.
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	Leave it alone until the abscess is drained, and the wound softens, beginning to fester with rot.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when the blood is stemmed, return to your work until you complete it.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	Then examine with your index finger if there remain any small boils; remove them and clean them thoroughly.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if there is a large wound at the root of the boil, it is not advisable to cut this boil in its root, but bind it with a strong double thread and let it fall off on its own, without harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then dress the wound with old cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment, then heal it.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	And if you remove the entire scrofula, then you must bring together the two lips of the wound, and suture them now, given that there has been no delay in treating the size of the scrofula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	you must proceed to cut the root of it, and draw out the humors, and suture it as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	Boils that hold excessive pus should be lanced where they appear to die off.
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	And pierce it like that one mentioned before, depending on the situation, then apply tenting with ointment and similar treatments so that it corrupts what remains of the corruption.
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the wound is well cleaned, treat it with ointment to encourage flesh growth until it heals.
de squinance	of dislocation
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The ancients spoke of the incision in the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	But I have never seen it done in our land, this is merely the writing of their words.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	For those with difficulty breathing, it is necessary that the flap in the throat known as the epiglottis be removed.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	And if no help is given by this method, it is because all the veins and passages of the patient are affected by abscesses hot in the mouth, or in the throat or both tonsils.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the illness is in the channel of the pore, it is necessary to cut the epiglottis to escape the destruction that comes from suffocation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	It is necessary, then, when we wish to split the epiglottis, that we divide it beneath three circles or four with a small crosswise incision between two circles or in accordance with the quantity of the incision on the surface, not at all in the cartilage.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	And these veins are suitable for the division of the epiglottis because there is no flesh at this point, and the vessels are long in quantity.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	And if the master is afraid, it is necessary that he stretches the skin of the throat entirely around, then divides the heart until he reaches the trachea.
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	And remove the vessels of blood, if you see anything, then cut the surface as we have said.
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	And it is proven by the cutting of the dog's windpipe that death occurs from the place where it was broken and through the fault of the voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	Leave the wound open in one piece.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	And when the time has passed that one doubts strangulation, bring together the two lips of the wound from the heart, and sew it all up without the cartilage.
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then administer medicine that promotes flesh growth until it is healed.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Al-Bukhari states that one should not do this until the throat is completely blocked, and the patient is judged to be dying, and breathing becomes impossible.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Therefore make a hole in the epiglottis for when the patient cannot breathe, and they will inhale through the wound, thus saving them from death.
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	And for this the ancients commanded to leave the wound open until the poison of the disease has passed, and it passes in three or four days. Then they would command to sew up the wound and treat it until it was cured.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	And I will tell you what I saw.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	I saw that a damsel took a knife, and thrust it into her throat, cutting part of the veins of the heart.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	And I was called upon to cure her, but I found her as good as dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I uncovered the wound and found blood flowing from it; I knew she had not cut a vein or damaged her lungs, but air was escaping through the injury.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	I hurried, sewed up the wound, and treated her until she was healed.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	And all it took for the damsel was to clear her throat, and she returned to her normal self afterwards.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	Therefore I say that there is no fear in cutting the epiglottis.
de la grosse gorge	Of the swollen throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	This abscess is called "hernial goiter", and it is a large abscess with a yellow colour, which occurs often in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	and it has two types:
naturez, et accidens;	natural and accidental;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	or natural has no cause.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	And the accidental type has two forms: one similar to our fat, and the other form resembles an abscess caused by our artery;
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	and there is fear, and it should not be treated with fire cautery except in the small one, proven and sought after by all those who are involved:
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	If you find it as hard as our fat, and cannot reach any vein, cut it like one cuts nails, and draw out all its skin if there is no hair.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	And cauterize it quickly, and treat it as required until it is perfectly healed.
des nous	Des nous
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	There are many ways to do this, of which I will describe all the similarities;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	And it is necessary that I explain all the differences between our method and theirs.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	I say that theirs is hot and feverish until the ebullition passes, and the putrefaction is complete;
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	Then the fever and heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	With the nut there is no heat, fever, or pain, and it contains one cystic, which is its own sack and matches the body's colour. It starts like a pimple and becomes swollen
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	and they come in two forms: hard or soft, and very varied in colour as I have said before.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	It is necessary, when you come to treat the shoulder, that you first examine and inquire about all the instrument which is called an 'entromissoire', according to how its form will appear in the following chapter.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	The way to examine abscesses is as follows: take the softest spot you can find on the abscess and rotate your fingers back and forth until you feel the instruments have pierced through. Make sure this is proportionate to the size of the abscess.
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	Then withdraw the instrument carefully so as not to spill anything.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	If running moisture is clear, whatever its colour, treat it as I have said for other abscesses;
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	And if no moisture comes after the opening instrument is used, know that it is greasy, so treat it in a cross shape, and take pincers to gently peel away the skin from each side and keep the membrane where it lies so you draw it out clean with the knot.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	And if you cannot draw it out clean, then pull it out by pieces so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	For if anything remains, the wound will return many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if a little remains and the blood bothers you, then fill the wound with some sharp corrosive powders, tighten the wound, and put on hot substances that ease abscesses, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	And if it is large to us, then cut the two lips of the wound, and treat that which produces flesh.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	And if the beating vein is contrary to you or otherwise causes hastiness, use a place of powdered vitriol, and leave it bound for two days or three, until the wound rots, and stops the boiling of blood.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	Then return to cut away that which has remained from the night.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	See here the forms of instruments for insertion, and they are of three kinds:
grans et moien et petit;	Large, medium, and small.
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	And there are three types of squares, which are called "albaret", and one type is called "breb", and they come in three ways:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	Large, medium, and small, to surround abscesses of fistulas.
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	And they are like the needles with which we sew seams, and they are made of yellow brass, or iron, or silver, and those that are golden are better suited for treating gangrenous fistulas.
et sont de III manieres:	And they come in three types:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	Large, medium, and small, depending on the size of the wound.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The shapes of the probes are very similar to these:
grans, moiens, et petis;	Large, medium, and small.
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	And there are probes that have two curves of three types as well;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	and so for those who have three dislocations, and they are also of three kinds;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	and also for those who have two dislocations or only one dislocation, and they are of three types
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	and all these [dislocations] are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	The head of these [dislocations] is where they are sharp, and there are some that only cut from one side, which can strip away the nerves because the vein or nerve is not severed.
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	and these intrusive ones [dislocations] are the raised responses in many cases, so that the patient does not perceive them when abscesses open.
et sont de III manieres:	and they are of three kinds:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	large, small, and medium, as you see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	and one should not use fire there unless it is in fleshy areas like legs, arms, breasts, and similar places;
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	and sometimes one makes another small instrument, similar to the bark of fig trees, according to this form, with which blood is stopped:
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and it is placed back into position to heal by compression of the veins, arteries, and sometimes according to this large form.
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	Sometimes men's breasts swell when they begin to deteriorate, so that they resemble women's breasts;
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	and they remain ugly and swollen, and for those who wish to cure them, one should proceed according to this form of the following lines .b. until .g..
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	Then scrape away the fat, and fill the wound with medicinal flesh-forming paste, then join together the two lips of the wound with stitches, and treat it until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	And if the nipple sags downwards, and is softened due to its size like what happens in women, make an incision into it in two parts above with similar cuts;
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	so that one part holds the other at their end, so that the greater line contains the lesser according to this form, from this line (b) up to the line (g);
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then scrape away the skin that is between the two lips, and remove the fat, and apply what we have mentioned about stitches and powders, and whatever is necessary for treatment, until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	and if it is not healed, or the incision is not fully complete, due to the patient's unwillingness to rest, or because of blood loss, you must fill the wound with moist cotton soaked in corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	and leave it until the membrane and fat separate, then clean it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	Of abscesses under the armpits
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses which come from under the armpits are like hard scrofulae when they have sides, and if there is moisture contained within them.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those which contain moisture should be cut according to this form, from line b. to line g.
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the matter within the abscess is evacuated, fill the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day; then remove all the cotton, and dress it gently until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.
