And if the abscess resembles a scrofula, treat it as we have said for scrofulae incisions; and if the wound is deep, apply cauterization as mentioned before.
de la routure de l’artere	From the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is torn, and the skin above it is sealed, many abscesses often occur, and likewise, swelling and abscesses appear in the vein.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and if you recognize it as such for the artery, then the abscess is long and perforating.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your hands, you sense a tightening.
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is for the vein, there are clear reasons to act;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolishness to cut this abscess, especially when it is below the armpits and on the neck and many other places, and it is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	One must therefore avoid iron treatment, and for the one at the head, it should also be avoided, as well as in cases of an arterial swelling that breaks through above the long skin.
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then operate at the waist with a lancet, and carefully separate the artery from the veins until it is exposed.
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then insert a needle below it and pierce through to the other side, and secure the artery with a doubled thread in two places, according to what I taught you about extracting the two arteries located at the temples.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	Then mark the place between the two ligaments of a tourniquet so that the blood there comes out and the abscess is loosened.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	Then bring about the treatment that drains the pus until the ligament falls away.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat what is next to it, proceeding in order until it is healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	And if the abscess is on account of the size of the vein, then you must grasp with your hand as much of the abscess and skin as possible, then push the needle beneath the place that you hold in your hand, and make it pierce through, and have a double thread so that you draw it out from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	Then bind the abscess, as I have told you, with a ligament of one part to two parts of the thread.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	And if you doubt that the thread will not go through, insert another needle along its path beneath all of the abscess to the incision of the first needle and hold the threads in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then lance the abscess until all of its excess comes out, then lance the heart's superfluity and leave what is bound.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Place upon it a cloth moistened with wine and oil, then treat him with tenths of the ointments until he is healed.
des apostemes des ners	Of abscesses of nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Likewise abscesses come to the arteries and veins, abscesses come to the nerves when they are torn, or due to excessive heavy labor, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	These happen more often in the shoulders and hands where there are joints, and they become abscesses, taking on a colour resembling that of the body with pain felt across many areas.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	And when it is held tightly, the patient feels pain, and it is not complete within the body, but beneath the heart.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	It moves well from all sides, it neither goes forward nor backward, not below or above, and one that is dislocated should not be cut with iron.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	Perhaps there would be contraction in this case.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And one who is at the head or forehead should make an incision with a spatule.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with forceps and cut it at its root.
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is large, suspend it with a hook and remove the skin; then take out the abscess and sew up the wound, treating it until it is healed.
des grosses boces pendans	large boils hanging down
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes occurs in bellies and nowhere else an inflammation, and it is a disease called "fungus" due to its likeness with mushrooms, and its root is subtle but the head large.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and in it there are small ones and very big ones.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw a man who had two in his belly which resembled mushrooms more than anything else, and there was no difference, they were white, had fine roots, were slightly split, and moisture came out of them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them open and found one weighing eighteen ounces, while the other weighed six thirds. The procedure for incision is to check whether the patient is moist, and if the material's colour is white, moist, with a fine root. 
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	If you treat the broad spinal bone, let the fire cautery be present before you.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	As there is often too much loss of blood from the cutting, and if you faint from it, then quickly begin with cauterization.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	And if you see the patient afraid and fearful of the incision with iron, then take a well-made thread of lead, and bind it to the arm as we have said, leaving it for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	Then restrain them, and do not stop tightening the lead thread until it reaches the arm bone, each time feeling for work by it.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	And if the roots are thick, fear to cut them especially in the belly, but you can well cut half of it, then cauterize so that it does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and make sure you do not cut the tissue that is of a pale colour and poor texture and has no veins.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an aggravated abscess, and I shall come to the treatment of cancer afterwards.
quant li boude ist fuer	When it rages with hunger.
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of swelling comes from a wound cauterization or tear caused by poison, and it is on the abdomen and affects some of the intestines, as happens in other injuries, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries according to what was mentioned before, or due to windiness;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is due to the tear caused by poison and the release of pus, then its colour is similar to that of the body, being a mild condition without pain and appearing with multiple discharges.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to an intestinal discharge, then it becomes more varied: when pressed by two fingers it retracts and reappears, or perhaps it stretches out, becoming enlarged at the entrance of the bath and after heavy labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a minor issue, and it becomes apparent when you press it with your hand, but it does not cause any restriction.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it is due to blood, it shows these signs: large, hard abscesses that are fixed in one place according to a certain quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is due to wind or gas, it is soft to the touch; and for the treatment, you must examine whether its appearance indicates arterial blood, venous blood, or wind/gas.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	You should leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For he has doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding arteries and veins.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	and if it appears to be related to the intestines or the stomach, you must instruct the patient to hold their breath and lie flat and straight; then bleed them all around the navel.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then have them lay frequently in your hands, and go around the place you marked with all your fingers; then extend half of the abscess above all the large thumb.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then tie it around with a strong thread or a cord of sturdy silk firmly, and let the knot be secure.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Next, open the extended half of the abscess over the knot, and insert your index finger, searching for the intestine.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you find it trapped by the knot, untie it, and push the intestine out of the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find the wound, grasp it with a hook, and cut away any excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	If the artery or vein opposes you, go around it carefully, then return to your work and take two needles, insert two strong threads, and pass the two needles through what you have pierced in a cross pattern.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then extract the abscess in four locations above the needles, and if you see it, remove the needles, leaving the place to rot, and let the dead flesh fall off by itself.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	or you must cut it when it is soft and rotten, then treat it with what is appropriate, and heal the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and extract the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the place with what is necessary, and heal the wound.
dou chancre	Of cancer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have spoken about the likenesses of cancer in the division, and how to treat it with medicine, and how one must avoid iron treatment.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And we say that cancer engrained in the flesh requires great caution in its treatment, and the ancients said that when cancer is in a place where it can be scraped away like cancer of the breasts, thighs, and similar places, one must remove it entirely at its beginning.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	And when it is large and old, you should not attempt to treat it, for I have never been able to heal anyone in such a condition.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	No one has ever healed it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And for the treatment, when it is in place and can be removed as we have said, you should purge the patient of black bile once.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	Then make the patient bleed if there is evident congestion, then prepare him well to undergo the treatment.
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	Then remove your ulcers or cancerous growths, shave him all over, and extract it completely from every part without leaving any remains.
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And let the blood flow freely, press the area well with your hand or an object, and if the outflow of blood opposes the incision of the artery or vein, then cauterize it until the bleeding stops.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat with another treatment until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already spoken about the different types of dropsy, and how the accumulation of water is formed, along with the signs of each type, and the cures that can be achieved through medicine or surgery.
si est eclites soulement;	So it has been written.
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	And one should not use iron in these two types (of dropsy).
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	That is to say, tympanites and yposarche, for they are mortal afflictions.
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when you treat this type of dropsy called 'eclites' with medicine, and the cure is ineffective, consider if the patient is weak or suffering from other ailments like constipation, stomach issues, and similar conditions.
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	If you use iron [instruments], then there is doubt [about the outcome].
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	And if you see the patient is strong [has a strong constitution], and he has no other disease but only dropsy, and he is neither too young nor too old, then proceed like this:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Make the patient lie straight on your hands, and press his abdomen with your fingers to release water from the lowest part of the stomach [abdomen], then take the sharp-edged instrument in this manner:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	Et let it be divided into two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	It should be sharp-pointed but not so much as to reach the intestine when inserted and cause injury.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	Then examine if the dropsy is directed towards the intestines.
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	You must cut above the hump three fingers directly above the wrist.
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	And if it is due to liver disease, your incision should be on the left side of the hump at three fingers' width.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	If it is due to the spleen, then make your incision on the right side, and ensure that the patient does not lie directly over the wound so as not to weaken the afflicted area with their weight.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	Then pierce the entire skin with your instrument and push it through, lifting your hand to take all of the excess skin between the hide and the subcutaneous layer just like you would when skinning an animal down to one nail's width or less.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	Pierce the subcutaneous layer until the water cavity is reached and then drain it by drawing out all of the fluid, using this tool which I will now describe.
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a subtle silver cane, and is made of light brass or iron, and has on its underside a small hole.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and where it ends on one side, there are three holes.
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two at the other end, and one on another side;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the tip is cut like a quill, which is the shape of the incision as described by the writers who cut quills.
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top is an arm, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it immediately rises up onto the instrument.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty it then by half or a third part, because if you empty more than is appropriate at that time, perhaps the patient will die due to their spirit leaving the body, or they may fall unconscious, or they may come close to death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but evacuate it according to its quantity of virtue, and according to what the condition of the patient's virtue signifies, and his pulse;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then draw out the instrument and retain the water, and it is retained now for the heart which stops up the perforation that I spoke of on the surface, in this way that you pierce it;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then reinsert the instrument the next day if you see the patient suffering this, and draw out a small quantity of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this every day, and be careful not to draw out too much water but only a little bit.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you are doubtful about the patient and leave a lot of water inside them, it will destroy the heart due to excessive sweating or bathing in hot sand or sun, and prevent them from drinking.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And treat with drying medications until it is healed, and cauterize over the stomach, liver, and spleen after draining the water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	Of the stopping of the penis.
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	There are times when children are born without an opening in the penis, or with a small one, or it is not in its correct position.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to pierce it sometimes with a very fine spatula in this way...
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then insert a soft tube into the bladder, and bind it, holding it for three or four days. When he wishes to urinate, remove the tube, let him urinate, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And perhaps it is not necessary, for the urine that comes out will not allow the tube to stay in place.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those in whom the fistula is small will be treated with the white lead plug as we have said and this will widen it.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the tube in its proper place are distressed, as some people are born without a tube at the head of their penis, which is why they cannot urinate unless they lift their penis upwards.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and cannot heal because the material cannot reach the marrow, and it is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	and the method of treatment is to have the patient lie on their back, then stretch the head and neck as if they were extending an arrow, so that the hole pierces through in the middle, just as it should be.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and beware of the escape of blood which often happens, and if it does, stop it with what stops bleeding, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	Pustules on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	This inflammation often occurs in the throat, and it is an appearance of ugly flesh.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and there are malignant and non-malignant ones.
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	You must take them with a subtle pincers, grasp and clean them all, then place cotton moistened with Egyptian ointment over it.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat with fine healing Diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, of a foul colour and stinking, then you must apply a cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cleaned it, and if the albath is on top of the rod, and has part inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the albath that is inside.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	And when it is fused, treat it from the outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat them together, the head of the rod is not secured so it may be pierced, and blackness and decay will come inside the rod and joint.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	You must cut away all that is black and corrupt, then bind it with a plaster made of honey and flour which has been prepared from pomegranate bark and figs, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, apply the lunar caustic according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauteries assist the two dispositions together.
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	That is to say, in the evacuation of blood and in corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	And if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, you must insert a hollow reed into the penis and make the patient urinate through it.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the skin is tight at the head of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it occurs due to a wound or abscess, then you must peel it with a sharp instrument so that the ties are loosened, and release the head of the penis from all sides.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if this is an important thing to discuss, you must then peel it with a spatula on some part of the head of the penis and skin.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	then carefully remove it between two [fingers], and place a fine linen cloth dampened in cold water, so that it does not dry out again.
de la circoncision	Of circumcision.
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	circumcision is not like the separation of continuity as with other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	nevertheless when we do this work of our own accord, and especially for children, it is necessary that we perform the best work, and the most gentle for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of circumcising their children, for they do not practice it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	for I have seen most masters and doctors performing circumcision around one day, with forceps, and all at once [i.e., in one cut];
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	If the heart was pierced because there were two knives, and perhaps one of them fell out while the other remains inside.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now you must cut it out again, and the pain is doubled, and during the removal which comes from its root, the tip of the knife was not properly secured inside the body.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	And during the removal of the nail, perhaps the iron slips and runs wild, and many times it happens that they do not need treatment and I wish to share this with you.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le lien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	Because when you press your hand, you cut evenly across all the flesh beneath it.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	But make sure that the knife is tightly wrapped in leather.
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and let the method of the first operation be such that you make the child believe, if he understands, that you are not tying a thread around his penis just enough, and then you can make him ejaculate in any way you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then make it stand straight between your hands, and hide the cords between your hands or below your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then put your hand on his penis and blow into the heart, and pull it upwards so that the head of the penis is inside;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then clean it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then tie the place with a doubled thread, and bind it below with another link;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	Et hold it with your two fingers - the thumb and index finger - and cut between the two lines, then lift up the heart quickly and draw out the head of the penis.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	Then let the blood flow forth repeatedly, for this is an injury.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And put powder on top and cover the powder with a cloth glued with raw egg cooked in rose water, prepared with good fresh oil, and leave it there until the next day; treat him with other remedies until he is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The shape of the forceps for cleaning is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The two blades should be curved and sharp, and the blades should also be as big as the handles equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error of purification is when the heart within escapes to the incision.
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, you must stretch it with your nail, otherwise the flesh will form an abscess.
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, then grasp it with pliers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if it exceeds three days, and that which is beneath the ridge becomes swollen, then leave it until the hot abscess subsides, and gently pare it.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	Then cut it as you can move, and take care of the part of the ridge, this will not harm anything.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Cure therefore the location of burning wounds with powder, as we have said in the treatment of powders, and if it bleeds excessively from the heart outwards, and it goes above (the wound), it will not harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat it therefore, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	where there is retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is caused by the obstruction of stones, or frozen blood, or faeces, or new flesh (scar tissue), or similar things, which we have mentioned in the section on obstructions.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not released, and you find that the retention is due to stones in the lower part or neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent forward over their knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and place his feet on his back, and stretch out his belly from the upper part of his back, and restrain the patient's elbow as much as you can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then the neck of the bladder is constricted by the expression of the stone above it, which loosens the urine and allows it to pass.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it doesn't come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must perform an extraction with all the instrument which is called "syringe," this is its form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and made of fine silver, light as the feather of a bird's wing;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and be half a palm in length with a fine point at its tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And for the method of urine evacuation, you must take a doubled thread, and tie it to one end of a wool or cotton bag, then insert the other end of the thread into the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	cut the excess wool and push it up to the end of the syringe, then lubricate the syringe with oil or butter and a raw egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a stool, anointing their bladder and penis with moist oil, olive oil, and warm water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the organ, and bend the penis upward toward the belly.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	push the syringe forward into the bladder, and have the patient feel it until the bladder is empty, this cannot be done correctly if the guide (the syringe) has gone astray from its intended path.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch the thread through all the wool here and there, and the urine will follow the wool, then extract it out, and make the urine flow.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And restart the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and let the patient rest.
des maladies de la vessie	Of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scalding or blood enters the bladder, and putrefaction has gathered there, and you wish to see urine and medicines distilled, then make the whole instrument which is called "clepsydra", and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	And the narrow end which the doctor cuts should be such that it stops up the tube well without addition, so that one can draw out the moisture and push when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you see that your medicine is being put into the bladder, place the head of the syringe into the moisture, and draw out what comes next;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	If you draw out the moisture with a caustic agent, then firmly reset it by pulling on it.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	It will enter the moisture within, and come to the bladder immediately so that the patient feels it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	And this is the subtle form of the enema with which we enema the bladder.
si est ci:	Here it is:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or tin, with the head being at the top.
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	And you loosen it at the side where the ligaments fall.
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture you wish to enema into it, then tie it between the two breasts with a strong piece of thread, and heat this pouch over fire.
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then insert the head of the clyster into the urethra, then press your hand onto the bladder with all your might until the patient feels that this moisture has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	And if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make it into a circle, then pierce it roundly all around.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	Then insert a strong thread through this hole, then gather the circle as one would gather a bag, and put in whatever you wish of oil, moisture, and water, and tie it to the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	Of a stone.
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have spoken of the types of stones and their extraction along with treatments.
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and explained the distinction between kidney stones in the bladder and all their symptoms, as well as which stones require surgical intervention.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	in the bladder and in the urethra;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that stones which form in the bladder occur more often in children, and it is a sign that the urine escapes from the bladder like water in its subtlety.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and it makes the patient's urethra hard and rough, causing them to urinate frequently, and then it scabs over.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	And to many of them it causes their foundations (to fail).
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	And healing is light for children until the age of four years, and it is very difficult in the elderly, and it is average for those who are young, for those who are between youth and old age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And the treatment is lighter for those who have large stones, compared to those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to draw out all the bile that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes impedes trying to reach the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, lift them up and move them downwards, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it falls out from above.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	Then have the patient sit between your prepared hands, with their hands placed below their thighs, so that the bladder is completely declined downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	Then you grasp it and feel inside.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in space, then quickly proceed to cut above the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall upon touch from all sides, then wet your index finger with oil from the left hand if the patient is an infant, or your middle finger if they are a grown youth;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and push it into the base, and feel for the stone, and when you sense it with your finger, then direct it toward the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press down on your finger, and push the stone outside at the place where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with their hand, and tell them to pull up the testicles with their right hand, and with their left remove the skin below the testicles in the area where the incision is made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then I inserted the spatula cutting, which is its shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And splitting what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the groin;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and be straight over the stone, and place your thumbs near the anus or foundation, and make the incision so that it is wide on the outside but narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	if by chance the incision hurts your thumbs that are near the anus, it may need more work;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there is such a stone where it has corners and edges;
si est griés a issir;	It must be pulled out gently.
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And if there is bone underneath, similar to a pea, and round with a small opening.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	Where it has corners and edges, make the incision wider;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	And if it doesn't come out, you must extract it with tongs that are like a file at the end to grasp and pull out the stone so that it does not escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	Or you push aside the delicate curved instrument from its head;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	And if you cannot manage it this way, then enlarge the hole with your finger, and if blood flows, extract it with vitriol.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there are multiple stones, push the largest one first towards the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, pull out with forceps, and treat the smaller ones afterward if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, you must take care of it, and make a bigger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	where either they die, or urine returns due to the wound being unable to heal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	nevertheless, make an effort to pull it out or crush it with tongs until you extract it in pieces.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and once you have completed your work, fill the wound with incense, aloe and dragon's blood, hold it tight and place on top a cloth moistened in oil and wine or in oil, rose water and cold water to soothe the hot abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then place the patient on their neck, and do not loosen the binding until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you release them, thoroughly wash the wound with oil and water, then treat it with ointment of daffodil and an ointment of basilicon until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if an abscess develops in the wound and there are blood clots in the bladder, causing a retention of urine, which is known to occur in such a manner that it comes out with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Push your finger into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will affect the bladder and cause damage;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then clean the wound with water, soap, and silk, and aid it in every way you know until it is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And during every hour of treatment, bind the two thighs together, and apply the remedies in place.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is lodged in the urethra, stuck within, and the urine cannot exit;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if the treatment I describe here requires cutting, you are excused from performing the cut due to this therapy.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven this thus.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take iron forged with three-pronged ends fixed on one spike:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot retreat into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then gently insert the probe into the penis until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the probe with your hand within the stone gently, until you are able to pierce it from another side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	the urine will come out immediately, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it is dislocated again soon, and urine is passed quickly, then the patient will recover.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that hinders you, then tie a thread under the stone and another above it, then make an incision in the flesh towards the stone between the two threads, then extract it quickly, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood from the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat them until they heal.
de la piere des femmes	Of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	Sometimes stones form in women, and if this happens once, then the treatment is quick, but it is prevented by three things:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	And secondly, one cannot find a woman who is an expert at revealing herself to mirrors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third manner is that, by chance, one cannot find a woman who is an expert in this craft of hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth manner is that the stone of the woman may be more perfect than that of a man, which requires a deeper incision and there is great fear involved. And if necessity arises for this, you must take an expert surgeon, and rarely can one be found, and if not, then seek out no chaste but subtle mirror;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And the present is a wise counsel in the life of women, or a woman who knows one part of this art, and instruct her to do what you command regarding the investigation of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and carefully check if the woman is a virgin;
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then it is necessary to insert one's finger into her anus and search for the stone.
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, push the stone away from your finger, and advise her to insert her finger into her vagina as deep as possible, and press and massage with her left hand firmly on top of the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, move the stone gradually from the bladder entrance to deeper inside until reaching the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then squeeze the stone in the root of the thigh towards the middle of the vagina where it is located, and feel for it in this area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	And do not move your thumb above or below the stone, let the incision be small at first.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	Then push the rod into the incision; if you feel a stone, widen the wound so that the stone can be extracted and know that there are many types of stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	That is to say, small and large, rough and soft, long and round, and those with cracks.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you know these similarities to understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood defeats you, quickly apply powdered vitriol, holding it there for an hour until the bleeding stops.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work, ensuring the stone is extracted and having the instruments I mentioned for extracting stones from men ready to assist you.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood overtakes you, and it is from an artery that has been severed, place the powder on the wound and apply the juice of tents and bandages, do not restart this procedure again, leave the stone alone and do not extract it, as the patient might die.
puis cure la plaie.	then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is cooled and the site is accessible, return to your work until the stone is expelled.
de hernie carnouse	Of fleshy hernia.
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ramus aqueous is nothing other than an accumulation of moisture or white of egg, which lies beneath the heart of calves and is contained within the egg.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called 'albumen', and sometimes it is properly contained within the membrane of the egg, so people think that it is another egg.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the calf's skin between the white of egg we have mentioned.
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And this does not happen unless the patient agrees.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ruminant aqueous is due to weakness that comes to calves, and this matter is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from blows to the hips, and this moisture has many colours:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	where it may be discoloured to yellow, or there is redness, blackness, white watery fluid, and this happens more frequently;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognise this dislocation, for if it is white and soft like we have said, then the abscess is ripe, ready to burst as with an egg, but does not open the hip joint because it has moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the surrounding tissue, then the abscess is ripe with part of the egg inside it, and for this reason people think that there are more than one.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if moisture is between the skin of the calves and the white sinew, one will feel it well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	therefore when you wish to know the colour of the moisture, test all parts as described above, from which its form is derived.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what comes after the introduction, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron [instruments], the patient must be bled according to their strength and the fullness of their body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then place them supine on their back, on something slightly elevated, and put a lot of cloth underneath them;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on their left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right, and stretch out the leg towards one of the two sides from the centre of the calves;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spatula and peel back the skin of the calves between their length to just below the wrist, and make your incision straight while dividing the calf muscle down until you see white fascia, then carefully remove it according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the white fascia with an aqueous solution through a wide orifice and extract all of the water and then place your fingers there to stretch out the fascia.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	And do not touch the heart of the calves but only the white fascia.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Peel it all or in pieces especially the side of him carefully so that if you don't remove all the water sufficiently it will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the egg pops out during your work then replace it in its place when you have finished treating the fascia.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then join the two sides of the heart of the oxen with a stitch, then treat it like other wounds until they are healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then you must bind the suspending vessels, fearing blood loss.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut open the oxen along with its suspension, extract the egg, and treat it as we have described.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if fluid gathers in two parts together, know that these are two branches.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	Cut open the other part as you did with the first one evenly, then wipe away the blood and place moist linen soaked in rose oil onto the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	et put defoer auter lane moilli en vyn eyn oylye, eyt syx lycyon, eyt dyssys drapayz doblyes, eyt ly lye syx tot ly lyn qe st sylons cesth forn
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	puys prayn syx drapayz, eyt llys emplye de lane charypy sylons cesth semblans eyt syont asyambley pyr custuure en la ghorle des brayes, eyt ly yns ddes chyays preynt sus ly fondymyn jusc’aw dos, eyt ly ytare a la partye du poynyl;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	eyt ly ytare duy cheyf syx lyssynglys, eyt syot tute asymblye ly restrynfor en la blyq du bayere;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	et sometimes this type of cautery is used instead of cutting with an iron knife, and you should take a thin scalpel-like cautery, and slice the skin from the testicles, and heat it as we have said so that the white part containing water is exposed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	then take the cautery in this manner, and pierce that white part with your nails, and scrape it with this heated fine cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And you should scrape it in every way possible until everything is scraped out.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg.
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is safer.
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And watch out for bleeding, and beware of operations involving cutting.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if anything opposes you, whether it be a hot swelling or bleeding or any other thing, then treat what opposes you according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	If the patient is fearful and unwilling to undergo this procedure due to its horror, then administer an anaesthetic as I have told you, and when you are confident through the signs we have discussed that water on the brain is present, make the patient sit on a raised seat.
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	Pierce the abscess below at twice the width of the thumb, and make the hole as long as the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	Make the openings wide so that all the water may flow out.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	Then place cotton on the spot, bind it, and leave it to drain the rest of the water, then treat until the wound is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	And if the white membrane does not allow water to escape through the wound's mouth, you must insert a feather or the instrument used for drawing water from hydropic patients, which is shaped as previously described.
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	Widen the wound's cavity, and know that water will return; it is gathered after six months or so, and when it has reassembled as before, then the patient will live through their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Be aware that in many situations when dealing with this branch of medicine there is much fear involved, therefore it seems to me better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you about the procedure and similarities of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say that many abscesses come from boils, especially on the head.
et c’est par mout de cas.	And it is due to these circumstances.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It arises from the excess of sour and sharp humours which is spread over the head, or by concussion.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	And its colour matches that of the boil.
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	It does not cause pain, but is a deep abscess.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	Sometimes a deep, fearful, stony-hard abscess is of a dark colour and originates from a new artery or the swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is due to arterial blood, it is recognized by the hot abscess-like disposition when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	One who is afflicted with edema of the vein is recognized by its feeling when touched with fingers, and one can properly make an incision on this as well as other similar swellings;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and it is that you cut the heart of quinsy, then break the egg above, and drain out its white substance, and remove the covering membrane from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already solid with these new growths, then you must drain out the egg and cut it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	For air is in the wound or within the vessels, you must release all that pressure and round off the edges.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is at the place behind, then you must cut it all away and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Once your work is completed, cover the wound with wet wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a swelling resembling a boil, with the softening of the flesh, and the patient becomes ill when it bursts.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment of this disease is almost as fearful as the one before it, yet we shall tell you its work, according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must have the patient sit on an elevated chair, then place the flesh-softening suspension below your two hands, at all vessels near the shaft, and hold them firm, while stretching it hard.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then cut with the sharp-edged spatula across the vessels until they are exposed, and then remove the skin from each side as we have said in the extraction of arteries found in temples.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then insert a needle where there is a doubled thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein has come, and then tie it again to the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them in half straight down the middle, along the length of the body, and remove the corrupted moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as with other bow wounds, so that no vessel bleeds to nourish one of the portions.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For in this way there is no harm done, and if all the vessels have become veins, it is necessary to drain the portions from all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the wind does not escape its direction due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry out and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	From a fracture of the sacrum
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The events of this branch are due to the rupture that occurs in the diaphragm or its extension on the abdomen in the area of the omentum, which causes the intestines to descend through this opening into one of the cavities.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	And this rupture is either in the diaphragm or its extension, and these two types of hernia arise from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	due to impact, jumping, straining, lifting heavy loads, or similar actions;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	The signs that it is an extension of the diaphragm are a gradual development over long periods and do not occur suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	And the abscess is equalized towards the surface, so that the skin covers the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are that when it's a case of sectioning in the sacrum, there is sudden pain at first and the abscess appears differently just below the skin, due to the intestine protruding through the body outside the sacrum.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the tendons descend with the intestine, getting caught, which causes great pain to endure for the patient, especially when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments with iron [instruments], there is fear, so it must be abandoned.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of treatment is that you instruct the patient to gather the intestine with their hand into the wound if they can reach it;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then support his neck between your hands, and lift up the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then extend the heart upwards, and cut all the skin from the hips down to the length of the leg;
