puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then push the hooks of the scissors into the abdomen, making an incision according to what is needed to open the wound, and make it such that the stomach can emerge;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then scrape off the sinew that lies beneath the hide of calves, so that the white hard sinew is uncovered on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then insert your index finger into the calf, in that which is between the white sinew lying beneath the hide of the egg, and the second sinew, separating what lies behind the egg from the second sinew;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And move your right hand inside the calf's heart, stretch the white sinew upwards towards your left hand, and lift the egg towards all of the sinews at the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	Instruct your assistant to stretch the egg upwards and untie that which is tied behind it;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	And look with your hands for signs of intestinal swelling or white hard cysts, and if you find any such things, push them down into the abdomen.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with a thick thread made of six strands, and insert it into the rear part of the cyst, which is beyond the sinews.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After measuring, cut through the head until you see four strands of thread appear.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then bring them together one on top of the other in a cross formation, and bind the cyst, which we said is beneath the sinews, with a strong two-strand thread.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the head of the thread and bind it with a two-strand thread so that none of the nourishing vessels can enter us, preventing an abscess from forming.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place again the ligament according to the first long ligament two fingers from that, and after these two ligaments leave a depression which is below the heart of the thigh the length of a finger.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after all this, follow the curvature that the egg presents
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut into the part that is below the skin of the thighs, as far as the blood and bowels run, just as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply damp wool with oil, and put it on the wound, and attach the ligament that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white skin we mentioned is cauterized after incision due to fear of excessive bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens many times, and leave the ligament until it dries on its own.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	And if it takes time to fall off, let it be soaked in warm water, and place on it what we have said [earlier], until it falls.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then treat the wound with another ointment, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	Of fleshy hernia.
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to treat it with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said it is made like a screw thread that holds together a nut, in such a way that you bind the vessels, after making an incision below and above [the wound] lightly.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut into the middle [of it], and treat the abscess with what works [on it], until the vessels fall out [i.e., are severed].
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes rupture occurs in anger, as we have said, and the skin tears.
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	And none of the intestines fall into the wound, but if they do, it is bad, and repair them every hour.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	However, if it remains too long at this stage, the wound or ulcer grows until the intestines fall out.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	This happens due to the extension of the ulcer at the wound, as we have said, for it is spread out, then softened and swollen, and the skin tears.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before.
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	Sometimes it is treated with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	And it is that the patient often lies on their back between your hands, then feel the place of the rupture swollen as wide as three fingers.
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	then extract the sinew that lies beneath the skin, then take the thread and place it on the surface of the wound.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	press it at the front of the belly, then cut two places visible on the wound above the head of the thread, and stitch one after another.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the head of the thread, and do not cut or stretch the sinew in any way, as I have instructed you for the treatment of intestinal rupture.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it with the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the sons' hairs, clean them thoroughly and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The surgeon is compelled to act; there are no signs of healing in the wound, and cauterization here is necessary for recovery.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	from softening the skin of the calves
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the calves is softened in some men, because the muscles within are weakened, and it is visible.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary, when one wishes to treat it, that the patient be made to lie on their back, and cut away the skin which has softened, down to natural flesh;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then join the two lips together with a seam, and if you wish to see it first sew away any excess of the softened skin with three or four firm stitches.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then cut between the seams, treat it like any other wound, until it is healed, then remove the thread.
dou chastrement	L'amputation
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that such procedures are taboo in our law, so it would please me to not speak of them in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is necessary for two reasons
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one of which is that the doctor should be able to provide an answer when asked, and know the treatment.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other reason is because we often need to castrate some animals for our benefit, such as goats, sheep, cows, and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that castrations are performed in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by traction or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the method we use traction, we make the animal sit in warm water until its testicles are softened and relaxed.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then grasp them with your hand until they are reset and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of circumcision:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you must hold the animal and press its skin with your left hand, then tie the suspension bandage, and cut each testicle with one stroke when you have properly skinned them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave no pouch of the fat nor the subtle fat which lies upon the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than the one done by traction because in that case some part of the testicles may remain, causing the animal to still have sexual desires;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Il sont bestes monstrueus qui ont les deux membres et ont la vertu de copuler comme l’omme et la femme, ce sont por ceu des bestes impures et abominables.
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphrodites occur among men in two ways:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One way is when between the two testicles there appears a structure similar to the female genitalia, where hair grows, and sometimes urine flows out of it.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And this other type [of dislocation] occurs in women, affecting the wrist like a rod and with two knobs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	The treatment for men and women is that you should separate the joined parts completely and then treat them like any other wound.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, for men whose urine escapes through the skin of the testicles, there is no treatment needed.
de la tentigene	Of tensioning.
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A fistula is a joined part on the natural body that is too ugly to look at.
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have them as large as a hand, which is the treatment for it.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must hold the excess of the tendon in your hand or pincers, and cut it lightly.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not cut too deeply, lest blood flow out, then treat the other side until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and in another case where it appears at the mouth of the wound, and fills it; and perhaps falls out, and is similar to cow dung; for this reason the ancients called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	You must cut it off, as we have said with tendonitis, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	Of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic when the woman's nature is not yet pierced or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth or accidental due to illness that has come upon her.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	Where it is fastened by a bandage, or with fine silk thread, or thin metal, and is tied securely in the groin, or on the side, or below, or wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and prevents conception, and childbirth, and perhaps the flow of menstruation.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	And this knowledge is gained by observing the bathing place.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the obstruction is close to the surface, take it with your fingers or a rod.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is secured with fine silk thread, and it is close to the two fingers, be quick, and tie it like this:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread apart;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then stretch the two lips wide apart until the fine silk thread is tight and covers the vulva.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, dampen it in oil, and place it on the site; make the woman lie with her husband each day, so that it cannot heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the wound is hard and thick, you must cut it with a spatula similar to myrtle leaves.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the blockage is made of native wood, suspend it from the ceiling and cover it.
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And have the hemostatic medications ready as needed, such as dragon's blood, incense, along with some egg whites.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then bring an open trough of bronze, wide enough so that the wound cannot heal.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And it should be this way for some time, and bring him a dry linen tent.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat with other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when a tumor develops in the womb, it should be removed in this manner, unless there are embedded abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For the abscess that is embedded in the womb, one should not attempt any treatment involving fire.
des emorroides	Hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood normally escapes, and when hemorrhoids are old they become tumor-like.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have already mentioned in the classification their similarities with other ailments, and the signs, and now I will tell you which ones can be cured.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and hard tumors, when they are perfectly located in the anus and do not protrude, should not be treated with fire.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the mare's [illness], one can feel, are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	You should thus place the woman in a cold house, then stretch the tumor with forceps, and cut it at its roots, then apply powder made of blood-coagulating medicines such as dragon's blood and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then make her stand with her feet against the wall for an hour, then place her in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if there is bleeding, have her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate bark, and galls, and similar things; then take barley flour, mix it with honey and egg white, and apply this poultice to her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops bleeding, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, have him apply cupping glasses to his back and breasts without injury;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take linen, dip it in plantain juice or hawthorn juice mixed with old wine, and apply it to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess is healed, treat the area with an ointment until it is fully recovered.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And the one called "albathir" is red, similar to a harsh head, it should be cut like the teething ring that I mentioned.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is fully recovered.
des apostemes de la marris	Abscesses of the cheek
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscess arise in the cheek, such as cancer, stone-filled abscess, herpes, shingles, fistulas, haemorrhoids and hot abscess, along with numerous other diseases that I have mentioned in my classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is therefore necessary for me to discuss in this treatise the hot abscess that appears on the genitals, which is not among the abscesses that should be lanced.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the work of iron, look to see if the abscess is acute at its onset, full of heat and fever, and becomes red when visible to you.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hasten to pierce, but let it die until the pain subsides;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	And then have the patient sit on a chair, and place two small stools where they can lean, supporting their back and bringing their feet outside the legs;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And have their thighs spread apart, place their arms beneath their knees, and bind them well with a good bandage;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then turn them towards their right side and bring the instrument used to open the joint, which then takes shape;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you go to introduce this instrument, that you first insert the tip in order to know the depth of the wound so that what enters within from the instrument does not go deeper than it should and does not injure the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths so that the instrument does not harm them.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he places the handle of the instrument above and holds the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens, and it is done with the hand softly, it is necessary to cut at its head, or with a spatula gently.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	And when the bowel is empty, you must place into the wound moistened tents in rose oil or in dry green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	place the tent far outside of the wound in front of the orifice, and put on top of the orifice and over the wrist clean linen moistened in water where mallows have been boiled.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it after two days of this treatment until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and every so often irrigate the orifice and wound with enema of water and honey, then with water where white lily roots and long aristoloche have been boiled.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the treatment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is red in the flesh, you must be cautious of applying hot iron, but treat it as we have said in the previous section.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	Mestier est premier a la baile 
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	Then the child must hurry to get out of fire.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	Therefore you know that these births are according to natural position, and the child comes out under its head, with the secondary (midwife) helping it.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	And when you see these signs, you should gently apply pressure on its belly so that the child comes out soon.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	For when it descends onto its head, the secondary helps with it, and the man is rid of his excesses through a good cleansing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	And this one who comes in another way does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes out on its feet, or from the body or shoulder, and with hands, or it comes from the belly, or often, and is turned by chance onto its neck, and in other evil positions.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	If it is necessary at the bath that she should be wise and skilful in these matters, avoiding error and deception, I will show you all the ways in which one must help her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out head first due to natural delivery, and the woman labours intensely during childbirth, and her strength is weak, let them make her sit on a saddle or seat which women hold for her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	And her nourishing broth of oil or fenugreek be boiled, then pour some bathwater between her two hands with the small spatula of this shape:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	And open up the amniotic sac, and cut by her fingernail so that the fluids which are within flow out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	And press on the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must administer an enema to the woman with a mixture of fenugreek and sesame oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her swallow coltsfoot and sneeze, holding her mouth and nose closed for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Now proceed to extract the child.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands appear first, you must gently return them, one at a time.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	And if they cannot enter, place the woman on a chair and lift her feet upwards.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	Then raise the chair from the ground, supporting the woman so she does not fall when rising.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if your hands cannot enter, and the child dies, then cut open their hands with the knife that was mentioned before, extract the child, and reset them evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	At the child's birth from its feet.
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child starts walking on their feet, you must push them upwards.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn it over repeatedly until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then take one of their feet and stretch it again and again.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When they jump up to their thighs, instruct them to grasp it, and make them sneeze frequently.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If jumping happens, may God want it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not jump as we have said, turn it over and over until it is according to its natural form.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will be lightly done.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not happen as we have said, then take mucilage from flax, and oil of lilies, and melted gum, and grind everything together in a mortar.
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and place this ointment on her feminine nature, then have her sit in warm water up to under her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened underneath, make a collar of myrrh for her, and place it beneath her, leaving it there for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on a seat, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose shut, and press gently on her belly, for the child jumps now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	Of the child's exit onto their knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this manner, he puts his hands first forward and then backward.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	Then she should be supported under her neck, with her feet hanging downwards, and let her lie on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and folds his hands back and forth, then he presses his hands on the stomach, and removes the cushions from underneath, until she is aligned downwards;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, take his feet and move them vigorously, then massage his stomach upwards, then put your hands on him.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and rock the child back and forth.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and tell the woman to hold herself as long as the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	Of the child's exit from the broad side, with one hand hanging out.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	I must devise a way to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If one cannot restore it, then make the woman get up and go away.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then have her lie down on the bed and lift her legs vigorously.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then bring forward the poultice I described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if she does not give birth, make her sit on the chair, then help to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	And turn the child according to its natural position, make her sneeze, and instruct her to hold on until the baby comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	Of the child's emergence from its collarbone, let it spread its hands, with its face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary for the midwife to hold her hand, then turn it gently back and forth, and lift the child lightly;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is equalized, place the natural poultice of fat and oil on it, as we have said, then instruct her to move gently back and forth;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on a chair, and instruct her to grasp it.
et la fai esternuer.	make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in this same manner for all secondary dislocations
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out forcefully in this manner on the first attempt, scoop the moisture away with your nail, until it is emptied.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if any of it falls on her face or neck, wipe it off immediately, without delay, and remove the child.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then insert the child, ensuring it is placed correctly, and instruct the woman to hold onto something once.
adonques si istra legierement.	afterwards lift her gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	Of the dislocation of the hips
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII; 
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	And this is not a strange thing, and often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two such things are strange occurrences, and they do not live long if so named.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know these, that they multiply, and are dispersed by the surgeon who divides them, which is connected to the scabbard.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes they emerge naturally just as toes do, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they emerge severely, then the treatment should be as we have described, and the surgeon must be skilled, acting swiftly and lightly in their actions.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	And act accordingly to bring about recovery.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Some are formed in the womb I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or many up to XV, and they are all shaped in the form of a child by the measurement of the glorious sage, and it is necessary that the nurse knows all this, for perhaps similar things happen to him.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	He should do as he ought.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman for a dead child in her womb, as I said in the previous section, and it does not come out easily, and you are forced to perform manual labor;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	It is necessary that you know if the woman has sound virtue and no mishap, or she fears death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	The woman should be positioned on her back with her head inclined downwards, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And the minister holds her down with two parts of his body, or she is tied to the bed so that she cannot move during the child's descent.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the pregnant woman with moist oils, a mixture of alum, fenugreek, and flaxseed, then anoint her stomach with these oils and mixtures.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Gently shake the pregnant woman and place her in a position where she can easily expel the fetus, ensure that it is well-aligned with the birth canal, take care if the child's head has already appeared.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If the child's limbs are entangled in its eyes or neck, mouth, palate, under its beard, clavicle, or near its sides, and if it is descending feet-first, then push with your hand, holding firmly on to their middle and lower ribs.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he must hold the hook with his right hand, and place the curve between the fingers of his left hand, and push gently with all his might, and insert the hook into one of these places that we have mentioned, until it reaches the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the hook:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another hook opposite it, or the third if you need them, so that the extractions are even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch them evenly by moving one way and the other, to take it out, and let the hooks be toothed so as to hold [it], just like this is the shape:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if any part remains inside, anoint the hole with some of his fingers' oil, and push those fingers into that part, then pull out the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if there remains none, then place this sling higher up, and do so until he can pull himself forward with it.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot pull it back due to tightness, then you must wrap a cloth over it until they are both even.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then wrap the cloth around the junction of the palm or wrist, and do likewise for the other hand and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is stuck in the passage or has an acute presentation, then you must insert the sharp-pointed spatula between your fingers, split open the head and extract the fluid.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Ou you la ront a l'estrument qui est apelez "almidach", de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est apres cestui;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	Et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	Et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	Et s'elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	Et s'il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre;
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on their feet, then the traction is light, and the adjustments at the mouth of the womb are slight.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if there is constriction in the belly or chest, it is necessary that you extract it with a cloth wrapped around the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the belly or chest until the moisture within is released;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other member is removed and the head remains, push your hand along its length from above the joint to the mouth of the socket;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then insert one or two fingers and draw them out forcefully;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the socket is narrowed due to hot inflammation that has arisen there, it should not be disturbed but instead softened with moist and greasy things.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and administer plasters, as well as moistening agents in water to soften and moisturize.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is lying on their side, and you can position them evenly, administer what we have mentioned for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	If there is no other option, pull it apart piece by piece, leaving nothing of the caul (membrane) behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, administer what we mentioned for hot abscesses that form in the groin;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	If there is bleeding, apply cold water compresses to restrain it, and provide further treatment as needed.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly a child had been dead, then another was born on top of it, and the other one died as well.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess formed in the jaw, swelling until it burst open, and began to rot (or stink).
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat him, and I thought long about it, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster of strong attraction, and an object came out, seemingly like bone, then after some days another one did too.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly puzzled as to why the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it might be the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I treated the wound, extracting embedded bone fragments until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And the woman lived a long time like this, and there was now a small piece of flesh from that place.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have recorded this chapter only for those who, when the masters find a strange case, may know how to provide assistance.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring back the bone to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	After this comes the form of the pressure bandage, for which we have the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And on page two, at the second head of the second line.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the horns should be more subtle than the restraining device, and they should be made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And the mouth of the wood should be two fingers wide, and the edge of the tree it bites into should be one palm and a half long.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two limbs there should be two joints of this same wood, which are firmly attached to each other, half a palm in length or slightly more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two joints are inserted into the mouth of the socket to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more delicate and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, resembling the shape of pliers.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it has two joints at each end, as you see, one palm in length, and two fingers in width.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see that the socket needs to be opened with all the instruments, have the woman sit off the edge of the bed, her feet hanging down and legs open, then insert the two joints, which are attached together, into the socket, and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the instruments, just as you did with the equal pliers, according to the amount you want to open the mouth of the joint, so that the bail can do what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	This instrument is fully mounted, and its shapes are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when you have these instruments ready, the work is all the more urgent, and it brings greater esteem to men for their skill.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not despair of the instrument which you have prepared, because their need is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained in childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze vigorously, and keep your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she succeeds with this, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and make a hole in the lid, putting into it herbs that can open the pores of the skin as gently as possible: rue, anise, chamomile, wormwood and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs or some of them should be boiled in water inside the pot over fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then put one end of the tube or hole from the pot into the patient's mouth and the other towards their nose, holding it so that the steam enters the patient.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make them sneeze as we have said before.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the injury is caused by a fall.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	If it remains after this treatment and does not work, command the nurse to wet her left hand with oil of sesame or muskroot juice, then put it inside the patient's anus and massage it; she must also check the womb.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, then grasp it and extend it little by little straight, so that the husband does not suffer during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it must be moved lightly to the right and left, and then pulled.
si venra et se desaerdra.	then it will come out and dislodge itself.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the husband's throat is narrowed, we have mentioned the cure of sneezing and herbal fumigation;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not respond to all that we have said, take care that you do not rush when pulling it out;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is at the husband's throat be bound to the wife's thigh and enema her with ointment of four-fold composition.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If there is inflammation and it returns afterwards, you must treat it again.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But nevertheless, when inflammation occurs and it leads to foul smell in the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	It is necessary then to use suitable fumigations for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the ancients have tested fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one fumigates a woman to retain her flowers and second-course is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it should be similar to the appearance of a dog's head, with the subtle parts placed above in nature, and the larger parts over the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	The fumigation should be above the coals, and let it last as long as is necessary, then start another one anew.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament.
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without an open anus; instead, it is sealed by a subtle membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary for the nurse to pierce this membrane with her finger, and not use a sharp spatula, being careful not to harm the child.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place soft wool soaked in wine and oil on it, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, insert a plank peg into the hole, and leave it there for several days; remove it when the child wants to go outdoors.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this sealing occurs suddenly due to a wound or abscess.
si covient coper celui soudement:	It is necessary to cut through this sudden sealing.
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	Treat it as described for the anus of a newborn.
de la fistule dou fondement	From the anal fistula.
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when this old dislocation heals, it forms a white or subtle scar, and sometimes these are piercing fistulas;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they are recognized by those who have experienced it through evacuation or flatulence when the patient evacuates, and sometimes a worm jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that penetrate up to the bladder, and up to halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they reach up to the hip joint, and up to the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a piercing fistula in the anus, but not a non-piercing one:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and that you insert your index finger into the anus, and gently push a thin needle made of brass or iron into the fistula if it is not twisted.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it is twisted, insert a slender probe made of lead or horsehair until you feel the probe or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge of pus or air nor a visible wound as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not perforate;
si te haste dou curer.	then hasten to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula pierces through to the bladder or the urine passage, it leaks urine, and cannot be healed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is perforated up to the hip joint, then the probe has reached its destination.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twist and the pain is around that area, then it is likely in a curved section of the intestine, and neither medication nor immediate treatment through poultices are effective.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And for these persistent fistulas, there is no cure but toil, and the foolish pride of surgeons who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In that which is not persistent and not ancient, there is hope for healing with iron, as I have proven, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And lift their legs up to their thighs, and have their thighs inclined towards their belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert a tent of iron, or brass if there is torsion, until you know where the tip lies.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around their anus, then you must insert your index finger, and when you feel that the tent has pierced [the fistula];
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And if it is uncovered where you feel a fissure or flesh, then know that it is Persian.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If it is not worked on, one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One says nevertheless that they may be well healed, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And the treatment one applies is to heat the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as it has been said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	And place all of the hot [tool] into the fistula until it reaches its base.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	Do this twice or thrice until you know that these faulty tissues are burned, which resembles a bird's feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat wet bandages with butter until all moisture has left, then treat the ointment by drawing out matter and sealing it together.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healed, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this, no other way can be healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent enters, and does not pierce all the way through to the right side of the anus, and between your finger and the tent is a thick layer of flesh or sinew, and you see the fistula at that which sews together the covering from within;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	then cut off the beginning of the fistula, and push it back before the tent, and then cauterize after, until you reach the head of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent will be released, and fall out.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then avoid those damaged parts that look like a bird's feather, leaving them untouched.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if blood rushes into you and comes between your body and the work, cauterize it with fire or with medicated paste.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For fire cauterization combines two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these damaged parts and the stemming of blood flow along with drying out moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat wet wounds with butter or ground substances until the skin turns pale, and remove burnt flesh from the wound.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat open sores with soothing ointments for hardened skin, using dry medications.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For once it is reset, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes right up to the anus, and is away from the body, put your finger in the anus and ask the patient.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you notice the wound and there is either skin, membrane, or flesh between two parts that are about to break through, with no apparent way out and little hope, then administer one of the three methods below:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	where you cauterize as we have said, or you cut to the bottom, or if you can, apply tents and treat it as first described;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, lest you cut the membrane that holds the foundation and cause involuntary evacuation.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perhaps it will be ulcerated, so you remove the covering and clean it once cut near the foundation, either with a tent or another pointed instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then remove that faulty flesh which is in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then consider restoring the wound and removing the fistula from the part outside of the foundation.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it were a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes they form fistulas in this way:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert the tube into the fistula, and it is near the fundament next to the skin above, take a perforated tube with this shape:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	...and insert the thread awry into it in II, and pierce the tent with the thread into the fistula until its head is reached.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pierced in the margin of the fundament inside, then remove the wire from that perforation, just as you would insert your finger into the fundament;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	And pull the ends of the wire together, bringing the two sides into contact, and clamp them tightly to each other, leaving it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And clamp it periodically until the wire cuts through the flesh between them, allowing drainage;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is sealed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not rupture, make it burst in every way you can if it is not too deeply embedded.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not suitable to treat a wound that deeply embedded with cauterization; and then you must cure it as we have said until it heals.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spinal needle used to make the fistula is very sharp and pointed on one side, and serrated on the other.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	On the other side it is not sharp because we do not want to cut what should not be cut, as you can see here:
des emorroydes	For haemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Hemorrhoids are of two types:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	They are found inside the anus like small grains of resin, and they can be small or large, with some containing blood, and there may be one or several. They also protrude outside the anus and at its opening.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those which are deficient have little moisture, and also here or a little yellow water or a little blood, and they have the colour of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them inside the rectum is that you instruct the patient to strain when going to the bathroom until the faeces exit and the object appears.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, grab it with forceps or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the forceps cannot hold them due to moisture, grasp them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of chamois.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	Pull them out with your hands, then cut it, and sprinkle some hot powder on top as a caustic agent.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Where you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat other treatments until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundation cannot come out, administer to the patient a biting and harsh enema to wash what is in the fundament, so that it may exit clearly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	When the patient asks, and if the filament is forced out of the fundament, then the treatment is light.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grasp them with your nail or with pincers and cut them off, then treat them as we have said until they are healed, and be wary of cutting with a blade.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	Thus it is appropriate that you apply the suture in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread, and pass it through a needle, then draw the thread up and pierce the needle from the other side, turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let them hang loose.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	Hold the thread tightly, then tie a knot in it, remove the needle, and do this for all of them, leaving one to draw out any excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Place on the bottom a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or wax, and put it over the wound, then instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Leave it in place until the poultices fall off, and once they do, treat with ointment and other remedies until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	By drying out of faeces from the bowel/rectum.
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is drying out of faeces in the intestine, due to constraint by natural forces and when illness is longstanding and does not respond to treatment.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You must remove the bark with the tip of your spatula or nail, making sure it doesn't get wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then treat it until it is firm as needed.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot heal, begin the rasping again more vigorously than before until it bleeds a lot and becomes raw.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	From swelling.
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A fistula is a small faulty appearance between the body, which goes deep inside.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes it goes numb, and one feels it like a dead limb due to the tremors, spreading throughout the body, mostly in the hands more than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is such that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a strong vulture's feather, and place this quill onto the trembling, so that the purple circles touch the trembling all around;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand over the entire quill so that you cup it all around the trembling, and put it in perfectly, and eradicate the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit, make such a cane from copper or iron according to this form, and let it be thin below and thick above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce at all, but hold it with your finger, and press it firmly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see fit, then cauterize the trembling, as it is described in the previous chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	Of the form of the clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes an argentum, or arquus, or molten iron alloy is made into a clyster.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And sometimes one makes these instruments small and large, according to what they are adapted for.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those which we adapt for the treatment of children and those who are weak and full of pain are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and great clyster is thus broadly as follows: the bellies are tied according to this manner
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is an opening or the belly is tied like this, as you see, and the head is pierced inside;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	And has one side with two holes, and on the other side, one hole.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let the belly where one places the medicines be made of an animal bladder or parchment, and pierced all around with small holes, and have one finger's width between each hole, then thread into these holes a strong twine woven in a crisscross pattern like an X or tied tightly around it, and sew together the belly as if it were a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the physician is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then clyster.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the shape of the circle;
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the physician not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the clyster with oil or egg white, or something similar, then gently insert it;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then grasp the ministers with both hands together until it is completely visible, then remove the clyster and lift the patient's legs against the wall, and if the physician wants to exit, hold them as much as possible;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps for an entire night nearby, it is even greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you give him an enema for a bellyache, and the medicament comes out quickly, repeat it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the haemorrhoids are either on the anus or abscess, let the clyster be as subtle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtle clyster, upon which the skin is stretched:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already spoken about the treatment of wounds in the previous section;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	and we shall tell you the treatments of hands and medicine, according to their practice.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what has caused them, where they have been inflicted, and by which means.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by the striking of stones, and cutting by sword or knife, or by lance or stick or arrow, or by similar objects;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or by the location of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or on the head, or the foot, or the belly, or the liver, and similar parts;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, beginning with simple head wounds, since their memory will return in its own chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound occurs on the head, and the bone is not broken, take care if it is due to a blow from a rock or similar object, and the skin is still torn and the wound is large, and you slightly suspect hot abscess.
