si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	then make it bleed a little with the cerebral artery, especially if only a small amount of blood comes from the wound, and let the bleeding be on the opposite side of the injury.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and purge the patient of fullness from wine and fatty meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if they do not wish to bleed, their meat intake should be reduced, and they should refrain from drinking wine or eating meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place on the wound, if a hot abscess appears there, cotton moistened with rose oil only, or in styptic wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, apply on the wound, if it is fresh and full of blood, and has not been moved by air, a powder which I will mention shortly afterwards;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the air has moved it, apply some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	Et if the wound is large like that of a sword cut or similar, and the lips cannot be brought together with stitches, then bring them together by sewing, as I will explain for wounds in the belly, regarding suturing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound exposes the bone, is gaping, and only hangs by a small piece of flesh, then cut it off.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medication and restore hard flesh in place of leather, and instruct the patient to eat coarse meat, such as beef and wheat pudding, as well as poultry, and similar foods.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find skin with a rash that does not reach the bone, then cut out all of the affected area, discard it and then treat [the wound].
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or incision that does not stop bleeding and cannot be staunched with medicine, then seek out the artery and if you find it severed, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not bring benefit, then cauterize [the wound].
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if these wounds are small and simple, their treatment is also light [and straightforward]:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	It matters that you put this powder in, which seals [the wound] instead of letting it heal on its own.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And the manner of preparing this powder is as follows:
pren encens une partie;	Take frankincense, one part;
sanc de dragon II parties;	dragon's blood (resin), two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	quicklime (calcium oxide), three parts, and finely mix the powder, then apply it to the wound, pressing it firmly, until it dries completely and seals with all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	bind it well, and leave it untouched without unbinding it, if there is no swelling;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	for the medicine should not be removed until healing has taken place.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And at times one uses only lime [calcium oxide] when there is no frankincense or dragon's blood available, but the art has healed the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the burn had caused the wound to die, especially inside (the body), do not use this powder there at all;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some digestive ointments, or poultices made of barley flour with water and honey until it becomes soft;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat him with other treatments until he is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the bone fracture occurs with the wound, and it is small, extract it with fine pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about skull fractures hereafter.
de la plaie dou col	of the neck wound.
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound occurs on the neck and it is straightforward, there is no distinction between this and a head injury; however, if the carotid artery or the jugular vein in the neck has been severed, this is critical.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the brain, there is no other treatment besides letting it heal, and do not apply anything constricting, for it harms the brain and causes it to retract.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not apply anything cold to the wound, for the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuity is with the brain, which is the highest organ.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	but let the medicine be washed in warm water sweetened with rose oil, and cooked cabbage also washed in sweet water, and other stones of salt according to this way, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, cut it and bind it with bandages, then treat it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep, and it is covered with hair and full of bowels, then pierce it in a lower place.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is severed, and blood flows out, then uncover it, tie it off, and cauterize it if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	and if the windpipe of the throat is severed, or the heart, and breathing is maintained, as the flesh still lives, then cut the heart above the neck of the throat, and do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then restrain it carefully, leaving it for a few days, then treat it with draining ointments until it is healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	And if the wound has penetrated into the bone, treat it with cautery.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	If there are bone fragments, remove them forcefully if you can, and for those you cannot reach, leave it to let the wound rot, and ease the discharge.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle it with the powder I mentioned earlier.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound with a fistula, treat it as I have described in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	Of the wound from a lance or knife.
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it is a wound from a spear or knife, and the injury is deep, observe whether air escapes as the patient breathes in.
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	Know then that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And if it is not deep, and fresh with all its blood, do not apply the powder in the first hour, nor bind it to stop the blood from escaping entirely, and returning to the heart, which would kill the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	But apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	And if you have no ointment, then place old cotton in the wound to draw out the moisture, and make the patient sleep on the wound for three days, or four, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	And there will come no spasm, nor harmful trembling of the heart or breathlessness;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good signs, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat it then with tents and other remedies until it is cleansed.
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	And if it cannot be healed, and the wound persists, then know that there is a fistula present.
si la cure si com on doit.	So treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife incision, be it on the chest, arm, or back, treat as per the front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	If it is large, suture it.
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	And if it is small, treat with powder, and if it has penetrated the bone or broken into pieces, clean the wound, and realign any displaced parts.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not removed, let the wound fester, it will relieve the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds on different limbs, the judgment is the same as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	Rupture of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the abdomen are large, medium, and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From the large wound, sometimes the intestines or the nerves of the intestines protrude, leading to the introduction of others.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	The suturing is more difficult, and sometimes the small wound causes more trouble than the large one, because one must put back the intestines more carefully, unless they are placed back step by step.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Because the intestines swell sometimes when they feel cold, so they retract more tightly, and thus the medium-sized wound is preferred, because one must put back the intestine to its place rather than the other parts of the abdomen.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And know that a rupture of the belly occurs according to four manners:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	the two common sutures occur in the suture of the belly, and the suture of other wounds of the body, and two other proper sutures are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	and nevertheless they are more specific with the suture of the belly, and I shall say each one and explain.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small, and a part of the intestine comes out, and it is difficult to replace, this can be done through one of two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or due to the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestine is swollen from the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it in such a manner:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	Moisten a sponge or soft cloth with warm water only, or cook it in water infused with vinegar and spice, then apply to the intestine until the swelling is reduced.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And having made this constricting wine, it becomes mature under the sun to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the swelling start to subside, dampen the intestine with water or other soft cloths that have been cooked in malves, for by this method it is alleviated of much discomfort.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, then make a small incision in the wound with an instrument used for cutting haemorrhoids.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	and the first treatment is to close the wound by cutting it so one must not cut unless there is a great need for it.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument to open it with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	when cutting inside along its curve and not outside, and see here the shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines have come out, then replace them carefully according to their natural form into their proper place, if you are able, for this is better.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is wide and it is located in the lower part of the abdomen, one must lay the patient on their back and elevate their legs higher than their head.
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	And if the wound is in the upper part of the abdomen, place the head and chest higher than the lower parts; also, when the abdominal rupture occurs on one side or another, position the patient so that the affected part is higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus you must manage what I say for large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds, use what has been provided to you, take it in your hands and carefully apply a gentle medication that covers the entire wound, bringing its edges together.
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	This is the common method for stitching: take a needle or multiple needles according to the width of the wound and leave two inches at the tip of the wound before threading it with strong thread.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	Pierce the two sides of the skin with two ends of the siphac, which is beneath the skin on the inside, so that you make it pierce through from this part, and bring together the two ends of the siphac in a group of four.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	then strain a double thread around the needle in two parts, then bring together the two sides of the wound appropriately, and then leave one finger's width, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle, and do not stop until all needles are tied according to your need, until the entire wound is closed.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	and let the needles be medium-sized, between fine and thick, for the fine ones cut through all the flesh, while the very thick ones cannot enter properly.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	hence it is necessary that they be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	and one should not insert the needles too far beyond the flesh and skin, lest they cut and open the wound before it is sutured.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and then cut the skin around the needles so they do not wound the patient while sleeping, and place tents or bandages over the needle sites to hold them in place, leaving them there until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	This method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds because it only requires one or two needles.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second type of suture is common, and it involves gathering together the two sides of the skin and the two sides of the subcutaneous tissue with one needle or a strong medium-sized thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	And when you have pierced these four sides together, draw the needle back to the starting point, like one would sew fabric.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a space between each stitch equal to the thickness of a thumb.
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	these stitches will be used by the man, and I sewed a wound that a horse had on its belly, which was pierced by a knife, and the wound was larger than a palm, with the intestines protruding by two palms, and the wound was in the middle of the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	I returned his intestine after it had been outside for twenty-four hours, and the wound was healed up to fifteen days, I treated him, and he was cured.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And the doctor had judged that he would die, but it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat it with ointment, as I was in a place where none could be found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I placed old cotton on the wound twice a day, and washed it with water and honey until it was healed.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	Now I shall tell you of the two proper methods of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and push it from outside to inside through the wound;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	When it has pierced the heart from right to left, leave the tip of the needle where the vessel rests or pierces where you have pushed the needle through, and make it go through again from inside to outside.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And the method of this suturing is that you sew it like a peltier sews furs, leaving one vessel on one side and taking it up again from another, until the entire suture is complete.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	The second method of suturing, as Galen describes it properly, is done by bringing the two edges together naturally and pressing one tip of the vessel onto another in such a manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	Insert a needle at the base of the nose, and pierce that place only, leaving two holes on either side.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	Then turn the needle, and pierce it outward from that place until you reach inside, at the two holes on either side.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Pierce one and then the other outward from that place until you reach inside, at two more holes of the nose which are on the opposite side.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the modern method, and the most common way of suturing.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	Galen said this word, and many witness that one must suture the belly with two needles, having thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and you must pass one needle from one side to another, like those who sew leather straps;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	and know that when the rupture is in the middle of the belly, the suture is more grievous than those of other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments about the wound are such as the judgments about other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	and it is that when you find the wound fresh with all its blood, rather than let it dry out, you should replace the intestine and sew up the wound.
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	then apply the powder of burning flesh, and if it has dried out, then put some ointment that is appropriate until the wound heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	Tie the thread, and let the eyelids and eyebrows fuse together.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as you would others, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And if you don't have medicine, apply old cotton wool to it as soon as it begins to drain pus, and move it twice daily until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	Because you don't need any other medicine in many instances when the wounds are simple.
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	And if you suspect that the wound might cause the main limbs to become infected, you must dampen a light linen cloth with lukewarm oil or rosehip oil, and place it around the groin and under the armpits.
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	and if he feels pain or inflammation in the bowels, and it happens often, then cleanse them with a clister of red wine, especially if the inflammation has reached the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and pierce it from within, knowing that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to treat than the small one.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	The intestine which is called 'jeun' cannot be healed when it is wounded, and this is due to the fragility of its veins, and because of the delicacy of the whole body, and the proximity of its nature to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the belly button falls out of the wound, put it back in as with the intestine, while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	and if it is old and has turned worms or black, you must tie the spot that has gone black to prevent bleeding as there are veins and arteries there;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	then cut what is between the tie, and hang the two navels from beneath the wound outwards to ease its extraction when the belly button falls, and the wound heals.
de la routure dou boueil	On the rupture of the mouth
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	When the intestines are round and the wound is small, one can restore it in some men, for I saw a man who was wounded in the belly by a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach, and it became inflamed and turned into a fistula, from which excretions and gas came out;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated it according to my ability, and I did not cease to clean it until he was healed, and the wound closed up.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it healed, I suspected that the patient might have an ailment in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no illness there, but he remained in better health, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and certain experimenters say that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it must be bound in such a manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie, et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les II levres, si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	take coarse thread from large gut, then gather the lips of the wound together, and when the thread has opened its mouth, put it on both lips so that it tightens their mouths above.
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier, puis met I autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then cut the head of the thread and leave it so that it cannot be untied, then put another piece of thread afterwards in this same manner as before, until the wound is completely bound.
et cout la plaie.	and cut the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide, et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste, en teil maniere:	These stitches adhere in the intestine, and there is no harm to the patient, and if you want to sew up an intestine with a fine thread that is cut from the intestine of an animal, do it this way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez, et puis lie au chief de cest fil I fil de lin subtil tort, puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Take the end of this gut string, which should be very thin, then tie to its end a fine linen thread, then pass the thread through the needle and sew up the gut, then pull it back over the tear.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this way of sewing, it is not false, only according to the path of faith and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the intestinal bowels, there is no cure or health, only skillfulness.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a fistula wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	Know that any wound or abscess, when it heals, is universally called a "fistula", especially when it is healed and bowed inwards.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor, et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And a fistula is truly a false knotting that is hard and white, where there is no pain felt, and it also has hair like the feather of a bird.
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes it leaps clear, and other times dense.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes little, and others enough.
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char, ce n’est fuers que par une des VIIII causes:	and I have spoken of it in the division of wounds, that any wound that is not healed, and there is no flesh, this is true only for one of nine causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	that is to say, due to the scantiness of blood or pus;
ou por sa malice;	or because of its nature;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or due to the hard flesh within it, and on its lips, which does not allow new flesh to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or because there is too much corruption [putrefaction];
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	Where there are sores and the substance is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	where the medication is not effective in treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	where due to this, the corruption is like a plague;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	where due to the properties of the region, digestion is slow, healing takes time, and it swells naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	where there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, signs, and treatments with remedies in the section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I must inform you of the treatment for fistula, which is performed by manual operation.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas occur in any part of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners, ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes, ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	for there are fistulas that affect the large veins, arteries, nerves, anus, intestine, bladder, sides of the body, spine, or any joint in the hands and feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if there is any return to the property of the main member, and its similar places.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that are of this nature are difficult to cure, there is nothing but work [to do] and ignorance.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure, et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and if there is any fistula that does not reach the level I have mentioned, and you are confident of the treatment, and you know how to identify it, then take a tent of linen or iron, if the fistula is straight, make an incision.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc, car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	and if the fistula is twisted, then search for it with a thin tent of lead, because the lead can bend and move along the twisting.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes, si la clisterize par l’un des pertus, car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	and if the fistula has multiple openings and you cannot locate it well with tents, then cleanse it by clisterizing through one of the openings, as moisture flows from one opening to another, thus cleaning it.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont, et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	Then carefully examine it as best you can to determine if there is bone or nerve involved, and whether the injury is complete or not, and ask the patient well about the pain he feels when you press with your hand, and where exactly he feels this pain.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine, ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit, et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	And when you have truly located where it is, whether it is close to a joint, nerve, artery or vein, or any of the places I mentioned, treat it accordingly as I told you, and remove whatever is damaged and corrupt within.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee, et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues, puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule, tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	Then cure it until it is healthy, and if the fistula is deep in the right spot, you must treat it perfectly, as much as you can, then place moistened bandages soaked in healing ointment, pushing them inside until the tip of the fistula, so that the medicine corrodes any excess remaining at the bottom.
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then I apply invigorating ointments to healthy flesh until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit, et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if it is not healed by this, then cauterize as we have said, and if the bone is corrupted by the fistula, cut it out.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If the wound or inflammation does not burden your principal limbs as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee, puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if the bone is exposed, and there is corruption and blackening, cut away until all corruption is removed, then treat it with invigorating substances until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant, saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	And if it is not healed, and bends backward as before, know that you have not gone deep enough:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons, et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	If it is uncovered and searched thoroughly until you reach the bottom, remove all the decayed matter, then reset its position.
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it is healed in this way, it is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the decayed matter has penetrated too deeply, and you cannot reach it.
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	If there is another instrument left by nature.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles, si l’estrai a I estrument covenauble a ceu, et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	And if there is a small decayed bone that you can extract with pincers, remove it with the suitable instrument for this purpose. If there are multiple bones, remove them all together, leaving none behind.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour, si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	And if moisture prevents you from continuing without any errors or fear, cut away the moisture and flesh, and free the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture, et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os, et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And if you cannot remove them in an hour, apply something that causes suppuration to the wound and leave it until all the flesh is rotten around the bone. Then they will be able to extract the bones more easily.
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse, si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee, puis restoure la plaie;	And if it is a large bone, such as from the leg or thigh, treat only the suppuration until all discoloration has disappeared and then redress the wound.
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if a large part of it has become suppurated, and reaches the bone marrow;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	It must be cauterized and cut until all suppuration is removed, then treat it until it is healed.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint I home en sa jambe, si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	And I will tell you about a fistula that occurred in a man's leg so that you may take example from it and apply it to your work.
Il fut I jovencelz entor XXX ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors, tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	He was a young man of about thirty years old, who had pain in his leg due to an internal cause, such that the matter came up into the leg, and it swelled with a large abscess, and there was no external reason to open [it].
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri, et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	But the doctors, in their folly, worked on it so much that the abscess opened up and a lot of matter flowed out, becoming a fistula, and there came forth many discharges which threw out all bowel contents and moisture from the body;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor II ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains, tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit, et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	And many doctors put him through various treatments for about two years, and there was no wise person in the art of medicine, until I was called upon, and I examined his leg and the medicines they were using to treat it, and saw what was flowing out from the openings in great quantity. 
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And the young man's body became red, and he had a yellow complexion.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus, et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	I set up a tent in one of these holes, and then examined all the holes, and found that one came against the other from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os, et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	So I hurried and cut into one of the openings until I exposed part of the bone, and I found it corrupted and perforated, with the corruption reaching deep inside to the bone.
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I scraped away what appeared to be the corrupted part of the bone and believed there was no other corruption beyond what I removed.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And I began to treat the wound with soft medicine over a long period of time, but it could not heal.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant, et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	Then I started again and exposed the bone as before, finding that the corruption had spread into it. I scraped it away, then removed it, and tried in vain to close the wound.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole, puis le restourai de medicines;	but I could not cut around one palm's width of bone, and it remained stuck to all its soft tissue, then I treated it with medicine;
et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment, et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir, et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and it was quickly healed and fused, and there was no need to start the work again except for the patient's weakness, who could not endure more, and because of my fear of his death.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement, et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	For the evacuation, he often bled, but he was completely healed, and in place of the bone, a hard tissue grew, and it had good consistency and caused no harm or damage whatsoever, neither going nor coming.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if any bone in the body is broken, it should be treated in this way:
pren I liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert, et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	take a bandage, and bind the head of the bone that protrudes, and instruct someone to pull it upwards;
et met I autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os, et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz, et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and place another thicker bandage made of wool on the flesh that is above the bone, and extend the head (of the protruding bone), so that you pull away the corrupted flesh beneath, and uncover the flesh over the location where you wish to operate, ensuring that it does not cut into the flesh;
et met I tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And place a hot iron or a table beneath the bone to cut away the corrupted flesh.
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	One must be very careful to see and feel where the corruption is, and check again thoroughly.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie, si descuevre la char toute;	And if the bone is corrupted but does not break open, and the corruption lies either in the middle or on one side, expose all the flesh.
puis met I tison desoz, et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption I poc, si com nos avons dit;	Then place the hot iron underneath [the wound] and cauterise from one side to the other over the entire length of the corruption with a probe as we have said.
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	And if the corruption is in the joint, cut away the corrupted joint [surface], and cauterise the bone on its other side.
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des II jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	and if the corruption is located between two joints, there is no other option but to cut it out.
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose, mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	and if the corruption is in the wrist of the hand or the ankle of the foot, it is indeed very severe, yet you must still inquire about this corrosion, how it presents itself to you.
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	purify it in every way possible, but make sure that neither the vein nor the nerve oppose you.
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous, et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	know that there are many types of incisor tools and saws for cutting these bones, depending on the arrangement of the bones, their appearance, thickness, subtlety, size, smallness, and hardness.
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	and for this it is necessary to match each type of operation with its appropriate instrument.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art, et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	And know that your work will show you the instrument you need, according to the knowledge of this art and the signs of different illnesses.
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	If you think about the instrument you need according to its purpose.
dou feu	Of fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The head can be affected internally or externally;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie, si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient, si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	And when you have treated that injury with medicine and it doesn't heal, then you must amputate the limb up to where the corrosion begins so that the patient may escape death or the evil consequence of losing a limb.
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu, et porrist aprés la noiror, pues va celle corrosions de membre em membre, et prent par tout le cors;	And the signs are that the limb turns black as if burnt by fire and then after the blackness it spreads from limb to limb taking over the whole body.
si te haste dou coper, et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans, se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	If you hurry to cut it, and if it is due to the sting of venomous beasts, such as a scorpion or snake, and the corrosion is on the top of your arm, then cut it, but do not give it time to reach the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it has reached the hand, cut it at the joint so that the corrosion does not extend to the arm.
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute;	And if it reaches the arm, then cut it with a knife.
et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors, et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	If it passes the knife, then it is death, and no strong remedy will save them except for quantities of its virtue.
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet:	And do likewise when the corrosion comes to the foot:
s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	If it comes to the first joint, then cover it after the other joint.
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	And if it happens on the foot, then cover the whole foot.
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	And if it ascends to the leg, then cover at the knee joint.
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	And if it goes above the knee, there is no other option but to let the patient die.
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz, et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont, et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les II liiens a I spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	The method of covering or binding the limb is that you tie it above and below, and have some ministers pull on one of the bindings downwards while others pull on the other binding upwards, and you cut away the flesh that lies between the two bindings with a spatula that is wide enough to expose the bone.
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part I drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain, et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	Then cover it with cotton or silk, and place a linen cloth on each side so that the silk does not touch the healthy area, preventing further injury and an abscess from forming in the patient.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment, ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans;	And if bleeding occurs while you operate, cauterize the area immediately or apply some hemostatic powders.
puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie, puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then return to your medical treatment until it is completed, then bind the injured limb with a suitable bandage and treat it until it is healed.
et je te conterai k’il avint a I home en som piet:	and I will tell you what happened to the man with a wounded foot:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu, et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	He had a blackened wound that looked like a burn from fire, and this corrosion started on his big toe, spreading across the entire foot.
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	and when the man saw the corrosion, he rushed to cut off his foot, and was healed.
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi, et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	and long after, the corrosion returned to his thumb, and he came to me, and I applied resonant substances to it after purifying his body, but could not stop the corrosion.
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	and he saw that I had to cut off his hand, but I did not want to, as I hoped to reverberate the matter.
et doutai ausi que se je tailloie sa main, qu’il ne morist, car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible;	and I also doubted that if I amputated his hand, he would die, because the man's health was weak.
et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre, et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	and he became desperate, returned home, and hurried to cut off his own hand, and was healed.
et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	And I have not included cases where it is done otherwise, if one needs to do so.
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	There is no instance where an abscess forms in the flesh and remains for so long that it creates a large accumulation of pus;
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	And then it hardens and ruptures, discharging the pus which remains visible in the wound, just like a vessel;
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com I drapelz deliiez, et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain», et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	The skin above is as thin as delicate cloth, and does not extend to the bone or nerve; such a condition is called a "sinus" and is not known as a "fistula";
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	But if it extends all the way to the bone in depth, then it is called a "fistula";
et li cuire si est que tu cope celui cuir tout entor, et meismement quant il est subtilz, ausi com uns drapelz;	and the skin is such that you cut this skin all around it, especially when it is delicate, just like a piece of cloth.
et ne s’aert mie por sa corruption.	and it does not matter for its corruption.
Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont, et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	And if you are worried that the skin will rot, and the decay is not complete, and the skin is thick with flesh, then clean it thus with a clyster:
regarde se li seins est grans, et li bowe qui en ist est de puant odor, adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	check if the breasts are large, and the bowels that are inside emit a foul odour, then clysterise with Egyptian medicine which is made thus:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en I vassel au feu, tant que li medicine soit rouge, et deviegne ausi espesse com miel;	take equal parts quicklime, oil, and litharge, and cook them in a vessel over the fire until the medicine turns red and becomes as thick as honey;
et puis pren de ceu selonc ta necessiteit, et le font en aigue et en miel, et en clisterize lou sein, et estraint le pertus;	And then take according to your need, mix it with water and honey, and use it as an enema for the breast, holding the opening tight.
et laisse la medicine ens par II houres, puis l’estrai en espreignant;	Leave the medication there for two hours, then remove it by feeling around.
fai ce mout de fois, tant que li seins soit mondefiiez, et soit ostee li puor;	Do this several times until the breast is softened, and remove the pus.
et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres, quant ceste medicine n’est presens, et est que tu preignes cendres de fust de vigne, et giete aigue desus, puis la coule, et en clisterize, tant que tu saiches que li seins est bien mondez;	And sometimes you can use an enema of ash water if this medication is not available. Take ashes from grapewood and pour water over them, then strain it, and use it as an enema until you know the breast is well softened.
et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres, si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	And if the patient cannot tolerate it, neither Egyptian medication nor ash water, then use an enema of water and honey where there is a bit of powdered litharge.
ou tu la clistirize de miel et de vin melleit, que li mielz ait proprieteit de mundifiier et de laver, et li vins fait aerdre le sain;	where you cleanse it with honey and mixed wine, for honey has the property to purify and wash, and wine causes the blood to rise.
et quant tu as ce fait, et tu as fiance que li seins est bien mundifiiez, si le clisterize de ceu que fait naistre char en li, et est que tu preignes emplaustre diafinit, et le font avec oile roset et en vin;	and when you have done this, and you are certain that the wound is well cleansed, then cleanse it with what makes flesh grow in it, and take definitive cataplasm, and make it with rose oil and wine;
ou tu le clisterize d’aucunes medicines et d’oignemens, dont j’ai dit les proprietez ou traitier des oignemens;	where you cleanse it with some medicines and ointments, of which I have spoken about their properties in the treatise on ointments;
et se li pertus dou sein est petis, et li cainne dou clistere n’i puet entrer, si l’eslarge d’un fer un poc, et met ens une tente de l’oignement egiptiein, ou oignement basilicon, tant k’il soit eslargiez;	and if the wound of the breast is small, and the cane of the enema cannot enter, then enlarge it with an iron rod a little, and put in a bit of Egyptian ointment or Basilican ointment until it is enlarged;
et se li plaie est trop large, si la cout et i laisse tant soulement I leu ou li clistere puisse entrer, et se li pertus que giete bowe est au desus, si le cope ou plus bas leu que i est.	And if the wound is too wide, cut it and leave only enough space for the clyster to enter, and if the opening that emits excrement is above, then close or cover it at a lower place where it is located.
Car quant li bowe est en parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char;	For when the bowels are perforated, it does not allow food to pass through.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues, si appareille en tel maniere que li bowe corre au plus bas leu que i est, car quant li bowe est parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues, si apareille en teil maniere:	And if you cannot cut the skin below as you wish, prepare it in such a way that the bowels are directed to the lowest place they can be, for when the bowels are perforated, it does not allow food to pass through and if you cannot cut the skin below as you wish, prepare it in this manner:
que li bowe corre legierement aval, et n’i lassier rien de la bowe;	That the bowels flow slightly downwards, and leave nothing of the bowels behind;
et pren medicines consolidatives por mettre sor le sain, et estent sus I drapeil de lin que cuevre tout le sain;	and take consolidating medicine to put on the wound, and extend it onto a linen cloth that covers the entire wound.
puis cope as forces endroit le pertus dou sein I poc plus large dou premier, pues estent oignement souef sus I autre drapel selonc la quantiteit dou pertus, et le met sus le pertus dou sain por aligier la bowe, et n’oster mie le grant drapeil fuers que aprés maint jor une fois;	then cover as much of the surrounding area as possible with a hole in the center larger than the original one, then extend ointment on another linen cloth according to the size of the wound and place it over the injury to ease swelling. Do not remove the large outer bandage for several days.
et celui qui est sor le pertus dou sein, oste sovent por oster la bowe, et saiches ceu que corra de la bowe, se c’est venin ou poc ou assez, ou digeste, ou indigeste;	and the one on top of the wound, remove it often to reduce swelling and wipe away any discharge. Examine what comes from this swelling - is it poison or pus or just a lot of fluid, or is it digestible or undigestable?
et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non, et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sain, si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	and take note if the patient experiences pain and whether there is an abscess or not. Once your medicine has been applied in this way and you observe what emerges from the wound, know that the tissue is healing and bring the patient closer to health.
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie, si chainge I autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	Then you must release it in the morning or on the third day, and when you untie the wound, change to another cloth, and renew the ointment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if the breast ejects undigested food after many days, know that the breast is not healthy.
Et se venins subtilz cort aprés lonc tens, si ne te desperer mie de la santeit, car li santez aproche.	And if subtle venom emerges after a long time, do not despair of health, for healing is approaching.
Car il i a homes cui tarde enjanremens de char en ses plaies, et de ces que font le contraire;	For there are men who heal slowly in their wounds, and those who act contrary to this;
et se bowe indigeste saut dou sein aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie;	and if the bowels remain undigested after many days, you should know that this breast has not healed;
et se li seins tarde d’aerdre, et est porloigniez, si ajoste medicines sechans moistes en substance et seches en vertut, si com oignement diafinit, car il i a grant partie de vitriole, et c’est li derriene medicine;	and if the breast heals slowly and is remote (far away), apply drying medications that are moist in substance but dry in effect, such as a definitive ointment, for it contains a large part of vitriol, which is the final medication.
pren oignement dyafinit, et le font avec oile roset, et l’arose de viel vin igal en substance;	Take definitive ointment, make it with rosehip oil, and moisten it with old wine equal in volume;
puis le confit et en use;	Then boil it and use it.
et ceu meisme fait mielz cuit engroissiez, quant oignemens dyafinit n’est presens, ou tu pren mirre et aloen et encens, et le broie, et le poudre sus le miel quant il est sor le feu;	And this same thing is better boiled when there's no definite ointment present, or take myrrh and aloe and incense, grind it up, and sprinkle the powder on honey while it's still on the fire.
et puis en glue I drapel, et l’estent sor le sein, et aucune fois i aministre on aristologe longe, et racines de lis celeste, qui est ausi com farine de veces et centoire;	Then mix it with a linen cloth and spread it over the chest. Sometimes an aristoloche is used, or roots of celestial lily, which are like barley flour and chickling vetch.
et en use de simples ou de compostes:	Use it as either a simple medicine or in combination with other treatments.
broie les, et en fai poudre, et met sus le miel que j’ai dit, et en use;	Grind them up into powder and mix it onto the honey I mentioned before, then apply it.
et se li cure est alongie, et n’est curez par ceste cure, adonc saiches que la corruptions est em parfont, et fait empression en l’os, ou as membres durs, ou as liemens;	And if the cure is prolonged and not healed by this treatment, then know that corruption has reached the bone, or to hard tissues, or ligaments.
si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	If the treatment for curing fistula, as we have said before.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	Of an abscess under the nail
Panarice est un aposteme que naist desoz l’ungle dou pouchiet de la main, ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	A panaricium is an abscess that forms beneath the nail of the finger or toe, or it may appear in other places.
et quant il est envielliez, et on n’i prent garde, si i vient I aposteme chaus, et corront et giete bowe tant qu’elle corront la racine de l’ungle, et par aventure la corront toute;	And when it is neglected and left untreated, an abscess can form beneath the nail, leading to a deep pus-filled cavity that erodes and destroys the root of the nail, and sometimes even removes it entirely.
et vient li corrosions jusc’a l’os, tant qu’il i vient dolor puant, et est li chiés dou doi larges, et est li color fuxe.	It causes corrosion down to the bone, resulting in a foul-smelling pain and the affected area is wide and discolored.
Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu copes a i. fer toute la superfluiteit qui est demoree de l’ungle, puis cauterize la plaie aprés.	When you treat it as we have said in the previous section, and the treatment is not effective, then it is necessary to cut away all the remaining unhealthy tissue near the nail with an iron tool, then cauterize the wound afterwards.
Li cauteres est mout grans aide se li os est sains, et li ungle est sainne;	The cauterizations are a great help if the bone is healthy and the nail is sound;
et se li ungle apresse la char ens, et l’encomence a poindre, et la blece, si covient que tu mettes lou rait desoz l’ungle que point la char, et la boute en haut, et cope celi char subtilment et legierement, et met sus le remenant de la char medicines ardans et corrosives por oster tout;	And if the nail presses against the flesh, beginning to prick and wound it, you should place a needle beneath the nail that pierces the flesh, push it upwards, and cut away this flesh carefully and lightly, then apply burning and corrosive medicines onto the remaining flesh to remove all.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et se li corrosion est en l’os, si le cope, et trai fuer, car tant com li os corrumpus i est, si ne puet saner;	And if the corruption has reached the bone, cut it away, and pull hard, for as long as the corrupted part of the bone remains, healing cannot occur.
et se tu vois le doi corrumpre, si le cope en I des nous si com il est devant dit, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you see the finger is corrupted, cut it away from us as described before, then treat it until it is healed.
et s’il est ferus, et boutez, et il sent grant dolor, si covient que tu le sainnes premier;	and if he is wounded, and kicked, and feels great pain, then you must first treat his wounds.
puis cope l’ungle dou spatumile agut en taillant de travers desus, et warde que li taille ne viegne jusc’a la char qui est desoz l’ungle, car li malaides sentiroit trop grant dolor;	then cut the nail with the sharp spatula by slicing across it, and ensure that the cut does not go all the way through to the flesh beneath the nail, for the patient would feel too much pain.
et s’il avient, si met chose sus qui apaise.	and if it happens, place something soothing on it.
la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	The pain of the shoulder joint from the hand
Li dois ajostez qui naist en mains d’aucuns homes par aventure est toz charnus, et par aventure i a teil ou il a osses, et aucune fois i a ungle, et aucun d’aus naissent en la racine de la jointure, ou li naissance est en aucuns nous des dois.	The two adjusting thumbs that are born in some people's hands are sometimes very fleshy, and there is either skin or bones; at times they have nails, and one of them grows on the root of the joint, while the birth occurs in several of us.
Cil qui naist en aucune nout dou doi ne se muet, et cil qui naist a la jointure dou doi, par aventure se muet;	One who is born with a deformity of the finger will not move it, but one who is born at the knuckle of the finger may move it.
la taille de celui qui est charnus si est legiere, en teil maniere:	the incision for someone with fleshy fingers should be made in this way:
taille le en sa racine d’un large spatumile.	Cut it at its root with a wide spatule.
Cil qui naist en la racine de la jointure si est grief a curer:	He who is born in the root of the joint, so it is hard to cure.
si te tien dou coper.	So you must hold on firmly while cutting.
En celui qui naist ou doit au derrien nout, si covient que tu copes premier la char reondement jusc’a l’os, puis cope l’os a une soie convenable a ceu, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	In one who is born or must be delivered by the posterior route, you must first cut the round flesh down to the bone, then cut the bone to a suitable depth for it, and cure it until it heals.
Li soudemens que vient as dois ensamble vient par naissance, ou par soudement de plaie, ou par arsure de feu, ou par semblans choses.	The joining together of bones occurs either by birth, or by the healing of a wound, or by burning with fire, or by similar things.
Si couvient que tu copes celle soudeure, si que li doit repairent selonc lor formes naturelz;	It is necessary that you cut the sutures, so that they may heal according to their natural form;
puis met entre dous tentes ou drapelz moilliez en oile roset, qu’il ne se soudent;	Then place between two tents or moist cloths with rose oil, so that they do not adhere.
ou tu met entre dous pieces de plonc subtilz, tant que li leus soit soudez, si com il covient.	Or you place between two soft cloth pieces, until the flesh is sutured, as it should be done.
Se soudemens vient a aucun de ses dois avec la paume, si cope celle sodure si com il covient.	If a fusion occurs on someone's hand with the palm facing upwards, cut this fusion as it is required.
des vils	des villages
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	Veins are open wounds filled with melancholy humours that come to many body parts.
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	And more dislocations happen in legs of those who walk on foot and work hard, compared to others.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	So it is necessary for you to administer purging of the bile sometimes, then treat with the basil plant.
Li cure de fer si est selonc II manieres:	The treatment with iron is according to two methods:
l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	One method involves scraping [the wound] and drawing out the black blood;
et li autre maniere si est que tu lieves la voinne, et la trai toute fuer.	The other way is to raise the vein and draw all of its blood out.
Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere:	The incision should be done in this manner:
arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez, puis estrain la jambe dou malaide des desus la cuixe jusc’a la partie desoz le genoil;	First immerse the patient's leg in hot water that is very strong [in temperature], until the large vein becomes subtle, then pull the sick person's leg up from above the thigh to just below the knee.
puis cope la voinne en I leu, ou en II ou en III, d’une taille large, puis eslieve et trair fuer le sanc noir a ta main, des l’un chief jusc’a l’autre, tant que tant de sans en isse com li vertus dou malaide puet soffrir;	then cut the vein at I place or II or III with a wide incision and lift it up then pull out black blood by your hand from one end to another until there is enough bleeding as the patient can tolerate.
et puis la lie, et li comande qu’il se teigne de viandes enjanrant cole noire;	and then tie it up, and instruct them to abstain from food that generates black bile.
et recomence l’evacuation et la sainie quant les voinnes sont plainnes, et nuist au malaide.	and repeat the evacuation process and cauterization when veins refill with blood and harm the patient.
Li alevemens de li est selonc ceste maniere:	The remedies will be as follows in this manner:
reis la jambe dou malaide, s’il i a mout de poil, puis le met ou bain, et li arose la jambe d’aigue chaude tant qu’elle deviegne rouge, et enflent les voinnes;	place the patient's leg in warm water and shave any hair on it until veins become dilated and prominent.
et se tu n’as point de baing, si le chaufe au feu, et puis le cope endroit la voinne dou lonc au chief dou genoil, ou en la partie desoz a la cheville;	and if you have no bath, heat it over the fire, then place it on the wound from the top of the knee down to the foot or below the ankle.
puis aoevre le cuir a l’oncine, et escorche la voinne de chescune part, tant qu’ele apere quant on la sent;	then work the skin with an unciner, and peel away the wound from each side until it appears when touched.
et on la voit rouge et noire, et quant elle entre ou cuir si semble ausi com une corde blainche;	and you see it red and black, and when it enters the skin it looks like a white cord.
puis boute le rait desoz, tant qu’ele soit alevee dou cuir, et puis la pent a l’oncine legier, puis le cope en I autre leu ensus III dois;	then push the thread underneath so that it is raised from the skin and then smooth it with an unciner gently, then place another piece of cloth on top three fingers wide.
puis escorche le cuir sus la voinne tant qu’ele apere, puis la lieve au rais, si com tu as fait, et la pent a un autre uncine, si com tu as fait premiers;	then peel away the skin above the wound until it appears and then lift it with the thread as you have done before and smooth it with another unciner as you did initially.
puis cope une autre taille, ou plusors se tu en as mestier, puis la lieve, et la cope au doi dou piet, puis la trai et lieve jusc’a la seconde taille;	Then cut another slice, or several if you need to, then lift it up and cut it at the toe of the foot, then draw it out and lift until you reach the second slice.
puis l’estrai de taille en taille, tant qu’elle isse toute fuer, puis la cope;	Then extract it slice by slice until it comes out completely, then cut it.
et se tu ne la pues traire et lever, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil fort double, et la lie et la trai, et i boute desoz I rait, et torne ta main d’une part et d’autre, tant qu’il en isse;	And if you cannot draw it and lift it out, then put a needle in from one side with strong double thread, tie and pull, push the needle underneath, turn your hand to either side until it comes out.
et garde qu’elle ne cope, car s’elle cope, si ne la puet on traire ne lever, et en vient nuisement au malaide;	And make sure it does not cut, because if it cuts, you cannot draw it or lift it out, and this will harm the patient.
et quant tu l’as toute traite, si met sor le leu de la plaie laine moillie en vin et en oile roset;	And when you have drawn it all out, place moist wool soaked in wine and rose oil onto the wound. 
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat [the wound] until it is healed.
Et se li vis est contraite et torte et envoloupee ensamble, et ele n’est mie droite, si com nos avons dit, si covient que tu la fendes tortement, mais ne la coper mie;	And if the face is distorted, twisted and enveloped together, and it is not straight, as we have said, then you must cut it open in a crooked manner, but do not amputate.
et la trai si com nos avons devant dit.	and draw [the incision] as we mentioned before.
Li forme dou fer dont on cope la vis si est corbes, et ne trenche mie, qu’il ne cope la voinne;	The shape of the iron with which one cuts the face is curved, and does not slice, so that it incises the vein.
et est de grosse corbeure, car s’il estoit subtilz, si coperoit la voine, mais soit gros si com nos avons dit, et ci est li forme:	And it is of a thick curvature, because if it were delicate, it would slice the vein, but let it be thick as we have said, and this is its shape:
de la voinne civile	of the civil vein
Ceste voinne est enjanree en jambes, en chaudes parties ou il ne naist herbes ne arbre, et en terre ou il n’a point de moistor;	This vein is entangled in the legs, in warm parts of the body where no herb or tree grows, and on earth where there is no moisture.
et par aventure naist autre part qu’en jambes, et ceu avient de la porriture que vient desoz le cuir, si com il vient dedens le cors serpens et vers, enjanrez entre cuir et char.	And perhaps it appears elsewhere than in the legs, and this occurs due to the decay that originates beneath the skin, much like how snakes and worms develop within the body, embedded between skin and flesh.
Et se li signes de l’encomencement de ceste voinne si est qu’il vient en la jambe une tres grans enflammation, puis se chainge li leus, et comence li voinne fors issir, ausi com une racine d’une plante.	And if the sign of the beginning of this vein is that a great inflammation comes to the leg, then the color changes, and the vein starts to protrude, just like the root of a plant.
Quant li chiés apert, si covient que tu envoloupes entor une piece de plonc des une З et demi jusc’a II З., et la noe, et laisse le plonc pendant a la jambe, et totes les fois qu’il en ist point au defuer, si l’envoloupe entor le plonc, et la nowe;	When the wound opens, you must wrap it with a piece of wood that is 3 and a half to 2 inches long, tie it in place, and leave the wood hanging from the leg. Each time fluid exudes from beneath it, rewrap around the wood and retie it;
et s’elle est trop longe, si en cope une partie, et envoloupe le remenant, et ne la coper mie en sa racine, tant qu’elle soit toute issue;	If it is too long, cut off a portion of it, then rewrap the remainder and do not cut into its root so that all of it emerges.
