Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	And instruct the patient to sleep on their healthy side or their back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	And if hot abscesses form there, do not touch them until the hot abscesses have cooled, and put on what we have said before;
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	Then return to the restoration process, and restrain it as needed if there are no other complications;
et c’est li maniere.	And that is how it should be done.
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	Of shoulder dislocation.
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	The shoulder aids are what connect the arm to the shoulder blade, and if they are broken one should restore them according to either of the two methods.
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	One is that you take one piece of wood of medium thickness, in the following shape:
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	Et bind the two shoulders with two bindings, raise them upwards, and lay the patient on a seat.
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	Then cast the broken arm onto the trunk [tree stump], until it reaches the armpit, and place in its middle a curved piece of wood, then raise upon some heavy object that the assistants stretch downwards.
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	Then place the splint to break evenly with his hands together, so that the fracture returns as it should.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a II ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout I liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	The other method is to have the patient lie on their back and bind his hand to his neck; command two ministers to hold the broken ends together with one holding above the break while the other supports from below with straps. Then each must pull in opposite directions until both halves of the fracture are realigned correctly.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	And if you see that the extraction is more intense, then tightly bind the ligament below the fracture and above it, and stretch each of the ministers to their respective sides.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	And if the fracture is close to the head of the shoulder, you must place one binding below the armpit and another towards the side [axilla], below the break.
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	And also if the break is towards the side [axilla], you must place one binding lightly without force so that the fracture aligns both on its spot and on the side.
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	Then align the fracture evenly, as it ought to be, and hold it steady, unless warm abscesses form there.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	And if warm abscesses do form there, do not hold it tight for seven days, and apply moist woolen cloth soaked in rose oil until the warm abscesses subside;
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	Then hold it firmly again, and the way to do so is to apply a plaster cast over the fracture, then position the arm on the shoulder or chest, and place your hand on the patient's shoulder or breast;
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	And apply the bandage, holding it over the shoulder and arm, so that the arm remains in its proper position, unless something prevents this or if the bone is displaced.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	And if you doubt that the bone will move, use splints, and place a larger and stronger splint over the break, with two fingers' width between each splint, and let each splint be large enough to extend three fingers' breadth beyond the fracture on either side.
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	Then draw up on the splints as I said at the beginning of this chapter regarding fractures, with greater force and less separation.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if you see the position of the splints and the tightness as we have said when restoring the broken limb, and doubt about an abscess getting hot, leave it bound until the seventh day, as we have instructed.
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	Then check every three days the binding to ensure that itching or swelling does not occur at the site, nor any numbness in the limb due to it being too tight.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	If the address, as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	And if no such accidents occur, do not release him from his bonds until three days or more have passed, and let the patient sleep on their back with their hands resting on their stomach.
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	place a pillow stuffed with wool underneath the injured area, and check every hour during the day or night to ensure that the broken limb does not move or loosen its bindings.
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	if it heals by the power of medicine, give them the food we mentioned earlier, making sure that the meat is of the highest quality.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	and when they start to regain strength, let their meals be hearty.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	It is customary for the splint and leg to be rewrapped every forty days of treatment.
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	And then you must loosen it and administer baths and ointment medicines to realign its place.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the dislocation is severe and stuck, it may take one day or two months to heal.
de la brisure du bras	Of the fracture of the arm:
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm is composed of two bones, which are called the "foscile," one of which is small and follows the wrist.
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	and the other is large, located below towards the little finger.
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	Should only one of these bones break or both together by chance.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	When the smaller bone is broken, its restoration and healing process is relatively easier.
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	And when the larger bone is broken, its healing is poor, more grievous than if both were broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If it is the small knuckle bone that is broken, you should gently stretch it slightly and make sure it is aligned.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	And if it is a large wound, you must compress it more firmly;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	lay him on a pillow, and hold the wrist of his hand higher than the others, and keep the little fingers lower than the other fingers, and have the patient cross their legs over themselves, and place the pillow in front of them, higher than the patient's body, so that he does not suffer any strain;
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	then have your assistants stretch out their arms under the part of his body below his hand or wrist, and have other assistants on the other side above him.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	Then place the mirror flat, according to its best shape.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if it is broken into pieces, you should put each piece back in its place and hold the heart-shaped one firmly; if you cannot restore it to its place, cut it out as we have said before.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if with the breaking of skin I have spoken about it in the singular chapter;
si pren la cure.	then take care [of it].
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if at the beginning of recovery warm abscesses appear, use a compress made of cerate composed of rose oil and white wax, which should be neither too hard nor too soft;
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and cover the compress gently above until the warm abscesses are soothed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	Then remove the cerate, and apply a plaster made of the mill powder with plenty of egg white, then place the splints, with the splint for the fracture being adjacent and slightly wider than the others;
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	and note that there must be six splints on an arm in various arrangements:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	whether the fracture is located in one of the bones or in two;
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	And hold it tighter above the fracture than elsewhere, and every day less in removing it, as I said at the beginning of this chapter.
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	Let the bandages that are on the fracture be soft and moist, and not hard or rough.
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	And the thread of which it is held should be linen, neither too thick nor too fine, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	And rest the limb and its connection for some days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	And if any bad accident happens to the limb, such as itching which occurs in the limb, you must rinse the limb with warm water until this itching is soothed.
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	And let the member rest without constriction.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	Then begin the compression again, and if the ligaments are softened and the bones are separated or similarly misaligned, then realign them.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses I poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if you note that blood cannot reach the limb because it is too tight, then you must soften it a little and leave it like this for some days until circulation returns, then apply compression again.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	And if none of these things we have said come to pass with the patient, do not release him until twenty days have passed.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	He should be wrapped in a bandage around the neck, and then you can tie his hands behind it. His collars must remain even, and he is to be guarded against any movements or twists while sleeping on his back.
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	Et know that this fracture heals in XXX days or XXXV, and perhaps even in XX days, depending on the combinations and constitutions of virtues.
de la brisure de la main	On la breche de la main, tu la frotteras tant qu'elle soit chaude et moult roide; car souvent est elle si roide que tu ne puisses la froter a nul chastez; adonques la laisseras desiester par le temp, et tu l'oigneras comme nous avons dit. Et tu la frotteras XX jors ou XXX jors ou XL jors selonc qu'elle soit plus roide ou moins roide, jusqu'a ce que le os se joignent a son chastez; et si elle est de telle nature que les osses ne puissent estre a leur chastez par frottement ni par oignement, adonques covient il que tu les remettes en leur place.
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	Know that on the back of the hand and the knuckles there are few fractures, but more often sprains occur.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	And when the palm of the hand is fractured or bent, the patient should have their arms crossed and sit upright in front of them evenly.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	Then place their hand on the extended cloth, and let the assistants extend the broken bones, aligning them with the mirror until they are properly joined.
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	And apply the plaster and bandages, unless an abscess forms, then insert a small stick according to the size of the place.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	And wrap it in one linen cloth.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the fracture is around the front of the foot near the sole, make a pad of linen cloths and instruct the patient to bind it tightly to their broken foot.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	Bind it with a long strip of cloth and provide a soft heart-shaped cushion as big as the sole of their hand; hold it tight as is required.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the fracture is on the outside, you must place a splint above it and another below, in the palm, so that the hand remains open and straight, then bind it all around with bandages, tightening them between the fingers.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	If the fracture affects one of our fingers or thumbs, make it even as is required.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	Bind it with the foot and if you wish to place a small straight splint to raise the fracture and prevent movement, do so.
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	If the fracture affects any other fingers such as the index finger or one of the others, make it even and bind it with the healthy finger next to it.
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	or you bind them all together with a bandage, holding it in place so that it may move better, or you put on a splint as for a fracture.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	and take care during the restoration and arrangement of a hot abscess, and help those who come to you with it, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	Of a broken thigh.
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The thigh bone is often broken, and you can see this clearly when the leg turns forward or backward.
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	and its restoration is such that you bind the ligament above the fracture, and another below it.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And the patient lies on their face, then each attendant stretches their bandage to its limit equally;
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	and that is when the fracture is in the middle of the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the break is close to the root of the thigh, then one bandage should be towards the wrist, and the other bandages below the break.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And also if it is near the knee, then let the binding be beside the knee, and let the extension be downwards.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	Then place the mirrors so that the bone is aligned with both hands, ensuring it is according to its natural shape, and then apply the plaster and bind it, if no abscesses arise.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	And if there is a hot abscess present, let it cool down before returning to your work and treatment.
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	The binding is done in the following way.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	You must wrap the fracture with one thick or two to three thin bandages, leaving some extra length, then turn the leg so that the heel reaches the base of the thigh, and pass a long thread between the thigh and the leg below the knee, bringing the end of the thread over it.
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then return to the leg and thigh with the bandage, then place splints on the fracture, and put a splint over the bone of the leg.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then fill the empty space between the leg and thigh with soft cloth to evenly tighten it, then start binding firmly in figure-of-eight turns three or four times over the splint.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	And as you go upwards beyond the fracture, tighten it less.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	Then take the two ends of the thread you passed between the leg and thigh, and bind three splints that are above it, then return to the bottom on the underside along the length of the foot.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	And tighten it so that it cannot move from its place, then leave it like this, and ensure no abscess or swelling develops there nor any other similar thing.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if it happens, then release it, and address what is coming, as we have said many times;
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	and if there are fragments of bone caught in it, then one must remove them if possible;
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	and if that cannot be done, then one must split the site open, and pull with force;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And sometimes the thigh is broken in such a way that pins are inserted, as in the shoulder and arm;
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	however, in this kind of restoration, the patient is not harmed.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en L jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And understand that the thigh is restored in L days, or perhaps a little less or more, according to the variations of constitutions [i.e., different patients].
de la ruelle dou genoil	Of the groove of the knee
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	Know that in the alley of the knee there is little breakage, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, it is only a crack or a hole, and this occurs with all wounds, whether felt as pain or not, and one feels well.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is such that one straightens what is bent to its proper place, as much as it can be assembled and moved.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	Then apply the plaster, and insert a round stent if necessary, holding it in place as required, then follow all the arrangements we mentioned for other fractures, such as hot abscesses and similar conditions.
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Apply to each condition what is appropriate for its healing.
de la brisure de la jambe	On the fracture of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	Know that in the leg there are two bones, of which one is rightly called "muscle", and the other is called "tibia".
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	All other fractures of the leg happen just as they do in the arm, and for this, the restoration is equal to that of the arm, and the work involved is all the same. And if both bones are broken together, the leg becomes twisted on all sides.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the subtle bone is broken, it turns forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the large bone is broken, one feels great pain, and it is clearly visible.
et torne desoz.	and comes underneath.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Then provide an extension, make it level, and bind the rods equally.
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	However, if the break is severe and there are multiple fragments, the extension should be shorter and lighter.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	lighten it according to your skill.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have completed your work, take two strips of wood that are as long as the leg from knee to ankle and bind them to either side.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap in two places with one bandage above and below, binding it tightly in the middle as well, so that at this time the leg cannot bend to the right or left, and thus it is sound.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And some administer two splints along the length of the leg, whether of wood or another material, and they put the leg in it to prevent movement, making this properly at the site of fracture or wound.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	And move the leg each day to check for abscess or other mishap.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Cure it until it is healed.
de la brisure des os dou piet	Of broken bones in the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle there is no break, but in the bones of the foot a break can occur and at the toes sometimes only cracking takes place in various situations.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if there is a break in the bones of the foot and you see these bones protruding from one another, then have the patient place their foot on the ground as though they were about to walk, and now put your foot on theirs where the bones are raised, then press until they return to their places.
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	Then apply the plaster and some padding on top, place beneath the patient's foot a small board with two feet in length, then gently restrain their foot, once you have wrapped it in bandages, along with any other necessary materials.
Et quant III jors ou IIII seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, untie the bandage, for you will find the bones equalized, whether they are broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if there be any broken bones therein, restore them in the same way we have said for fingers of the hand.
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place a splint on the broken toe according to its length and slightly wider, then put under the foot that small board I mentioned earlier, and restrain it gently.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there be two or three, or more, broken toes, then place a splint on each toe according to its size, wrapped in a linen cloth, and restrain the board beneath the foot.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And so keep them resting on top of the head of the table, removing their belly from the foot, so that they hold it well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And make sure you do not forget the other things I have said to the other bone setters, since we spoke of them earlier;
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	and treat each accident as it is required.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	Of the broken bone of the wrist
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the woman's bone is broken by nature, make her sit spread out and then lean her towards her back part, to be held from behind;
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the woman's broken area with cotton to the level of her natural shape;
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then help the woman stand up with her back lifted gently and slowly until the cotton comes out at the entrance of her body, allowing the bones to realign themselves;
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	When she wishes to urinate, remove the cotton, and when she is done, put it back in. Do this for seven days or so.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	If the fracture will be restored, and if you wish to see this, take a sheep's bladder, attach a tube to the opening, and insert the entire bladder into the wound.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow strongly through the tube so that the bladder is fully inflated inside.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	The wound will be restored as the fracture returns to its natural place.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It should then be filled with cotton and left like this for several days until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the wrist bone of a man or woman is broken, restore it as we have said for the hip bone.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	And these dislocations are not hidden from him who applies his study and practice to them, and reads my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the fracture indicates in many ways the correct path for restoration:
enten le donques.	Understand it then.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the penis, when it is broken, take a goose's gullet and insert the penis inside it;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	Then wrap it in fine linen, and leave for three days, and it will be healed quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	For break with wound:
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	He who has a break with wound, especially if it is large like the bone of the thigh or shoulder, must be treated now as we have described for treatment of wounds.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound heals, treat it with vitriol poultice, if you have nothing else, then repeat the treatment to restore the fracture that same hour or day, unless hot abscesses arise.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	If hot abscesses appear, leave the treatment until the ninth day, until the abscess has calmed down, and do not touch it on the third or fourth day, for you would cause a bad outcome.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	If the broken bone is apparent on an exposed heart, you must set it gently with your hands in a small extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extension does not seem sufficient to align with your hands, use this instrument of iron, which is seven or eight fingers long and its width depends on the size of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and for this it is necessary for the surgeon to use three or four of these, according to what he needs in each treatment for fractures.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and let them be round and slightly thicker so that they do not bend when compressed against the limb during your treatment, and pointed at one end, thickening towards the middle like this;
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called a "splint", which means the curved piece must be placed over the head of the visible bone;
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	and strike it once until it returns to its place, and let them be even with each other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the fracture is subtle and the instrument cannot properly grasp the bone, then you must cut off the head of the bone until the instrument has enough power to do so.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reset the bone as we have said, then use a suitable instrument for this purpose, either a chisel or a knife according to your ability.
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	Then remove what remains in the bone of roughness and small bark.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is reset, and the patient feels great pain afterward, know that it is not yet in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	Do this until it is in its place, then soak the cloth with black astringent wine, and properly so if it was on bone.
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	And do not put any ointment or other greasy substance on the wound for it may cause inflammation and decay.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	Then apply stitches once you have restored the bone, and leave the wound uncovered, wrapping the covering all around according to the size of the wound, taking great care that the wound is not bound tightly with the fracture.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	And many times these foolish surgeons have done this, causing death or corrosion to the patient at times.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	And the ligatures are softer and gentler than other fractures.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is severe or large, and you fear bad complications may arise, as we have said, and find pain at the site, it should not be treated with stars.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	But wrap around, instead of using stars, use hard rags, and bind them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after one or two days that the wound is inflamed, remove what you have applied to it entirely, and put on a healing ointment such as tetrafarmacon and similar ones.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre II fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	You must loosen the limb twice a day, in the morning and at night, until it is fused and healed.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is necessary that the limb be bandaged in such a way that the bowstring runs downward slightly.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if after many days it does not heal but becomes inflamed again, know that there are small pieces of bone present, which is why you must probe the wound with a needle and remove all these loose pieces that cause such pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula develops at the site or any other form of corruption occurs, you must treat it according to what he says in his chapter beforehand.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken and protruding from the limb, such as in the thigh or shoulder bones, and other similar large limbs, do not extract it, for many die due to this procedure, but leave it until it rots.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	Perhaps after twenty or thirty days it will fall off by itself, then treat the wound if you are able to do so.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	And if you cannot, then leave it be.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	Scabs that form over the healing.
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	We often come across the healing of fractures, especially when they are close to the joints, and it is an ugly sight to see the shape of the affected limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	And at times, the limb may not be able to perform its natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Take heed if it is fresh for us:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	If the physician administers styptic medicines such as aloe, incense, and myrrh, or substances like sarcocolla, aloeswood, and others of a similar nature, so that you take any of these things, or all together, then prepare them with a styptic wine, or with egg white, or with isinglass.
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and place them on the night over cotton wool, and hold it tight, and do not untie for two days.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	then untie it, and start again with another one until the knots are removed;
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or you may hold it tight on a well-made wooden block;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	for the property of wood is such that it removes all swelling from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the knot has already turned hard like stone and must be removed, then cut it out, and split open the excess;
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you may take it to a barber so that he removes it, and treat the wound until it is clean.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	Of the member which is weak after treatment
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the bone fracture is healed, and afterward the limb remains weak and delicate, it happens for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	because one reason is that it was bound too tightly, and not tied as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many bindings, and nourishment could not reach the limb;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or due to excessive drainage;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or from too much movement, not at the right time;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because there is little blood in their body, thus they are weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment is to have the patient eat, and make the body soft, so that blood multiplies within them;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and administer well, and give joy and permission;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then apply pitch on the limb, so that the pitch draws out the great discharge, and moisten it often with warm water until the discharge reaches the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and restore it to its natural form.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	A joint twisted after the injury.
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the bone appears broken, and the form of the limb is ugly, nevertheless it does not lose its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	do not believe the fools who say one must break the limb anew, and many foolish doctors have done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and these practices are to be blamed, as they lead to great harm, and even death;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	However, if the nodules and pain are fresh, they must be soaked in warm water, or softening herbs should be cooked, such as leaves of mallow, roots, honeysuckle, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	And make a softening plaster, such as well-made diachylon, and take the mucilage of mallow, mixing it with goose grease or sesame oil, and apply this ointment.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	Alternatively, you can take fatty figs, grind them with coltsfoot meal, and similar medicines that soften the swelling.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And sometimes the swelling is removed by continually and thoroughly rubbing with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	Make gentle movements to the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	If the tendon is old and hardened like stone, and must be removed with an iron tool, then it should be cut right up to the bone using a delicate and light incision instrument.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and apply a compress; focus diligently on treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation occurs to anyone, you must now reset it without delay.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if one delays, the joint swells, and it may be reset painfully in place.
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	since one should not move it while swollen;
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	often causing spasms and other pains.
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	however, when it happens, have the patient bleed, then leave them be until the abscess is quietened.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	immerse the limb in warm water and oil, then gently reset it; treat each member as it returns to its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters on dislocations of the head down to foot.
des mandibules	Of the jaws.
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	where they are slightly out of place, and somewhat softened;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	where they are completely dislocated, and hanging towards the worse, and saliva falls from his mouth which he cannot hold in, nor can close his mouth, and it affects his speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it returns through various positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is complete and fully dislocated, you must reset it promptly, without delay;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a manner that the assistant holds the patient's head, and presses their thumb from one of their hands into the root of the jaw dislocation inside the mouth, if the dislocation is on two sides;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and let the other two fingers of their hands be outside to keep it level;
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	And instruct the patient to soften their jaws, and move them from all sides.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	The mirror is placed evenly until it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if it is severely dislocated, especially if both jaws are involved, bathe them in warm water and oil until they can be gently reset.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Do not delay the resetting process as we have mentioned before.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	Once the jaws are realigned evenly and the patient's mouth feels well-lubricated, apply damp cloth dressings infused with a mixture of rose oil and wax, then lightly bind them with soft bandages.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	Let the patient sleep on their back with their jaws resting between two cushions to prevent any movement to the right or left, and refrain from exerting themselves by chewing. Instead, consume light meals until the pain subsides and the jaws are fully healed.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then let him eat what he wants lightly, and do not exert himself to open his mouth for eating or drinking, until the mandible is well-nurtured and healed.
Et se les II mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two jaws cannot be reset at once and fail to return to their original position, then fevers and sweating may follow, possibly accompanied by a loosening of the bowels or even vomiting up clear fluid.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see that, know that it is fatal.
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many times the one it befalls dies within nine days.
de la forcelle	Of the fork.
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The fork cannot be reset from the sides within its limits; sometimes it is dislocated externally and this can be easily felt.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the restoration is such that the patient often lies on their back and stretches out their arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the place firmly with your palm, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then apply the plaster and bind it up, and hold it firmly.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the head which faces towards the cut cannot dislocate;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it dislocates at all, then reset it to its place, as we have said;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	then apply the poultice and bandage it tightly, holding it firmly in place, and instruct the patient to rest until healed;
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	and thus also reset the head of the shoulder when it is dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Of shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Know that the shoulder is dislocated only in three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	one is when it dislocates to the lower part behind;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second one is at the part of the shoulder;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and sometimes dislocates in the upper part, which happens often;
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and it does not dislocate behind the shoulder, nor inside towards the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and often dislocates downwards towards the armpit, especially in those with little flesh, as it falls easily without support;
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	in those who have enough flesh, it falls slightly, and returns slightly.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And perhaps it happens to some men by blow or fall, and the shoulder swells from a hot abscess, and one thinks that it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	You must therefore test it until you are certain;
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And dislocation is recognized when it falls toward the axilla, creating a noticeable distinction between the affected shoulder and the healthy one; you will observe an evident disparity between them.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	And you will find at the head of the shoulder a hollow, and beneath the axilla up to the acromion process of the scapula, resembling an egg.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	And the patient cannot bring their hand to their nose nor move any of its joints.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	And if it is dislocated upwards, it is not hidden, for you will find it clearly at the acromion process.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	And this type of dislocation is not difficult to reset when it is new or if the patient is an infant.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the method is that the assistants lift the patient's hand upwards, then place your palms underneath the armpit, and raise the joint forcefully to its correct position;
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	and the assistants lift the hand, extend it upwards, then place it underneath;
si venra hastanment.	there will be dislocation.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not work as we have said with hands outside afterwards, then the patient must be bathed in warm water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the assistants apply softening and soothing ointments, such as a decoction of althea, fenugreek, and melilot in water, to be administered;
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	then the patient should be reminded on their back, and a pad of equal woollen cloth, neither too soft nor too hard, is placed underneath the armpit. The heel of the patient's other foot is placed onto this pad, then they lift up the affected shoulder with care. They draw their hand;
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and another assistant holds the patient's head so it does not move downwards;
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	that shoulder returns immediately now, and if you see that it dislocates again according to this method:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and have a stronger man present than the patient;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and stand upright facing the patient's side, and push their shoulder beneath the armpit of the patient, and lift the armpit upwards so that the patient hangs in the air;
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	and another assistant pulls the patient's hand downwards towards their stomach.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too light, weigh them down with something heavy, and the dislocation will return now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it is also reset in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	And one should insert a long peg into the ground, so that the shoulder is as round as an apple seed, and it should not be too thick nor too thin.
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	Then one should be placed beneath the patient, but ensure they have soft blankets on top, and the patient should lie along the length of the peg.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	Afterward, extend their arm from the other side in this way, and the joint will return to its place gently.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	And if it does not want to come back due to all the aforementioned things, then do this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	Take a peg of two arms' length and four fingers in width, which has an end rounded for insertion perfectly beneath the shoulder joint, according to this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	Then place over his head a soft cloth cushion, so that the wood does not hurt the patient, then put it under the patient's armpit;
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and extend his arm over the long side of the wood, and tie the shoulder to the wood, and the arm to the head of the patient, then place the arm on a stool with a wide base, and let the hands be extended downwards, and let the body hang loose on the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	the joint returns now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is in place, no matter how it was done, you must put under the arm a wad of equal wool then apply the plaster prepared with flour powder, incense and egg white over all shoulder and around, then tighten the strap under the arm accordingly, return the binding on top of the plaster, embrace the hand to his neck, and leave hands in that position.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And make sure he moves little, so that the limb is comfortable, for it will heal sooner;
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then move more after five or seven days, and change his position;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	If it is closed and not softened, then it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint has moved out of place due to moisture or for any other reason, you must apply cauterization to three openings, as described before in the chapter on cauterization.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all that and it still dislocates after seven days, and the joint does not hold, and they cannot lift their arm above their head, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is either cut or stretched or weakened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and know that the joint will never be fixed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation towards the armpit, breasts, or behind is caused by a push and stretching of hands, and another place must be treated.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after the healing process, there is cracking in the limb, and delayed movement, let the patient bathe frequently until this cracking eases, and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	Of shoulder dislocation:
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the jaw joint is often dislocated and returns with difficulty;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And if it is dislocated on all sides, especially in front and behind, and the dislocation has not been reduced, for it can be seen and felt clearly;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	and dislocated according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick person's wound with the healthy one, you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	Because the joint is dislocated, and cannot bend the arm or reach their shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And it is necessary that you reset it, even if abscesses appear afterward, because if abscesses were to develop, it would be difficult to reduce.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and perhaps it cannot be reduced completely in all directions, especially when it is at the back.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	it is worse than other dislocations, and causes even greater pain; moreover, death may occur as a result.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the restoration is such that when it is possible to reduce it, you should extend your hand with both hands to them;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And let his arms be spread out, and the hands of the mirror according to the cut around, above, and below, and push the joint towards their armpits together, or at the root of their palms, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is at the front, it returns when he bends his hand towards his hand, and press against the root of the palm the bone which has come out of joint.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to return to its place, administer strong traction.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and let two people administer the extension of the arm, and the other two hold it, so that it does not move in the traction.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm on both sides, after you have wrapped it with a long and wide piece of doubled cloth.
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the mirror has joined the joint to the hand, anoint it with some oil to soften the joint, then push the joint firmly until it returns.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, apply dry poultice with raw egg white on top, strap it tightly and tie the arm to the neck of the patient for a few days, then remove the binding.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	and if the joint is firmly in place, untie the bandage, and leave it be.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	and if you see that the joint is not held firmly, reapply the poultice and bandage, and leave it there for a few days until it is securely in place.
puis le deslie.	then untie the binding.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if he feels soreness after resetting the joint and it moves again, bathe him and massage gently, pressing until the pain is soothed.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Tu places sur la jointure un emplâtre de graisse de mouton, puis le laisse pendant un jour et une nuit, ensuite tu l'enlèves, et il doit aller dans le bain ;
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	Et quand il sue, s'il frotte la jointure doucement, ensuite remet l'emplâtre dessus, et retourne dans le bain ;
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Et ainsi fais cela deux ou trois fois, jusqu'à ce qu'il soit guéri ;
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	Et s'il y a une plaie, applique du foin de vache humide chauffé au beurre, ensuite recouvre ;
si revenra a sa disposition.	Cela reviendra à sa position d'origine.
li dislocation de la main	The dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	La jointure de la main disloquée, et son retour en place est léger, plus facile que pour les autres articulations.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it must be repositioned immediately to its place of origin, in the same hour that it is dislocated, unless the area becomes swollen or an abscess forms there, which causes heat.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the process of repositioning is as follows: place the patient's hand on a table and have your assistants stretch out their arm, aligning it with the patient's; then match the appearance of the dislocated joint to the palm of their hand and push until it returns into place.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, you must ensure that it is properly aligned.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then have the patient place the back of their hand on a table for extension and repositioning.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is on the back of the hand, make the patient lay the back of their hand on the table and have the assistants place their hand above that joint's position.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns to its position now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If this is not the case, if the extract of healing plasters soothes hot abscesses, and you leave it thus without restarting.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot endure it, and you cannot put it back in place after some days, the joint remains deformed.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and it neither harms nor hurts the patient to keep the hand soft as long as possible, and he is unable to grip anything at all.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	then know that the nerve or artery has been severed.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is any other method to treat it except by the application of a caustic near the wound, and perhaps nothing else will be beneficial.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse V jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is in place, apply the poultice we mentioned, then restrain it and leave it for five days, then release it and leave it like that.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he cannot move it properly, and there is any tearing, then bathe it with warm water, and rub it until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	Of the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	At times the finger of the hand is dislocated towards each side, at times on the back of the palm or on the belly.
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	Then stretch out the finger, and push on the dislocation with your thumb until it returns, then support the head of the finger, bending it towards the part where it is disjoined.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	Leave it for two days, then straighten it that day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	And bind it at night as we have said, unbind it during the day, make it move, and re-bind it at night.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Do this frequently until it becomes narrow. Do the same if dislocated at the palm of the hand, act in the way you have done before, until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	And do likewise when dislocated elsewhere.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	Of dislocation of the spine from the back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the spine from the back or neck is dislocated, or there are multiple dislocations, there is no cure, for death hurries the patient.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	The signs are that involuntary excretion occurs without his will, he cannot control it, and often one or more limbs become weakened, whether the two thighs, both arms, or one of them.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the spine bends into four parts.
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	Those who bend backwards are called "hunchbacks.
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The treatment is to turn back if the hunchback developed in childhood:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	There is no cure or healing for it at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And for those who develop it from falling or blows or similar things, the ancient ways of treatment with big words have little real benefit according to them.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	But I have shortened it according to my intention, and I have crafted instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that with regard to the humpback disease which presents in front, no one knows its cause nor cure;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also the one that develops directly in two sides, and it cannot be cured except for that which specifically presents at the back, as I say.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And it is that the patient must be stretched out on their face in an equal place, and have a restraint underneath them so they do not injure themselves.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then fix one iron rod firmly into the ground at their head and another at their feet, and tie a cord across the shoulder blades of the patient, and another to their hips, knees, and ankles.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	and two assistants will hold the bindings, one at the head and another at the feet, between the two fire irons.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and they should be well secured, the fire iron as we have said, and the patient's palms placed on their spine so that it straightens.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not straighten with this treatment, take a board three feet long and insert its head under the wall, then have the patient lie on their side, push the board's end under the wall, placing the middle of the board onto the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and have the patient place their feet on the other end of the board, pressing hard until it returns to its original position.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	And if you see this, have him turn his hand around.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And insert two red-hot iron rods into the head of the patient's affected arm, and place two more near their feet, with each rod a palm's length apart vertically.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	And ensure there is one hole in each iron rod for the turner's hand to fit through, and make sure these rods are firmly embedded into the ground so they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	And between the two larger iron rods place a turning rod, which causes the ties to turn, and have two smaller turning rods, each one palm length long, to rotate this handle.
